janamejaya uvāca
prādurbhāvaḥ purāṇeṣu viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ
satāṃ kathayatāṃ vipra vārāha iti naḥ śrutaḥ
na jāne tv asya caritaṃ nikhilaṃ ca savistaram
na dharmaguṇasaṃsthānaṃ na hetuṃ na manīṣitam
kimātmako varāho 'sau kiṃvīryaḥ kāsya devatā
kimācāraḥ kiṃprabhāvaḥ kiṃ vā tena purā kṛtam
etan me śaṃsa tattvena vārāhaṃ śrutivistaram
yajñārthaṃ ca sametānāṃ dvijātīnāṃ mahātmanām
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
hanta te kathayiṣyāmi purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam
samāhitamanā bhūtvā śṛṇu rājan yathātatham
mahāvarāhacaritaṃ kṛṣṇasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ
yathā nārāyaṇo devo vārāhaṃ vapur āsthitaḥ
daṃṣṭrayā gāṃ samudrasthām ujjahārārisūdanaḥ
chāndasībhir udārābhiḥ śrutibhiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ
śuciḥ prayatnavān bhūtvā nibodha janamejaya
idaṃ purāṇaṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiś ca saṃmitam
nānāśrutisamāyuktaṃ nāstikāya na kīrtayet
purāṇam etad akhilaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ yogaṃ ca veda yaḥ
kārtsnyena vidhinā proktaṃ so 'syārthaṃ vedayiṣyati
viśvedevās tathā sādhyā rudrādityās tathāśvinau
prajānāṃ patayaś caiva sapta caiva maharṣayaḥ
manaḥsaṃkalpajāś caiva pūrvajāś ca maharṣayaḥ
vasavo 'psarasaś caiva gandharvā yakṣarākṣasāḥ
daityāḥ piśācā nāgāś ca bhūtāni vividhāni ca
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā mlecchādayo bhuvi
catuṣpadāni sattvāni tiryagyonigatāni ca
jaṅgamāni ca sattvāni yac cānyajjīvasaṃjñitam
pūrṇe yugasahasrānte brāhme 'hani tathāgate
nirvāṇe sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvotpātasamudbhave
hiraṇyaretās triśikhas tato bhūtvā vṛṣākapiḥ
śikhābhir vidhamaṃl lokān saṃśoṣayati dehinaḥ
dadyamānās tatas tasya tejorāśibhir agrataḥ
vivirṇavarṇā dagdhāṅgā hatārciṣmadbhir ānanaiḥ
sāṅgopaniṣadā vedā itihāsapurogamāḥ
sarvavidyākriyāś caiva satyadharmaparāyaṇāḥ
brahmāṇam agrataḥ kṛtvā prabhavaṃ viśvatomukham
pūrvadevagaṇāś caiva trayastriṃśac ca chandajāḥ
tasminn ahani saṃprāpte taṃ haṃsaṃ mahadakṣaram
praviśanti mahāyogaṃ hariṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum
teṣāṃ bhūyaḥ praviṣṭānāṃ nidhanotpattir ucyate
yathā sūryasya satatam udayāstamayāv iha
pūrṇe yugasahasrānte kalpo niḥśeṣa ucyate
tasmiñ jīvakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ niḥśeṣam avatiṣṭhate
saṃhṛtya lokān sarvān sa sadevāsurapannagān
kṛtvātmagarbhaṃ bhagavān āsta eko jagadguruḥ
yaḥ sraṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ kalpānteṣu punaḥ punaḥ
avyaktaḥ śāśvato devas tasya sarvam idaṃ jagat
naṣṭārkakiraṇe loke candraraśmivivarjite
tyaktadhūmāgnipavane kṣīṇayajñatapaḥkriye
apakṣigaṇasaṃpāte sarvaprāṇyacare pathi
amaryādākule raudre sarvatas tamasā vṛte
adṛśye sarvaloke 'sminn abhāve sarvakarmaṇām
praśānte sarvasaṃpāte naṣṭe vairaparigrahe
gate svabhāvasaṃsthāne loke nārāyaṇātmake
parameṣṭhī hṛṣīkeśaḥ śayanāyopacakrame
pītavāsā lohitākṣaḥ kṛṣṇo jīmūtasaṃnibhaḥ
śikhāsahasravikacaṃ jaṭābhāraṃ samudvahan
śrīvatsakalilaṃ puṇyaṃ raktacandanarūṣitam
vakṣo bibhran mahābāhuḥ savidyud iva toyadaḥ
puṇḍarīkasahasrasya mālāsya śuśubhe tadā
patnī cāsya svayaṃ lakṣmīr deham āśritya tiṣṭhati
tataḥ svapiti dharmātmā sarvalokapitāmahaḥ
kim apy amitavikrānto yoganidrām upāgataḥ
tato yugasahasre tu pūrṇe sa puruṣottamaḥ
svayam eva vibhur bhūtvā budhyate vibudhādhipaḥ
tataś cintayate bhūyaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ lokasya lokakṛt
pitṛdevāsuranarān pārameṣṭhyena karmaṇā
tataś cintayate kāryaṃ deveṣu samitiṃjayaḥ
saṃbhavaṃ sarvalokasya vidadhāti sa vākpatiḥ
kartā caiva vikartā ca saṃhartā ca prajāpatiḥ
dhātā vidhātā prabhavaḥ saṃyamo niyamo yamaḥ
nārāyaṇaparā devā nārāyaṇaparāḥ kriyāḥ
nārāyaṇaparā yajñā nārāyaṇaparā śrutiḥ
nārāyaṇaparo mokṣo nārāyaṇaparā gatiḥ
nārāyaṇaparaṃ satyaṃ nārāyaṇaparaṃ padam
sa svayaṃbhūr iti jñeyaḥ sa brahmā bhuvanādhipaḥ
sa vāyur iti vijñeya eṣa yajñaḥ prajāpatiḥ
sadasac ca sa vijñeyaḥ sa yajñaḥ sa prajākaraḥ
yad veditavyaṃ tridaśais tad eṣa parivindati
yac ca vedyaṃ bhagavato devā api na tad viduḥ
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sapta ṛṣayaś ca sahāmaraiḥ
nāsyāntam adhigacchanti tenānanta iti śrutiḥ
yad asya paramaṃ rūpaṃ tan na paśyanti devatāḥ
prādurbhāveṣu saṃbhūtaṃ yat tad arcanti devatāḥ
darśitaṃ yad anenaiva tad avekṣanti devatāḥ
yan na darśitavān devaḥ kas tad anveṣṭum arhati
grāmaṇīḥ sarvabhūtānām agnimārutayor gatiḥ
tejasas tapasaś caiva nidhānam amṛtasya ca
caturāśramadharmeṣu cāturhotraphalāśanaḥ
catuḥsāgaraparyantacaturyugavivartakaḥ
tad eṣa saṃhṛtya jagat kṛtvā garbhastham ātmanaḥ
mimocāṇḍaṃ mahāyogī dhṛtaṃ varṣasahasrikam
surāsuradvijabhujagāpsarogaṇair
mahauṣadhikṣitidharayakṣaguhyakaiḥ
prajāpatiḥ śrutidhararakṣasāṃ kulaṃ
tadāsṛjaj jagad idam ātmanā prabhuḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
jagadaṇḍam idaṃ sarvam āsīt pūrvaṃ hiraṇmayam
prajāpater bhūtimayam itīyaṃ vaidikī śrutiḥ
tato varṣasahasrānte bibhedordhvamukhaṃ vibhuḥ
lokasaṃjananārthāya bibhedāṇḍaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
bhūyo 'ṣṭadhā bibhedāṇḍaṃ vibhur vai lokayonikṛt
cakāra jagataś cātra vibhāgaṃ sarvabhāgavit
yac chidram ūrdhvam ākāśaṃ parā sukṛtināṃ gatiḥ
vihitaṃ viśvayogena yad adhas tad rasātalam
yad aṇḍam akarot pūrvaṃ devalokasisṛkṣayā
samantād aṣṭadhā yogī chidrāṇi kṛtavāṃs tu saḥ
diśaś ca vidiśaḥ sarvā manasaivākarod vibhuḥ
nānārāgavirāgāṇi yāny aṇḍaśakalāni vai
bahuvarṇadharāś citrā babhūvus te balāhakāḥ
yad aṇḍamadhye skannaṃ tad dravam āsīt samāhitam
jātarūpaṃ tad abhavat tat sarvaṃ pṛthivītale
tasya kledo 'rṇavaughena prācchādyata samantataḥ
pṛthivī nikhilā rājan yugānte sāgarair iva
yac cāṇḍam akarot pūrvaṃ devalokacikīrṣayā
tatra yat salilaṃ skannaṃ so 'bhavat kāñcano giriḥ
tenāmbhasā plutāḥ sarvā diśaś copadiśas tathā
antarikṣaṃ ca nākaṃ ca yac cānyat kiṃcid antaram
yatra yatra jalaṃ skannaṃ tatra tatrotthito giriḥ
śailaiḥ sahasrair gahanā viṣamā medinī kṛtā
taiḥ sā parvatajālaughair bahuyojanavistṛtaiḥ
pīḍitā gurubhir devī pṛthivī vyathitābhavat
mahāmate bhūmitale divyaṃ nārāyaṇātmakam
hiraṇmayaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ tejo vimalarūpi tat
aśaktā vai dhārayitum adhastāt praviveśa ha
pīḍyamānā bhagavatas tejasā tena sā kṣitiḥ
pṛthivīṃ viśatīṃ dṛṣṭvā tām adho madhusūdanaḥ
uddhārārthaṃ manaś cakre tasyāḥ sa hitakāmyayā
śrībhagavān uvāca
matteja eva balavat samāsādya tapasvinī
rasātalaṃ viśed devī paṅke gaur iva durbalā
dharaṇy uvāca
trivikramāyāmitavikramāya
mahānṛsiṃhāya caturbhujāya
śrīśārṅgacakrāsigadādharāya
namo 'stu tasmai puruṣottamāya
tvayātmā dhāryate deva tvayā saṃdhāryate jagat
tvaṃ dhārayasi bhūtāni bhuvanaṃ tvaṃ bibharṣi ca
yat tvayā dhāryate kiṃcit tejasā ca balena ca
tatas tava prasādena mayā paścāt tu dhāryate
tvayā dhṛtaṃ dhārayāmi nādhṛtaṃ dhārayāmy aham
na hi tad vidyate bhūtaṃ yat tvayā nāvadhāryate
tvam eva kuruṣe vīra nārāyaṇa yuge yuge
mama bhārāvataraṇaṃ jagato hitakāmyayā
tavaiva tejasākrāntāṃ rasātalatalaṃ gatām
trāyasva māṃ suraśreṣṭha tvām eva śaraṇaṃ gatām
dānavaiḥ pīḍyamānāhaṃ rākṣasaiś ca durātmabhiḥ
tvām eva śaraṇaṃ nityam upayāmi sanātanam
tāvan me 'sti bhayaṃ bhūyo yāvan na tvāṃ kakudminam
śaraṇaṃ yāmi manasā śataśo 'py upalakṣitā
śrībhagavān uvāca
mā bhair dharaṇi kalyāṇi śāntiṃ vraja samāhitā
eṣa tvām ucitaṃ sthānaṃ mānayāmi manīṣitam
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tato mahātmā manasā divyaṃ rūpam acintayat
kiṃ nu rūpam ahaṃ kṛtvā uddharāmi vasuṃdharām
jale nimagnāṃ dharaṇīṃ yenāhaṃ vai samuddhare
ity evaṃ cintayitvā tu devas tatkaraṇe matim
jalakrīḍārucis tasmād vārāhaṃ vapur asmarat
harir uddharaṇe yuktas tadā bhūmeḥ sa bhūmidhṛk
adhṛṣyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ vāṅmayaṃ brahmasaṃmitam
daśayojanavistāram ucchritaṃ śatayojanam
nīlameghapratīkāśaṃ meghastanitanisvanam
mahāgireḥ saṃhananaṃ śvetadīptogradaṃṣṭriṇam
vidyudagnipratīkāśam ādityasamatejasam
pīnavṛttāyataskandhaṃ dṛptaśārdūlavikramam
pīnonnatakaṭīdeśaṃ vṛṣalakṣaṇapūjitam
rūpam āsthāya vipulaṃ vārāham amitaṃ hariḥ
pṛthivyuddharaṇārthāya praviveśa rasātalam
vedapado yūpadaṃṣṭraḥ kratudantaś citīmukhaḥ
agnijihvo darbhalomā brahmaśīrṣo mahātapāḥ
ahorātrekṣaṇadharo vedāṅgaśrutibhūṣaṇaḥ
ājyanāsaḥ sruvas tuṇḍaḥ sāmaghoṣasvano mahān
dharmasatyamayaḥ śrīmān kramavikramasatkṛtaḥ
kriyāsatramahāghoṇaḥ paśujānur mahākṛtiḥ
udgātāṅgo mahāliṅgo bījauṣadhimahāphalaḥ
vāyvantarātmā mantrasphig vikṛtaḥ somaśoṇitaḥ
vediskandho havirgandho havyakavyātivegavān
prāgvaṃśakāyo matimān nānādīkṣābhirācitaḥ
dakṣiṇāhṛdayo yogī mahāsatramayo mahān
upākarmoṣṭharucakaḥ pravargyāvartabhūṣaṇaḥ
nānāchandogatipatho guhyopaniṣadāsanaḥ
chāyāpatnīsahāyo vai maṇiśṛṅga ivocchritaḥ
bhūtvā yajñavarāho 'sau drāgadhaḥ prāviśad guruḥ
adbhiḥ saṃchāditām urvīṃ sa tām ārchat prajāpatiḥ
rasātalatale magnāṃ rasātalatalaṃ gataḥ
prabhur lokahitārthāya daṃṣṭrāgreṇojjahāra gām
tataḥ svasthānam ānīya pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīdharaḥ
mumoca pūrvaṃ sahasā dhārayitvā dharādharaḥ
tato jagāma nirvāṇaṃ medinī tasya dhāraṇāt
cakāra ca namaskāraṃ tasmai devāya śaṃbhave
evaṃ yajñavarāheṇa bhūtvā bhūtahitārthinā
uddhṛtā pṛthivī devī lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
athoddhṛtya kṣitiṃ devo jagataḥ sthāpanecchayā
pṛthivīpravibhāgāya manaś cakre 'mbujekṣaṇaḥ
rasātalagatām evaṃ vicintya sa surottamaḥ
tato vibhuḥ pravaravarāharūpadhṛg
vṛṣākapiḥ prasabham athaikadaṃṣṭrayā
samuddharad dharaṇim atulyavikramo
mahāyaśā lokahitārtham acyutaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tasyopari jalaughasya mahatī naur iva sthitā
vitatatvāt tu dehasya na yayau saṃplavaṃ mahī
tataḥ sa cintayām āsa pravibhāgaṃ kṣiter vibhuḥ
samucchrayaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ parvatānāṃ samantataḥ
vilekhanaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca gatiṃ prasavam eva ca
māhātmyaṃ ca viśeṣaṃ ca nadīnām anvacintayat
caturantāṃ dharāṃ kṛtvā kṛtvā caiva mahārṇavam
madhye pṛthivyāḥ sauvarṇam akaron meruparvatam
prācīṃ diśam atho gatvā cākarodayaparvatam
śatayojanavistāraṃ sahasraṃ ca samucchrayāt
jātarūpamayaiḥ śṛṅgais taruṇādityasaṃnibhaiḥ
ātmatejoguṇamayair vedikābhogakalpitaiḥ
vividhāṃś ca mahāskandhān kāñcanān puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ
nityapuṣpaphalān vṛkṣān kṛtavāṃs tatra parvate
śatayojanavistāraṃ tatas triguṇam ucchritam
cakāra sa mahādevaḥ punaḥ saumanasaṃ girim
nānāratnasahasrāṇāṃ kṛtvā tatra susaṃcayam
vedikāṃ bahuvarṇāṃ ca saṃdhyābhrābhām akalpayat
sahasraśṛṅgaṃ ca giriṃ nānāmaṇiśatālayam
kṛtavān vṛkṣagahanaṃ ṣaṣṭiyojanavistṛtam
āsanaṃ tatra paramaṃ sarvabhūtanamaskṛtam
kṛtavān ātmanaḥ sthānaṃ viśvakarmā prajāpatiḥ
śaiśiraṃ ca mahāśailaṃ tuṣāracayasaṃnibham
cakāra durgagahanaṃ kandarāntaramaṇḍitam
śiśiraprabhavāṃ caiva nadīṃ dvijagaṇākulām
cakāra pulinopetāṃ vasudhārām iti śrutiḥ
sā diśaṃ nikhilāṃ prācīṃ puṇyair mukhaśataiś citām
śobhayaty amṛtaprakhyair muktāśaṅkhavibhūṣitaiḥ
nityapuṣpaphalopetaiś chādayadbhiḥ susaṃhitaiḥ
bhūṣitābhyadhikaṃ kāntaiḥ sā nadītīrajair drumaiḥ
kṛtvā prācīvibhāgaṃ tu dakṣiṇāyām atho diśi
cakāra parvataṃ ramyaṃ sarvaṃ kāñcanarājatam
ekataḥ sūryasaṃkāśam ekataḥ śaśisaṃnibham
sa bibhracchuśubhe 'tīva dvau varṇau parvatottamaḥ
tejasā yugapad vyāptaṃ sūryācandramasor iva
vapuṣmantam atho tatra bhānumantaṃ mahāgirim
sarvakāmaphalair vṛkṣair vṛtaṃ ramyair manoramaiḥ
cakāra kuñjaraṃ caiva kuñjarapratimākṛtim
sarvataḥ kāñcanaguhaṃ bahuyojanavistṛtam
ṛṣabhapratimaṃ caiva ṛṣabhaṃ nāma parvatam
hemakāñcanavṛkṣāḍhyaṃ puṣpahāsaṃ sa sṛṣṭavān
mahendram atha śailendraṃ śatayojanam ucchritam
jātarūpamayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ supuṣpitamahādrumaiḥ
medinyāṃ kṛtavān devaḥ pratikṣobham ivācalam
nānāratnasamākīrṇaṃ sūryendusadṛśaprabham
cakāra malayaṃ cādriṃ citrapuṣpitapādapam
mainākaṃ ca mahāśailaṃ śilājālasamākulam
dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi śubhaṃ cakāra sa mahācalam
sahasraśirasaṃ vindhyaṃ nānādrumalatāyutam
nadīṃ ca vipulāvartāṃ vipulaśroṇibhūṣitām
kṣīrasaṃkāśasalilāṃ payodhārām iti śrutiḥ
suramyāṃ toyakalilāṃ vicitrāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ diśam
divyatīrthaśatāpāṅgīṃ plāvayantīṃ śubhāmbhasā
diśaṃ yāmyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya pratīcīṃ diśam āgamat
akarot tatra śailendraṃ śatayojanam ucchritam
śobhitaṃ śikharaiś citraiḥ supravṛddhair hiraṇmayaiḥ
kāñcanībhiḥ śilābhiś ca guhābhiś ca vibhūṣitam
samākulaṃ sūryanibhaiḥ sālais tālaiś ca bhāsvaraiḥ
śuśubhe jātarūpaiś ca śrīmadbhiś citravedikaiḥ
ṣaṣṭiṃ girisahasrāṇi tatrāsau saṃnyaveśayat
merupratimarūpāṇi vapuṣā prabhayā ca ha
sahasrajaladhāraṃ ca parvataṃ merusaṃnibham
puṇyatīrthaguṇopetaṃ bhagavān saṃnyaveśayat
ṣaṣṭiyojanavistāraṃ tāvad eva samucchritam
ātmarūpopamaṃ tatra vārāhaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
niveśayām āsa vibhur divyaṃ vaidūryaparvatam
rājatāḥ kāñcanāś caiva yatra divyāḥ śiloccayāḥ
tatraiva cakrasadṛśaṃ cakravantaṃ mahābalam
sahasrakūṭaṃ vipulaṃ bhagavān saṃnyaveśayat
śaṅkhapratimarūpaṃ ca rājataṃ parvatottamam
sitadrumalatākīrṇaṃ śaṅkhaṃ nāma nyaveśayat
suvarṇarasasaṃbhūtaṃ pārijātaṃ mahādrumam
mahataḥ parvatasyāgre puṣpahāsaṃ nyaveśayat
śubhām atirasāṃ caiva ghṛtadhārām iti śrutiḥ
varāhaḥ saritaṃ puṇyāṃ pratīcyām akarot prabhuḥ
pratīcyāṃ saṃvidhiṃ kṛtvā parvatān kāñcanojjvalān
guṇottarān uttarasyāṃ saṃnyaveśayad agrataḥ
tataḥ saumyagiriṃ saumyam antarikṣapramāṇataḥ
rukmadhātupraticchannam akarod bhāskaropamam
sa tu deśo visūryo 'pi tasya bhāsā prakāśate
tasya lakṣmyādhikaṃ bhāti tapatā raviṇā yathā
sūkṣmalakṣaṇavijñeyas tapatīva divākaraḥ
sahasraśikharaṃ caiva nānātīrthasamākulam
cakāra ratnasaṃkīrṇaṃ bhūyo 'staṃ nāma parvatam
manoharaguṇopetaṃ mandaraṃ cācalottamam
uddāmapuṣpagandhaṃ ca parvataṃ gandhamādanam
cakāra tasya śṛṅgeṣu suvarṇarasasaṃbhavām
jambūṃ jāmbūnadamayīm atyantādbhutadarśanām
giriṃ triśikharaṃ caiva tathā puṣkaraparvatam
śubhraṃ pāṇḍurameghābhaṃ kailāsaṃ ca nagottamam
himavantaṃ ca śailendraṃ divyadhātuvibhūṣitam
niveśayām āsa harir vārāhīṃ tanum āsthitaḥ
nadīṃ sarvaguṇopetām uttarasyāṃ diśi prabhuḥ
madhudhārāṃ sa kṛtavān divyāṃ mukhaśatākulām
sarve caiva kṣitidharāḥ sapakṣāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
tadā kṛtā bhagavatā vicitrāḥ parameṣṭhinā
sa kṛtvā pravibhāgaṃ tu pṛthivyā lokabhāvanaḥ
devāsuragaṇotpattau kṛtavān buddhim akṣayām
sarvāsu dikṣu kṣatajopamākṣaś
cakāra śailān vividhābhirāmān
hitāya lokasya sa lokanāthaḥ
puṇyāś ca nadyaḥ salilopagūḍhāḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
jagatsraṣṭumanā devaś cintayām āsa pūrvajaḥ
tasya cintayato vaktrān niḥsṛtaḥ puruṣaḥ kila
tataḥ sa puruṣo devaṃ kiṃ karomīty upasthitaḥ
prayuvāca smitaṃ kṛtvā devadevo jagatpatiḥ
vibhajātmānam ity uktvā gato 'ntardhānam īśvaraḥ
antarhitasya devasya saśarīrasya bhāsvataḥ
praśāntasyeva dīpasya gatis tasya na vidyate
tatas teneritāṃ vāṇīṃ so 'nvacintayata prabhuḥ
hiraṇyagarbho bhagavān ya eṣa cchandasi śrutaḥ
eṣa prajāpatiḥ pūrvam abhavad bhuvanādhipaḥ
tadāprabhṛti tasyādyo yajñabhāgo vidhīyate
prajāpatir uvāca
vibhajātmānam ity uktas tenāsmi sumahātmanā
katham ātmā vibhajyaḥ syāt saṃśayo hy atra me mahān
iti cintayatas tasya om ity evotthitaḥ svaraḥ
sa bhūmāv antarikṣe ca nāke ca kṛtavān svanam
taṃ caivābhyasatas tasya manasāramayat prabhuḥ
hṛdayād devadevasya vaṣaṭkāraḥ samutthitaḥ
bhūmyantarikṣanākānāṃ bhūrbhuvaḥsuvarātmikāḥ
mahāsmṛtimayāḥ puṇyā mahāvyāhṛtayo 'bhavan
chandasāṃ pravarā devī caturviṃśākṣarābhavat
tatpadaṃ saṃsmaran divyāṃ sāvitrīm akarot prabhuḥ
ṛksāmātharvayajuṣaś caturo bhagavān prabhuḥ
cakāra nikhilān vedān brahmayuktena karmaṇā
tatas tasyaiva manasaḥ sanaḥ sanaka eva ca
sanātanaś ca bhagavān varadaś ca sanandanaḥ
sanatkumāraś ca vibhus tatra jajñe sanātanaḥ
mānasāś caiva pūrvādyā ity ete ṣaṇmaharṣayaḥ
brahmāṇaṃ kapilaṃ caiva ṣaḍ etāṃś caiva yoginaḥ
yatayo yogatantreṣu yān stuvanti dvijātayaḥ
tato marīcim atriṃ ca pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum
bhṛgum aṅgirasaṃ caiva manuṃ caiva prajāpatim
pitṝṃś ca sarvabhūtānāṃ devatāsurarakṣasām
maharṣīn asṛjac chaṃbhur aṣṭāv etāṃs tu mānasān
ete yugasahasrānte yāś caiṣām abhavan prajāḥ
kalpe niḥśeṣamukte tu tato gacchanti nirvṛtim
bhūyo varṣasahasrānte utpattis tu vidhīyate
eteṣām eva devānāṃ prajākāraṇayoginām
kiṃ tu karmaviśeṣeṇa devatānāṃ yuge yuge
nāmajanmaviśeṣāś ca tathā yugaviparyaye
aṅguṣṭhād dakṣiṇād dakṣa utpanno bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
tasthaiva tu punar bhāryā vāmāṅguṣṭhād ajāyata
tatra tasyābhavat kanyā viśrutā lokamātaraḥ
yābhir vyāptās trayo lokāḥ prajābhir manujādhipa
aditiṃ ca ditiṃ kālām anāyuṃ siṃhikāṃ munim
prādhāṃ krodhāṃ ca surabhiṃ vinatāṃ surasāṃ tathā
danuṃ kadrūṃ ca duhitṝḥ pradadau kaśyapāya tu
prajāḥ saṃcintya manasā gatijñenāntarātmanā
arundhatīṃ vasuṃ yāmīṃ lambāṃ bhānuṃ marutvatīm
saṃkalpāṃ ca muhūrtāṃ ca sādhyāṃ viśvāṃ ca bhārata
manave brahmaputrāya kanyā dakṣo dadau daśa
tāś ca sarvān avadyāṅgyaḥ kanyāḥ kamalalocanāḥ
kīrtiṃ lakṣmīṃ dhṛtiṃ puṣṭiṃ buddhiṃ medhāṃ kriyāṃ tathā
matiṃ lajjāṃ vasuṃ caiva dakṣo dharmāya vai dadau
ātreyas tu tato bhūtas tasya toyātmakaḥ prabhuḥ
putro gṛhāṇām adhipaḥ sahasrāṃśus tamisrahā
tasmai nakṣatrayoginyaḥ saptāviṃśatir uttamāḥ
rohiṇīpramukhāḥ kanyā dakṣaḥ prācetaso dadau
etāsāṃ putrapautraṃ tu procyamānaṃ mayā śṛṇu
kaśyapasya manoś caiva dharmasya śaśinas tathā
aryamā varuṇo mitraḥ pūṣā dhātā puraṃdaraḥ
tvaṣṭā bhago 'ṃśaḥ savitā parjanyaś ceti viśrutāḥ
adityāṃ jajñire devāḥ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ
dityāṃ putradvayaṃ jajño kaśyapād iti naḥ śrutam
hiraṇyakaśipuś caiva hiraṇyākṣaś ca vīryavān
dvāv apy amitavikrāntau tapasā kaśyapopamau
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāḥ pañcaiva sumahābalāḥ
prahrādaḥ pūrvajas teṣām anuhrādas tato 'paraḥ
saṃhrādaś caiva hrādaś ca kanīyāṃsau babhūvatuḥ
virocanaś ca prāhrādir daityendro 'bhūn mahāyaśāḥ
virocanaś ca jambhaś ca sujambhaś ceti viśrutāḥ
balir virocanasuto bāṇa eko baleḥ sutaḥ
danoḥ putrās tu bahavo vaṃśe khyātā mahāsurāḥ
vipracittiḥ prathamajas teṣāṃ rājā babhūva ha
gaṇaḥ prajajñe krodhāyāḥ putrapautram anantakam
raudrāḥ krodhavaśā nāma krūrakarmāṇa eva te
siṃhikā suṣuve rāhuṃ grahaṃ candrārkamardanam
grastāraṃ caiva candrasya sūryasya ca vināśanam
kālāyāḥ kālakalpas tu gaṇaḥ paramadāruṇaḥ
abhavad dīptasūryākṣo nīlameghasamaprabhaḥ
sahasraśīrṣā śeṣaś ca vāsukis takṣakas tathā
bahūnāṃ kadruputrāṇām ete prādhānyam āgatāḥ
dharmātmāno vedavidaḥ sadā prāṇihite ratāḥ
lokatantradharāś caiva varadāḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
tārkṣyaś cāriṣṭanemiś ca garuḍaś ca mahābalaḥ
aruṇaś cāruṇiś caiva vinatāyāḥ sutāḥ smṛtāḥ
imāś cāpsarasaḥ puṇyā vividhāḥ puṇyalakṣaṇāḥ
suṣuve 'ṣṭau mahābhāgā prādhā devarṣipūjitāḥ
anavadyām anūkāṃ ca anūnām aruṇapriyām
anugāṃ subhagāṃ caiva striyaḥ prādhā vyajāyata
alambuṣā miśrakeśī puṇḍarīkā tilottamā
surūpā lakṣmaṇā kṣemā tathā rambhā manoramā
amitā ca subāhū ca suvṛttā sumukhī tathā
supriyā ca sugandhā ca surathā ca pramāthinī
kāśyā śāradvatī caiva mauneyāpsarasaḥ smṛtāḥ
viśvāvasur bharaṇyā ca gandharvāś caiva viśrutāḥ
menakā sahajanyā ca parṇinī puñjikasthalā
ghṛtasthalā ghṛtācī ca viśvācī corvaśī tathā
anumloceti vikhyātā pramloceti ca tā daśa
manovatī tathā caiva divyā apsarasaḥ smṛtāḥ
prajāpates tu saṃkalpāt saṃbhūtā bhuvanaśriyaḥ
amṛtaṃ brāhmaṇā gāvo rudrāśceti catuṣṭayam
surabhyapatyam ity etat purāṇe niścayo mahān
etad vai kaśyapāpatyaṃ manor vaṃśaṃ nibodhata
saṃkṣepeṇaiva tatsarvaṃ kīrtayiṣyāmi te 'nagha
viśvedevās tu viśvāyāḥ sādhyā sādhyān vyajāyata
marutvatyā marutvanto vasos tu vasavaḥ smṛtāḥ
bhānos tu bhānavas tāta muhūrtās tu muhūrtajāḥ
lambā ghoṣaṃ vijajñe 'tha nāgavīthī ca jāmijā
pṛthivīviṣayaṃ sarvaṃ marutvatyām ajāyata
saṃkalpāyās tu kauravya jajñe saṃkalpa eva ca
dharmasya putro lakṣmyās tu kāmo jajñe jagatpriyaḥ
yaśo harṣaś ca kāmasya ratyāṃ putradvayaṃ smṛtam
somasya putro rohiṇyāṃ jajñe varcā mahāprabhaḥ
udayann eva bhagavān varcasvī yena jāyate
evaṃ putrasahasrāṇi strīṇāṃ caiva parasparam
etāvat tu jaganmūlaṃ yatra lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
prajāpatis tu bhagavān guṇataḥ prekṣya dehinaḥ
ādhipatyeṣu yukteṣu niyojayati yogavit
diśo daśa kṣitim ṛṣayo 'rṇavān nagān
drumauṣadhīr uragasaritsurāsurān
prajāpatīn bhuvanasṛjo nabho bhuvaḥ
kriyā makhān atha kṛtavān girīṃś ca saḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
trayāṇām api lokānām ādityānāṃ ca bhārata
cakāra śakraṃ rājānam ādityasamatejasam
sa vajrī kavacī jiṣṇur adityām abhijajñivān
smṛtīsahāyo dyutimān yathā so 'dhvaryubhiḥ stutaḥ
jātamātro 'tha bhagavān adityā sa kuśair vṛtah
tadāprabhṛti deveśaḥ kauśikatvam upāgataḥ
abhiṣicyādhirājye tu sahasrākṣaṃ puraṃdaram
brahmā krameṇa rājyāni vyādeṣṭum upacakrame
yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ caiva nakṣatragrahayos tathā
dvijānām oṣadhīnāṃ ca somaṃ rājye 'bhyaṣecayat
dakṣaṃ prajāpatīnāṃ tu ambhasāṃ varuṇaṃ patim
pitṝṇāṃ sarvanidhanaṃ kālaṃ vaiśvānaraprabham
gandharvāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ ca śarīriṇām
śabdakālabalānāṃ ca vāyur īśas tadā kṛtaḥ
sarvabhūtapiśācānāṃ mātṝṇāṃ ca gavāṃ tathā
unmādagraharogāṇāṃ vyādhīnām ītināṃ tathā
pretānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ mahādevaḥ kṛtaḥ prabhuḥ
yakṣāṇāṃ rākṣasānāṃ ca guhyakānāṃ dhanasya ca
ratnānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ kṛto vaiśravaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
sarveṣāṃ daṃṣṭriṇāṃ śeṣo nāgānām atha vāsukiḥ
sarīsṛṣāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ prabhur vai takṣakaḥ kṛtaḥ
sāgarāṇāṃ nadīnāṃ ca meghānāṃ varṣitasya ca
ādityānām avarajaḥ parjanyo 'dhipatiḥ kṛtaḥ
gandharvāṇām adhipatiṃ cakre citrarathaṃ prabhum
sarvāpsarogaṇānāṃ ca kāmadevaḥ kṛtaḥ prabhuḥ
catuṣpadānāṃ sarveṣāṃ vāhanānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
maheśvaradhvajaḥ śrīmān govṛṣo 'dhipatiḥ kṛtaḥ
daityānāṃ ca mahātejā hiraṇyākṣaḥ prabhuḥ kṛtaḥ
dānavānāṃ ca sarveṣām anīkānāṃ tathaiva ca
vipracittaḥ prathamajas teṣāṃ rājye 'bhiṣecitaḥ
hiraṇyakaśipuś caiva yauvarājye 'bhiṣecitaḥ
gaṇānāṃ kālakeyānāṃ mahākālaḥ kṛtaḥ prabhuḥ
anāyuṣāyāḥ putrāṇāṃ vṛtro rājā tadā kṛtaḥ
siṃhikātanayo yas tu rāhur nāma mahāgrahaḥ
utpātānām anekānām aśubhānāṃ patiḥ kṛtaḥ
ṛtūnām atha sarveṣāṃ yugānāṃ caiva bhārata
pakṣāṇāṃ ca kṣapāṇāṃ ca tathāhastithiparvaṇām
kalākāṣṭhāmuhūrtānāṃ gater ayanayos tathā
kṛtaḥ saṃvatsaro rājā yogasya gaṇitasya ca
pakṣiṇām atha sarveṣāṃ nāgānāṃ ca mahābalaḥ
suparṇo bhogināṃ caiva guruḍo 'dhipatiḥ kṛtaḥ
aruṇo guruḍabhrātā japāpuṣpacayaprabhaḥ
rājā prācyāṃ diśi tathā vāsavo 'dhipatiḥ kṛtaḥ
ādityasya vibhoḥ putro dharmarājo mahāyaśāḥ
dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi yamo mahendreṇābhisatkṛtaḥ
kaśyapasyaurasaḥ putraḥ salilāntargatas tathā
amburāja iti khyātaḥ pratīcyāṃ diśi pārthivaḥ
pulastyaputro dyutimān mahedrapratimaḥ prabhuḥ
ekākṣaḥ piṅgalo nāma saumyāyāṃ diśi pārthivaḥ
evaṃ vibhajya rājyāni svayaṃbhūr lokabhāvanaḥ
lokāṃś ca tridive divyān adadāt sa pṛthak pṛthak
kasyacit sūryasaṃkāśān kasyacid vahnisaṃnibhān
kasyacid vidyududyotān kasyacic candranirmalān
nānāvarṇān kāmagamān anekaśatayojanān
satāṃ sukṛtināṃ lokān pāpaduṣkṛtidurlabhān
ye ca bhāsā vibhānty agre saumyās tārāgaṇā iva
ete sukṛtināṃ lokā ye jātāḥ puṇyakarmiṇaḥ
ye yajanti makhaiḥ puṇyaiḥ samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ
svadāraniratāḥ kṣāntā ṛjavaḥ satyavādinaḥ
dinānugrahakartāro brāhmaṇā lobhavarjitāḥ
te tyaktarajasaḥ śāntā yānti tatra tapojjvalāḥ
evaṃ niyujya tanayān svayaṃ lokapitāmahaḥ
puṣkaraṃ brahmasadanam āruroha prajāpatiḥ
sarve svayaṃbhudatteṣu pālaneṣu divaukasaḥ
remire sveṣu lokeṣu mahendreṇābhipālitāḥ
svayaṃbhuvā śakrapuraḥsarāḥ surāḥ
kṛtā yathārhaṃ pratipālaneṣu te
yaśo divaṃ ca pratipedire śubhaṃ
mudaṃ ca jagmur makhabhāgabhojinaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
kadācit tu sapakṣās te parvatā dharaṇīdharāḥ
prasthitā dharaṇīṃ tyaktvā nūnaṃ tasyaiva māyayā
tadāsurāṇāṃ nilayaṃ hiraṇyākṣeṇa pālitam
diśaṃ pratīcīm āgamya hrade 'majjan yathā gajāḥ
tatrāsurebhyaḥ śaṃsanta ādhipatyaṃ surāśrayam
tac chrutvāthāsurāḥ sarve cakrur udyogam uttamam
krūrāṃ ca buddhim atulāṃ pṛthivīharaṇe ratāḥ
āyudhāni ca sarvaṇi jagṛhur bhīmavikramāḥ
cakrāśanīṃs tathā khaḍgān bhuśuṇḍīś ca dhanūṃṣi ca
prāsān pāśāṃś ca śaktīś ca musalāni gadās tathā
kecit kavacinaḥ sajjā mattān nāgān samāsthitāḥ
kecid aśvarathān yuktā apare 'śvā mahārathāḥ
kecid uṣṭrāṃs tathā khaḍgān mahiṣān gardabhān api
svabāhubalam āsthāya kecic cāpi padātayaḥ
parivārya hiraṇyākṣaṃ talabaddhāḥ patākinaḥ
itaś cetaś ca niścerur hṛṣṭāḥ sarve yuyutsavaḥ
tato devagaṇāḥ paścāt puraṃdarapurogamāḥ
daityānāṃ viditodyogāś cakrur udyogam uttamam
mahatā caturaṅgeṇa balena susamāhitāḥ
baddhagodhāṅgulitrāṇās tūṇavantaḥ samārgaṇāḥ
ugrāyudhadharā devāḥ sveṣv anīkeṣv avasthitāḥ
airāvatagataṃ śakram anvagacchanta pṛṣṭhataḥ
tatas tūryaninādaiś ca bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaiḥ
abhyadravad dhiraṇyākṣo devarājaṃ puraṃdaram
tīkṣṇaiḥ paraśunistriṃśair gadātomaraśāktibhiḥ
musalaiḥ paṭṭisaiś caiva chādayām āsa vāsavam
tato 'strabalavegena sārciṣmatyaḥ sudāruṇāḥ
ghorarūpā mahāvegā nipetur bāṇavṛṣṭayaḥ
śiṣṭāś ca daityā balinaḥ śitadhārāparaśvadhaiḥ
parighair āyasaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ kṣepaṇīyaiś ca mudgaraiḥ
gaṇḍaśailaiś ca vipulair aśmabhiś cādrisaṃnibhaiḥ
ghātanībhiś ca gurvībhiḥ śataghnībhis tathaiva ca
yugair yantraiś ca nirmuktair argalaiś ca vidāraṇaiḥ
sarvān devagaṇān daityāḥ saṃnijaghnuḥ savāsavān
dhūmrakeśaṃ hariśmaśruṃ nānāpraharaṇāyudham
raktasaṃdhyābhrasaṃkāśaṃ kirīṭottamadhāriṇam
nīlapītāmbaradharaṃ sitodvṛttogradaṃṣṭriṇam
ājānubāhuṃ haryakṣaṃ vaidūryābharaṇojjvalam
samudyatāyudhaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve devagaṇās tadā
te hiraṇyākṣam asuraṃ daityānām agrataḥ sthitam
yugāntasamaye bhīmaṃ sthitaṃ mṛtyum ivāgrataḥ
pravivyathuḥ surāḥ sarve tadā śakrapurogamāḥ
dṛṣṭvāyāntaṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ mahādrim iva jaṅgamam
devāḥ saṃvignamanasaḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanāḥ
sahasrākṣaṃ puraskṛtya tasthuḥ saṃgrāmamūrdhani
sā tu daityacamū reje hiraṇyakavacojjvalā
pravṛddhanakṣatragaṇā śāradī dyaur ivāmalā
te 'nyonyam abhisaṃpetuḥ pātayantaḥ parasparam
babhañjur bāhubhir bāhūn dvaṃdvam anye yuyutsavaḥ
gadānipātair bhagnāṅgā bāṇaiś ca mathitorasaḥ
vinipetuḥ pṛthak kecit tathānye vijughūrṇire
babhañjire rathān kecit kecit saṃmṛditā rathaiḥ
saṃbādham anye saṃprāptā na śekuś calituṃ rathāḥ
dānavendrabalaṃ tat tu devānāṃ ca mahad balam
anyonyaṃ bāṇavarṣeṇa yuddhadurdinam ābabhau
hiraṇyākṣaś ca balavān kruddhaḥ sa ditinandanaḥ
vyavardhata mahātejāḥ samudra iva parvaṇi
tasya kruddhasya sahasā mukhān niścerur arciṣaḥ
taiḥ sāgnidhūmapavanair vyadahad devatāgaṇān
śastrajālair bahuvidhair dhanurbhiḥ parighair api
divyam ākāśam āvavre parvatair ucchritair iva
bahubhiḥ śatranistriṃśaiś chinnabhinnaśirorasaḥ
na śekuś calituṃ devā hiraṇyākṣārditā yudhi
tena vitrāsitā devā hiraṇyākṣeṇa saṃyuge
na śekur yatnavanto 'pi yatnaṃ kartuṃ vicetasaḥ
tena śakraḥ sahasrākṣaḥ stambhito 'streṇa dhīmatā
airāvatagataḥ saṃkhye nāśakac calituṃ bhayāt
sarvāṃś ca devān akhilān sa parājitya dānavaḥ
stambhayitvā ca deveśam ātmasthaṃ manyate jagat
satoyameghapratimogranisvanaṃ
prabhinnamātaṅgavilāsavikramam
dhanurvidhunvantam udāravarcasaṃ
tadāsurendraṃ dadṛśuḥ surāḥ sthitam
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
niṣprayatne surapatau dharṣiteṣu sureṣu ca
hiraṇyākṣavadhe buddhiṃ cakre cakragadādharaḥ
vārāhaḥ parvato nāma yaḥ pūrvaṃ samudāhṛtaḥ
sa eṣa bhūtvā bhagavān ājagāmāsurāntakṛt
tataś candrapratīkāśaṃ so 'gṛhṇāc chaṅkham uttamam
sahasrāraṃ ca taccakraṃ cakraparvatasaṃsthitam
mahādevo mahābuddhir mahāyogī maheśvaraḥ
japyate yo 'maraiḥ sarvair guhyair nāmabhir avyayaḥ
sa ca sarvātmani śreṣṭhaḥ sadbhir yaḥ sevyate sadā
ijyate ca purāṇaiś ca triloke lokabhāvanaḥ
yo vaikuṇṭhaḥ surendrāṇām ananto bhoginām api
viṣṇur yo yogaviduṣāṃ yo yajño yajñakarmaṇi
makhe yasya prasādena bhuvanasthā divaukasaḥ
ājyaṃ maharṣibhir dattam aśnuvanti tridhā hutam
yo naidhano 'gnir daityānāṃ yaḥ surāṇāṃ parā gatiḥ
yaḥ pavitraṃ pavitrāṇāṃ svayaṃbhor api yo vibhuḥ
yasya cakrapraviṣṭāni dānavānāṃ yuge yuge
kulāny ākulatāṃ yānti yāni dṛptāni vīryataḥ
tato daityadravakaraṃ paurāṇaṃ śaṅkham uttamam
dadhmau prāṇena balavān vikṣipan daityajīvitam
śrutvā śaṅkhasvanaṃ ghoram asurāṇāṃ bhayāvaham
kṣubhitā dānavāḥ sarve diśo daśa vilokayan
tataḥ saṃraktanayano hiraṇyākṣo mahasuraḥ
ko 'yam ity abravīd roṣān nārāyaṇam udaikṣata
varāharūpiṇaṃ devaṃ saṃsthitaṃ puruṣaṃ yathā
śaṅkhacakrodyatakaraṃ devānām ārtināśanam
rarāja śaṅkhacakrābhyāṃ tābhyām asurasūdanaḥ
sūryācandramasor madhye yathā nīlaḥ payodharaḥ
tato 'suragaṇāḥ sarve hiraṇyākṣapurogamāḥ
udyatāyudhanistriṃśā dṛṣṭvā devam upādravan
pīḍyamāno 'tibalibhir daityaiḥ sarvāyudhodyataiḥ
na cacāla harir yuddhe 'kampamāna ivācalaḥ
tataḥ prajvalitāṃ śaktiṃ varāhorasi dānavaḥ
hiraṇyākṣo mahātejāḥ pātayām āsa vīryavān
tasyāḥ śaktyāḥ prahāreṇa brahmā vismayam āgataḥ
tasyāṃ pratihatāyāṃ tu brahmā sādhv iti cābravīt
yaḥ prabhuḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ varāhas tena tāḍitaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tato bhagavatā cakram āvidhyād ity asaṃnibham
pātitaṃ dānavendrasya śirasy uttamatejasaḥ
tataḥ sthitasyaiva śiras tasya bhūmau papāta ha
daityendrasyāśanihataṃ meruśṛṅgam ivottamam
hiraṇyākṣe hate daitye ye śeṣās tatra dānavāḥ
sarve tasya bhayatrastā jagmur ārtā diśo daśa
sa sarvalokāpraticakracakro
mahāhaveṣv apratimogracakraḥ
babhau varāho yudhi cakrapāṇiḥ
kālo yugānteṣv iva daṇḍapāṇiḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
vidrāvya tu raṇe sarvān asurān puruṣottamaḥ
mumoca tatra baddhāṃs tān puraṃdaramukhān surān
tataḥ prakṛtim āpannāḥ sarve devagaṇās tadā
puraṃdaraṃ puraskṛtya nārāyaṇam upasthitāḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
devā ūcuḥ
tvatprasādena bhagavaṃs tava bāhubalena ca
jīvāmo 'dya mahābāho niṣkrāntāś cāntakānanāt
tvacchāsanād dhi bhagavan kiṃ kurvantv aditeḥ sutāḥ
icchāmaḥ pādaśuśrūṣāṃ tava kartuṃ sanātana
tac chrutvā vacanaṃ teṣāṃ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇaḥ
uvāca vacanaṃ devān mudā yukto hatadviṣaḥ
yo 'yaṃ sa bhavatāṃ loko mayaiva vihitaḥ purā
pālyatāṃ sa tu yatnena prādhānyena kvacit kvacit
aiśvaryaṃ pratipannāḥ stha kratubhāgapuraskṛtam
mayaiva pūrvaṃ nirdiṣṭo niyogaḥ paripālyatām
śakraṃ provāca bhagavān vacanaṃ duṃdubhisvanaḥ
idaṃ yathāvat kartavyaṃ satsu cāsatsu ca tvayā
gacchantu tapasā svargaṃ munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
yajñair iṣṭvā yāyajūkāḥ phalaṃ te prāpnuvantu ca
bhāvaḥ svadharmaśīlānām abhāvaḥ pāpakarmaṇām
santaḥ svargajitaḥ santu sarvāśramanivāsinaḥ
satyaśūrā dānaśūrā raṇaśūrāś ca ye narāḥ
te svargaphalam aśnantu sadā ye cānasūyakāḥ
aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣāḥ kāmino 'rthaparāḥ śaṭhāḥ
abrahmaṇyā nāstikāś ca narakaṃ yāntu mānavāḥ
etāvat kriyatāṃ vākyaṃ mayoktaṃ tridaśeśvarāḥ
tato mayi sthite sarvān bādhiṣyante na cārayaḥ
ity uktvāntarhito devaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
devatānāṃ ca sarveṣām abhavad vismayo mahān
etad atyadbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā varāhacaritaṃ surāḥ
namaskṛtvā varāhāya nākapṛṣṭham ito gatāḥ
tataḥ svāny ādhipatyāni pratipannāni daivataiḥ
sarvalokādhipatye ca pratiṣṭhāṃ vāsavo gataḥ
vimuktā dānavagaṇaiḥ prakṛtiṃ dharaṇī gatā
sthairyahetor dharaṇyās tu jñātvā cāgaskṛtān girīn
sveṣu sthāneṣu saṃsthāpya parvatānāṃ puraṃdaraḥ
ciccheda bhagavān pakṣān vajreṇa śataparvaṇā
sarveṣām eva pakṣā vai chinnāḥ śakreṇa dhīmatā
ekaḥ sapakṣo mainākaḥ surais tatsamayaḥ kṛtaḥ
eṣa nārāyaṇasyādyaḥ prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ
vārāha iti viprendraiḥ purāṇe parikīrtitaḥ
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanamataṃ nānāśrutisamāhitam
nāśūcerna kṛtaghnāya nṛśaṃsāya na kīrtayet
āyuṣkāmair yaśaskāmair mahīkāmaiś ca mānavaiḥ
jayaiṣibhiś ca śrotavyo devānām eṣa vai jayaḥ
purāṇo vedasaṃbaddhaḥ śivaḥ svastyayano mahān
pāvanaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sāttviko vijayaṃkaraḥ
eṣa kauravya tattvena kathitas te 'nupūrvaśaḥ
varāhasya naraśreṣṭha prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ
ye yajanti makhaiḥ puṇyair daivatāni pitṝn api
ātmānam ātmanā nityaṃ viṣṇum eva yajanti te
lokāyanāya tridaśāyanāya
brahmāyanāyātmabhavāyanāya
nārāyaṇāyātmahitāyanāya
mahāvarāhāya namaskuruṣva
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
vārāha eṣa kathito nārasiṃham ataḥ śṛṇu
janamejaya uvāca
yatra bhūtvā mṛgendreṇa hiraṇyakaśipur hataḥ
purā kṛtayuge rājan hiraṇyakaśipuḥ prabhuḥ
daityānām ādipuruṣaś cakāra sumahattapaḥ
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca
jalavāsī samabhavat sthānamaunadhṛtavrataḥ
tataḥ śamadamābhyāṃ ca brahmacaryeṇa caiva ha
brahmā prīto 'bhavat tasya tapasā niyamena ca
tataḥ svayaṃbhūr bhagavān svayam āgatya tatra ha
vimānenārkavarṇena haṃsayuktena bhāsvatā
ādityair vasubhiḥ sādhyair marudbhir daivataiḥ saha
rudrair viśvasahāyaiś ca yakṣarākṣasakiṃnaraiḥ
digbhiś cāpi vidigbhiś ca nadībhiḥ sāgarais tathā
nakṣatraiś ca muhūrtaiś ca khecaraiś ca mahāgrahaiḥ
devair brahmarṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ siddhaiḥ saptarṣibhis tathā
rājarṣibhiḥ puṇyakṛdbhir gandharvair apsarogaṇaiḥ
carācaraguruḥ śrīmān vṛto devagaṇaiḥ saha
brahmā brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭho daityaṃ vacanam abravīt
prīto 'smi tava bhaktasya tapasānena suvrata
varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yatheṣṭaṃ kāmam āpnuhi
hiraṇyakaśipur uvāca
na devāsuragandharvā na yakṣoragarākṣasāḥ
na mānuṣāḥ piśācāś ca nihanyur māṃ kathaṃcana
ṛṣayo naiva māṃ kruddhāḥ sarvalokapitāmaha
śapeyus tapasā yuktā vara eṣa vṛto mayā
na śastreṇa na cāstreṇa giriṇā pādapena vā
na śuṣkeṇa na cārdreṇa na cānyenāpi me vadhaḥ
na svarge 'py atha pātāle nākāśe nāvanisthale
na cābhyantararātryahnor na cāpyanyena me vadhaḥ
pāṇiprahāreṇaikena sabhṛtyabalavāhanam
yo māṃ nāśayituṃ śaktaḥ sa me mṛtyur bhaviṣyati
bhaveyam aham evārkaḥ somo vāyur hutāśanaḥ
salilaṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca nakṣatrāṇi diśo daśa
ahaṃ krodhaś ca kāmaś ca varuṇo vāsavo yamaḥ
dhanadaś ca dhanādhyakṣo yakṣaḥ kiṃpuruṣādhipaḥ
mūrtimanti ca divyāni mamāstrāṇi mahāhave
upatiṣṭhantu deveśa sarvalokapitāmaha
brahmovāca
ete divyā varās tāta mayā dattās tavādbhutāḥ
sarvakāmapradā vatsa prāpsyase tān na saṃśayaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
evam uktvā sa bhagavāñ jagāmākāśam eva ca
vairājaṃ brahmasadanaṃ brahmarṣigaṇasevitam
tato devāś ca nāgāś ca gandharvā ṛṣibhiḥ saha
varapradānaṃ śrutvaiva pitāmaham upasthitāḥ
devā ūcuḥ
vareṇānena bhagavan vadhiṣyati sa no 'suraḥ
tat prasīdasva bhagavan vadho 'py asya vicityatām
vaiśaṃpayana uvāca
bhagavān sarvabhūtānām ādikartā svayaṃ prabhuḥ
sraṣṭā ca havyakavyānām avyaktaḥ prakṛtir dhruvaḥ
sarvalokahitaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā devaḥ prajāpatiḥ
āśvāsayām āsa surān suśītair vacanāmbubhiḥ
avaśyaṃ tridasās tena prāptavyaṃ tapasaḥ phalam
tapaso 'nte 'sya bhagavān vadhaṃ viṣṇuḥ kariṣyati
etac chrutvā surāḥ sarve vākyaṃ paṅkajajanmanaḥ
svāni sthānāni divyāni pratijagmur mudānvitāḥ
labdhamātre vare tasmin sarvāḥ so 'bādhata prajāḥ
hiraṇyakaśipur daityo varadānena darpitaḥ
āśrameṣu munīn sarvān brāhmaṇān saṃśitavratān
satyadharmaratān dāntān dharṣayām āsa vīryavān
devāṃs tribhuvanasthāṃś ca parājitya mahāsuraḥ
trailokyaṃ vaśam ānīya svarge vasati dānavaḥ
yadā varamadonmattaś coditaḥ kāladharmaṇā
yajñiyān akarod daityān devāṃś caivāpy ayajñiyān
athādityāś ca sādhyāś ca viśve ca vasavas tathā
rudrā devagaṇā yakṣā devadvijamaharṣayaḥ
śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ viṣṇum upatasthur mahābalam
devaṃ devamayaṃ yajñaṃ brahmadevaṃ sanātanam
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca prajālokanamaskṛtam
nārāyaṇaṃ mahādevaṃ devās tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ
tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo dhātā tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo guruḥ
tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo devo brahmādīnāṃ surottama
tvaṃ phullāmalapatrākṣa śatrupakṣakṣayāvaha
kṣayāya ditivaṃśasya śaraṇaṃ bhava naḥ prabho
viṣṇur uvāca
bhayaṃ tyajadhvam amarā abhayaṃ vo dadāmy aham
tathaiva tridivaṃ devāḥ pratipatsyatha māciram
eṣo 'haṃ sagaṇaṃ daityaṃ varadānena darpitam
avadhyam amarendrāṇāṃ dānavendraṃ nihanmy aham
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
evam uktvā tu bhagavān visṛjya tridivaukasaḥ
vadhaṃ saṃkalpayitvā tu hiraṇyakaśipoḥ prabhuḥ
sahāyaṃ tu mahābāhur jagrāhoṃkāram eva ca
athoṃkārasahāyo 'sau bhagavān viṣṇur acyutaḥ
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sthānaṃ jagāma prabhur īśvaraḥ
tejasā bhāskara iva kāntyā candra ivāparaḥ
narasya kṛtvārdhatanuṃ siṃhasyārdhatanuṃ prabhuḥ
nārasiṃhena vapuṣā pāṇiṃ saṃspṛśya pāṇinā
tato 'paśyat suvistīrṇāṃ divyāṃ ramyāṃ manoramām
sarvakāmayutāṃ śubhrāṃ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sabhām
vistīrṇāṃ yojanaśataṃ śatam adhyardham āyatām
vaihāyasīṃ kāmagamāṃ pañcayojanam ucchritām
jarāśokaklamatyaktāṃ niṣprakampāṃ śivāṃ śubhām
śubhrāsanavatīṃ ramyāṃ jvalantīm iva tejasā
antaḥsalilasaṃyuktāṃ vihitāṃ viśvakarmaṇā
divyaratnamayair vṛkṣaiḥ phalapuṣpapradair yutām
nīlapītāsitaśyāmaiḥ sitair lohitakair api
avatānais tathā gulmair mañjarīśatadhāribhiḥ
sitābhraghanasaṃkāśā plavantīvāpsu dṛśyate
śayyāsanavatī ramyā jvalantīva ca tejasā
prabhāvatī bhāsurā ca divyagandhā manoramā
nāsukhā na ca duhkhā sā na śītā na ca gharmadā
na kṣutpipāse glāniṃ vā prāpya tāṃ prāpnuvanti ha
nānārūpair viracitā vicitrair atibhāsvaraiḥ
stambhair maṇimayair divyaiḥ śāśvatī cākṣayā ca yā
ati candraṃ ca sūryaṃ ca pāvakaṃ ca svayaṃprabhā
dīpyate nākapṛṣṭhasthā bhartsayantīva bhāskaram
sarve ca kāmāḥ pracurā ye divyā ye ca mānuṣāḥ
rasavantaḥ prabhūtāś ca bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ tathākṣayam
puṇyagandhāḥ srajas tatra nityapuṣpaphaladrumāḥ
uṣṇe śītāni toyāni śīte coṣṇāni santi vai
puṣpitāgrā mahāśākhāḥ pravālāṅkuradhāriṇaḥ
latāvitānasaṃchannāḥ saraḥsu ca saritsu ca
manoharāṃś ca vividhān dadarśa sa tadā prabhuḥ
drumān bahuvidhāṃs tatra mṛgendro dadṛśe prabhuḥ
gandhavanti ca puṣpāṇi rasavanti phalāni ca
tāni śītāni toyāni tatra tatra sarāṃsi ca
apaśyat sarvatīrthāni sabhāyāṃ tasya vai prabhuḥ
nalinaiḥ puṇḍarīkaiś ca śatapatraiḥ sugandhibhiḥ
raktaiḥ kuvalayair nīlaiḥ kumudaiḥ saṃtatāni ca
sakāntair dhārtarāṣṭraiś ca rājahaṃsaiḥ saraḥpriyaiḥ
kādambaiś cakravākaiś ca sārasaiḥ kurarair api
vimalasphaṭikābhāni pāṇḍuracchadanāni ca
kalahaṃsopagītāni sārasābhirutāni ca
gandhavatyaḥ śubhās tatra puṣpamañjaridhāriṇīḥ
dṛṣṭavān pādapāgreṣu nānāpuṣpadharā latāḥ
ketakāśokasaralāḥ punnāgatilakārjunāḥ
cūtā nīpā nāgapuṣpāḥ kadambā bakulā dhavāḥ
priyaṅgupāṭalā vṛkṣāḥ śālmalyaḥ saharidravāḥ
sālās tālāḥ priyālāś ca campakāś ca manoharāḥ
tathaivānye vyarājanta sabhāyāṃ puṣpitā drumāḥ
vidrumāś ca drumānīkā dāvāgnijvalitaprabhāḥ
skandhavantaḥ suśākhāś ca bahutālasamucchrayāḥ
añjanāśokavarṇābhā bhānti vañjulakā drumāḥ
varaṇā vatsanābhāś ca asanāḥ syandanaiḥ saha
nīlāḥ sumanasaś caiva pītāḥ sāśvatthatindukāḥ
prācīnāmalakā lodhrā mallikā bhadradāravaḥ
āmrātakās tathā jambūr lakucāś cailavālukāḥ
sarjarasāḥ kundaravāḥ pataṅgāḥ kuṭajās tathā
raktāḥ kurabakāś caiva nīpāś cāgurubhiḥ saha
kadambāś caiva bhavyāś ca dāḍimā bījapūrakāḥ
kālīyakā dukūlāś ca hiṅgavas tailaparṇikāḥ
kharjūrā nārikelāś ca dharmavṛkṣā harītakī
madhukāḥ saptaparṇāś ca bilvāḥ pārāvatās tathā
panasāś ca tamālāś ca nānāgulmalatāvṛtāḥ
latāś ca vividhākārāḥ puṣpapatraphalopagāḥ
ete cānye ca bahavas tatra kānanajā drumāḥ
nānāpuṣphaphalopetā vyarājanta samantataḥ
cakorāḥ śatapatrāś ca mattakokilasārikāḥ
puṣpitān puṣpitāgrāṃś ca saṃpatanti mahādrumān
raktapītāruṇās tatra pādapāgragatā dvijāḥ
parasparam avaikṣanta prahṛṣṭā jīvajīvakāḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ daityendro hiraṇyakaśipus tadā
āsīna āsane citre nalvamātre pramāṇataḥ
divākaranibhe divye divyāstaraṇasaṃvṛte
rarāja suciraṃ rājañ jvalatkāñcanakuṇḍalaḥ
tasya daityapater mandaṃ virajaskaḥ samantataḥ
divyagandhavahas tatra mārutaḥ susukho vavau
tatra devāḥ sagandharvā gaṇair apsarasāṃ vṛtāḥ
divyatālena divyāni jagur gītāni gāyanāḥ
viśvācī sahajanyā ca pramlocety abhiviśrutāḥ
divyā ca saurabheyī ca samīcī puñjikasthalā
miśrakeśī ca rambhā ca citrasenā śucismitā
cārunetrā ghṛtācī ca menakā corvaśī tathā
etāḥ sahasraśaś cānyā nṛtyavāditrakovidāḥ
upatiṣṭhanti rājānaṃ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ tadā
hiraṇyakaśipus tatra vicitrābharaṇāmbaraḥ
strīsahasraiḥ parivṛtas tasthau jvalitakuṇḍalaḥ
tatrāsīnaṃ mahābāhuṃ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prabhum
upāsanta diteḥ putrāḥ sarve labdhavarāḥ purā
balir virocanas tatra narakaḥ pṛthivījayaḥ
prahlādo vipracittiś ca gaviṣṭhaś ca mahāsuraḥ
cakrahantā krodhahantā sumanāḥ sumatisvanaḥ
ghaṭodaro mahāpārśvaḥ krathanaḥ piṭharas tathā
viśvarūpaḥ surūpaś ca virūpaś ca mahādyutiḥ
daśagrīvaś ca vālī ca meghavāsā mahāravaḥ
ghaṭābho vikaṭābhaś ca saṃhrādaś cendratāpanaḥ
daityadānavasaṃghāś ca sarve jvalitakuṇḍalāḥ
sragviṇo vāgminaḥ sarve sarve sucaritavratāḥ
sarve labdhavarāḥ śūrāḥ sarve vigatamṛtyavaḥ
ete cānye ca bahavo hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prabhum
upāsante mahātmānaṃ sarve divyaparicchadāḥ
vimānair vividhair agryair bhrājamānair ivārcibhiḥ
sragviṇo bhūṣitāḥ sarve yānti cāyānti cāpare
mahendracāpasaṃkāśair vicitrair aṅgadair varaiḥ
bhūṣitāṅgā diteḥ putrās tam upāsanta sarvaśaḥ
tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ divyāyām asurāḥ parvatopamāḥ
hiraṇyamukuṭāḥ sarve divākarakaraprabhāḥ
kanakamaṇivicitravedikāyām
upahitavedisavajravīthikāyām
sa dadarśa mṛgādhipaḥ sabhāyāṃ
suruciradantagavākṣasaṃvṛtāyām
kanakakamalahārabhūṣitāṇgaṃ
dititanayaṃ sa mṛgādhipo dadarśa
divasakarakaraprabhaṃ jvalantam
asurasahasragaṇair niṣevyamāṇam
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tato dṛṣṭvā mahābāhuṃ kālacakram ivāgatam
nārasiṃhavapuś channaṃ bhasmacchannam ivānalam
vikuñcitasaṭāntasya nārasiṃhasya bhārata
rūpaudāryaṃ babhau tatra samastaṃ śaśisaṃnibham
aho rūpam idaṃ citraṃ śaṅkhakundendusaṃnibham
abruvan dānavāḥ sarve hiraṇyakaśipuś ca saḥ
evaṃ hi bruvatāṃ teṣāṃ nirdagdhānāṃ mahātmanām
nārasiṃhena cakṣurbhyāṃ coditāḥ kāladharmaṇā
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putraḥ prahrādo nāma vīryavān
divyena cakṣuṣā siṃham apaśyad devam āgatam
taṃ dṛṣṭvā rukmaśailābham apūrvāṃ tanum āsthitam
vismitā dānavāḥ sarve hiraṇyakaśipuś ca saḥ
prahrāda uvāca
mahārāja mahābāho daityānām ādisaṃbhava
na śrutaṃ naiva no dṛṣṭaṃ nārasiṃham idaṃ vapuḥ
avyaktaprabhavaṃ divyaṃ kim idaṃ rūpam adbhutam
daityāntakaraṇaṃ ghoraṃ śaṃsatīva manāṃsi naḥ
asya devāḥ śarīrasthāḥ sāgarāḥ saritas tathā
himavān pāriyātraś ca ye cānye kulaparvatāḥ
candramāḥ saha nakṣatrair ādityāś cāgninā saha
dhanado varuṇaś caiva yamaḥ śakraḥ śacīpatiḥ
maruto devagandharvā ṛṣayaś ca tapodhanāḥ
nāgā yakṣāḥ piśācāś ca rākṣasā bhīmavikramāḥ
brahmā devaḥ paśupatir lalāṭasthā vibhānti vai
sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni jaṅgamāni tathaiva ca
bhavāṃś ca sahito 'smābhiḥ sarvadaityagaṇair vṛtaḥ
vimānaśatasaṃkīrṇā tathābhyantarajā sabhā
sarvaṃ tribhuvanaṃ rājaṃl lokadharmaś ca śāśvataḥ
dṛśyate nārasiṃhe 'smin yathendau vimale jagat
prajāpatiś cātra manur mahātmā
grahāś ca yāgāś ca mahī nabhaś ca
utpātakālaś ca dhṛtiḥ smṛtiś ca
rajaś ca sattvaṃ ca tamo damaś ca
sanatkumāraś ca mahānubhāvo
viśve ca devā vasavaś ca sarve
krodhaś ca kāmaś ca tathaiva harṣo
darpaś ca mohaḥ pitaraś ca sarve
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
prahrādasya tataḥ śrūtvā hiraṇyakaśipur vacaḥ
uvāca dānavān sarvān sagaṇāṃś ca gaṇādhipaḥ
mṛgendro gṛhyatāṃ śīghram apūrvāṃ tanum āsthitaḥ
yadi vā saṃśayaḥ kaścid vadhyatāṃ vanagocaraḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tac chrutvā dānavāḥ sarve mṛgendraṃ bhīmavikramam
parikṣipanto muditās trāsayām āsur ojasā
siṃhanādaṃ vimucyātha narasiṃho mahābalaḥ
babhañja tāṃ sabhāṃ divyāṃ vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥ
sabhāyāṃ bhajyamānāyāṃ hiraṃyakaśipuḥ svayam
cikṣepāstrāṇi siṃhasya roṣavyākulalocanaḥ
sarvāstrāṇām atha śreṣṭhaṃ daṇḍam astraṃ subhairavam
kālacakraṃ tathātyugraṃ viṣṇucakraṃ tathāparam
dharmacakraṃ mahācakram ajitaṃ nāma nāmataḥ
cakram aindraṃ tathā ghoram ṛṣicakraṃ tathaiva ca
paitāmahaṃ tathā cakraṃ trailokyam ahitasvaram
vicitrām aśanīṃ caiva śuṣkārdraṃ cāśanidvayam
raudraṃ tad ugraṃ śūlaṃ ca kaṅkālaṃ musalaṃ tathā
astraṃ brahmaśiraś caiva brāhmam astraṃ tathaiva ca
aiṣīkam astram aindraṃ ca āgneyaṃ śaiśiraṃ tathā
vāyavyaṃ mathanaṃ nāma kāpālam atha kiṃkaram
tathā cāpratimāṃ śaktiṃ krauñcam astraṃ tathaiva ca
astraṃ hayaśiraś caiva somāstraṃ śiśiraprabham
paiśācam astram amitaṃ sārpam astraṃ tathādbhutam
mohanaṃ śoṣaṇaṃ caiva saṃtāpanavilāpanam
darpaṇaṃ pātanaṃ caiva tvāṣṭraṃ caiva sudāruṇam
kālamudgaram akṣobhyaṃ kṣobhaṇaṃ ca mahābalam
saṃvartaṃ mohanaṃ caiva tathā māyādharaṃ param
gāndharvam astraṃ dayitam asiratnaṃ ca nandakam
prasvāpanaṃ pramathanaṃ vāruṇaṃ cāstram uttamam
astraṃ pāśupataṃ caiva yasyāpratihatā gatiḥ
etāny astrāṇi sarvāṇi hiraṇyakaśipus tadā
cikṣepa nārasiṃhasya dīptasyāgrer yathāhutiḥ
astraiḥ prajvalitaiḥ siṃham āvṛṇod asurādhipaḥ
vivasvān gharmasamaye himavantam ivāṃśubhiḥ
sa hi varṣāniloddhūto daityānāṃ sainyasāgaraḥ
kṣaṇenāplāvayat siṃhaṃ mainākam iva sāgaraḥ
prāsaiḥ pāśaiś ca śūlaiś ca gadābhir musalais tathā
vajrair aśanikalpaiś ca śilābhiś ca mahādrumaiḥ
mudgaraiḥ kūṭapāśaiś ca śūlolūkhalaparvataiḥ
śataghnībhiś ca dīptābhir daṇḍair api sudāruṇaiḥ
te dānavāḥ pāśagṛhītahastā
mahendravajrāśanitulyavegāḥ
samantato 'bhyudyatabāhuśastrāḥ
sthitāstriśīrṣā iva nāgapotāḥ
suvarṇamālākulabhūṣitāṅgāś
cīnāṃśukābhogavibhūṣitāṅgāḥ
muktāvalīdāmavibhūṣitāṅgā
haṃsā ivābhānti viśālapakṣāḥ
teṣāṃ ca vāyupratimaujasāṃ vai
keyūramālāvalayotkaṭāni
tāny uttamāṅgāny abhito vibhānti
prabhātasūryāṃśusamaprabhāṇi
kṣipadbhir ugrajvalitānalopamair
mahāstrapūgaiḥ sa samāvṛto babhau
girir yathā saṃtatavarṣibhir ghanaiḥ
kṛtāndhakāro 'dbhutakandaradrumaḥ
tair hanyamāno 'pi mahāstrajālair
mahābalair daityagaṇaiḥ sametaiḥ
nākampatājau bhagavān pratāpavān
sthitaḥ prakṛtyā himavān ivācalaḥ
saṃtāpitāste narasiṃharūpiṇā
diteḥ sutāḥ pāvakadīptatejasaḥ
bhayād viceluḥ pavanoddhutā yathā
mahormayaḥ sāgaravārisaṃbhavāḥ
śatair dhanurbhiḥ sumahātivegato
yugāntakālapratimāñ śaraughān
ekāyanasthe mumucur nṛsiṃhe
mahāsurāḥ krodhavidīpitākṣāḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
kharāḥ kharamukhāś caiva makarāśīviṣānanāḥ
īhāmṛgamukhāś cānye varāhamukhasaṃsthitāḥ
bālasūryamukhāś caiva dhūmaketumukhās tathā
candrārdhacandravaktrāś ca dīptāgnipramukhās tathā
haṃsakukkuṭavaktrāś ca vyāditāsyā bhayāvahāḥ
pañcāsyā lelihānāś ca kākagṛdhramukhās tathā
vidyujjihvāstriśīrṣāś ca tatholkāmukhasaṃsthitāḥ
mahāgrahanibhāś cānye dānavā baladarpitāḥ
kailāsavapuṣas tasya śarīre śaravṛṣṭayaḥ
avadhyasya mṛgendrasya na vyathāṃ cakrur āhave
evaṃ bhūyo 'parān ghorān asṛjan dānavāḥ śarān
mṛgendrasyorasi kruddhā niḥśvasanta ivoragāḥ
te dānavaśarā ghorā mṛgendrāya samīritāḥ
vilayaṃ jagmur ākāśe khadyotā iva parvate
tataś cakrāṇi divyāni daityāḥ krodhasamanvitāḥ
mṛgendrāya kṣipanty āśu prajvalantīva sarvaśaḥ
tair āsīd gaganaṃ cakraiḥ saṃpatadbhiḥ samāvṛtam
yugānte saṃprakāśadbhiś candrasūryagrahair iva
tāni cakrāṇi vadanaṃ praviśanti vibhānti vai
meghodaradarīṃ ghorāṃ candrasūryagrahāv iva
tāni cakrāṇi sarvāṇi mṛgendreṇa mahātmanā
nigīrṇāni pradīptāni pāvakārciḥsamāni vai
hiraṇyakaśipur daityo bhūyaḥ prāsṛjad ūrjitām
śaktiṃ prajvalitāṃ ghorāṃ hutāśanataḍitprabhām
tām āpatantīṃ saṃprekṣya mṛgendraḥ śaktim uttamām
huṃkāreṇaiva raudreṇa babhañja bhagavāṃs tadā
rarāja bhagnā sā śaktir mṛgendreṇa mahīṃ tale
savisphuliṅgā jvalitā maholkeva nabhaścyutā
nārācapaṅktiḥ siṃhasya sṛṣṭā reje vidūrataḥ
nīlotpalapalāśānāṃ mālevojjvaladarśanā
garjitvā tu yathākāmaṃ vikramya ca yathāsukham
tat sainyam utsāritavāṃs tṛṇāgrāṇīva mārutaḥ
tato 'śmavarṣaṃ daityendrā vyasṛjanta nabhogatāḥ
nagamātraiḥ śilākhaṇḍair girikūṭair mahāprabhaiḥ
tad aśmavarṣaṃ siṃhasya gātre nipatitaṃ mahat
diśo daśa prakīrṇaṃ hi khadyotaprakaro yathā
tamaśmaughair ditisutās tadā siṃham ariṃdamam
prācchādayan yathā meghā dhārābhir iva parvatam
na ca taṃ cālayām āsur daityaughā devam āsthitam
bhīmavegā balaśreṣṭhaṃ samudra iva mandaram
tato 'śmavarṣe nihate jalavarṣam anantaram
dhārābhir akṣamātrābhiḥ prādur āsīt samantataḥ
nabhasaḥ pracyutā dhārās tigmavegāḥ sahasraśaḥ
āvṛṇvan sarvato vyoma diśaś copadiśas tathā
dhārāṇāṃ saṃnipātena vāyor visphūrjitena ca
vardhatā caiva varṣeṇa na prājñāyata kiṃcana
dhārā divi ca saṃsaktā vasudhāyāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
na spṛśanti sma taṃ tatra nipatantyo 'niśaṃ bhuvi
bāhyato vavṛśe varṣaṃ nopariṣṭāt tu vṛṣṭavān
mṛgendrapratirūpasya sthitasya yudhi māyayā
hate 'śmavarṣe tumule jalavarṣe ca śoṣite
sasṛjur dānavā māyām agniṃ vāyuṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
nabhasaḥ pracyutaś caiva tigmavegaḥ samantataḥ
jvālāmālī mahāraudro dīptatejāḥ samantataḥ
sa sṛṣṭaḥ pāvakas tena daityendreṇa mahātmanā
na śaśāka mahātejā dagdhum apratimaujasam
tam indras toyadaiḥ sārdhaṃ sahasrākṣo 'mitadyutiḥ
mahatā toyavarṣeṇa śamayām āsa pāvakam
tasyāṃ pratihatāyāṃ tu māyāyāṃ yudhi dānavāḥ
sasṛjur ghorasaṃkāśaṃ tamas tīvraṃ samantataḥ
tamasā saṃvṛte loke daityeṣv āttāyudheṣu vai
svatejasā parivṛto divākara ivābabhau
triśikhāṃ bhrukuṭīṃ cāsya dadṛśur dānavā raṇe
lalāṭasthāṃ trikūṭasthāṃ gaṅgāṃ tripathagām iva
vaisaṃpāyana uvāca
tataḥ sarvāsu māyāsu hatāsu ditinandanāḥ
hiraṇyakaśipuṃ daityā viṣaṇṇāḥ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ
tataḥ prajvalitaḥ krodhāt pradahann iva tejasā
hiraṇyakaśipur daityaś cālayām āsa medinīm
tataḥ prakṣubhitāḥ sarve sāgarāḥ salilākarāḥ
calitā girayaḥ sarve sakānanavanadrumāḥ
tasmin kruddhe tu daityendre tamobhūtam abhūj jagat
tamasā samavacchannaṃ na prājñāyata kiṃcana
āvahaḥ pravahaś caiva vivahaś ca samīraṇaḥ
parāvahaḥ saṃvahaś ca udvahaś ca mahābalaḥ
tathā parivahaḥ śrīmān mārutā bhayaśaṃsinaḥ
ity ete kṣubhitāḥ sapta mārutā gaganecarāḥ
ye grahāḥ sarvalokasya kṣaye prādur bhavanti vai
te grahā gagane hṛṣṭā vicaranti yathāsukham
ayogataś cacārāśu sarveṣv ṛkṣeṣu candramāḥ
sagrahaṃ sahanakṣatraṃ prajajvāla nabho niśi
vivarṇatvaṃ ca bhagavān gato divi divākaraḥ
kṛṣṇaḥ kabandhaś ca mahāṃl lakṣyate sma nabhastale
amuñcac cāsitāṃ sūryo dhūmavartiṃ mahābhayām
gaganasthaś ca bhagavān abhīkṣṇaṃ pariviṣyate
sapta dhūmanibhā ghorāḥ sūryā divi samutthitāḥ
somasya gaganasthasya grahās tiṣṭhanti śṛṅgagāḥ
vāme ca dakṣiṇe caiva sthitau śukrabṛhaspatī
śanaiś caro lohitāṅgo lohitārkasamadyutiḥ
samaṃ samabhirohanti durgāṇi gaganecarāḥ
śṛṅgāṇi śanakair ghorā yugāntāvartakā grahāḥ
candramāḥ saha nakṣatrair grahaiḥ saptabhir āvṛtaḥ
carācaravināśāya rohiṇīṃ nābhyanandata
gṛhīto rāhuṇā candra ulkābhir abhihanyate
ulkāḥ prajvalitāś candre pracelur ghoradarśanāḥ
devānām api yo devaḥ so 'py avarṣata śoṇitam
apatad gadganād ulkā vidyudrūpāśanisvanā
akāle ca drumāḥ sarve puṣpitāś ca phalanti ca
latāś ca saphalāḥ sarvā yāḥ prādur daityanāśanam
phale phalāny ajāyanta puṣpe puṣpaṃ tathaiva ca
unmīlanti nimīlanti hasanti ca rudanti ca
vikrośanti ca gambhīraṃ dhūmāyanti jvalanti ca
pratimāḥ sarvadevānāṃ kathayanti yugakṣayam
āraṇyaiḥ saha saṃsṛṣṭā grāmyāś ca mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
cukruśur bhairavaṃ tatra mṛgendre samupasthite
nadyaś ca pratilomāni vahanti kaluṣodakāḥ
na prakāśanti ca diśo raktareṇusamākulāḥ
vānaspatyā na pūjyante pūjanārhāḥ kathaṃcana
vāyuvegena hanyante bhidyante praṇudanti ca
tadā ca sarvabhūtānāṃ chāyā na parivartate
aparāhṇagate sūrye lokānāṃ ca yugakṣaye
tadā hiraṇyakaśipor daityasyopari veśmanaḥ
bhāṇḍāgārāyudhāgāre niviṣṭam abhavan madhu
śukra uvāca
asurāṇāṃ vināśāya surāṇāṃ vijayāya ca
dṛśyante vividhotpātā ghorā ghoranidarśanāḥ
ete cānye ca bahavo ghorā hy utpātadarśanāḥ
daityendrāṇāṃ vināśāya dṛśyante kalanirmitāḥ
tato hiraṇyakaśipur gadām ādāya satvaram
abhyadravata vegena dharaṇīm anukampayan
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityaḥ padā saṃghṛṣṭavān mahīm
saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭaḥ krodhād varāha iva mūrchitaḥ
medinyāṃ kampamānāyāṃ daityendreṇa mahātmanā
mahīdharebhyo nāgendrā niṣpetur bhayaviklavāḥ
viṣajvālākulair vaktrair vimuñcanto hutāśanam
catuḥśīrṣāḥ pañcaśīrṣāḥ saptaśīrṣāś ca pannagāḥ
vāsukis takṣakaś caiva karkoṭakadhanaṃjayau
elāpatraḥ kāliyaś ca mahāpadmaś ca vīryavān
sahasraśīrṣadhṛṅ nāgo hematāladhvajaḥ prabhuḥ
śeṣo 'nanto mahīpālo duṣprakampaḥ prakampitāḥ
dīptāny antarjalasthāni pṛthivīdharaṇāni ca
tadā kruddhena daityena kampitāni samantataḥ
āpaś ca sahasā kruddhā duṣprakampyarasāḥ śubhāḥ
nadī bhāgīrathī caiva sarayūḥ kauśikī tathā
yamunā caiva kāverī kṛṣṇā veṇṇā tathaiva ca
suveṇṇā ca mahābhāgā nadī godāvarī tathā
carmaṇvatī ca sindhuś ca tathā nadanadīpatiḥ
mekalaprabhavaś caiva śoṇo maṇinibhodakaḥ
susrotā narmadā caiva tathā vetravatī nadī
gomatī gokulākīrṇā tathā pūrvā sarasvatī
mahī kālanadī caiva tamasā puṣpavāhinī
jambūdvīpaṃ ratnavantaṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitam
survaṇakūṭakaṃ caiva suvarṇākaramaṇḍitam
mahānadaś ca lauhityaḥ śailakānanaśobhitaḥ
pattanaṃ kośakārāṇāṃ drumilaṃ rajatākaram
māgadhāṃś ca mahāgrāmān puṇḍrān vaṅgāṃs tathaiva ca
suhmān mallān videhāṃś ca mālavān kāśikosalān
bhavanaṃ vainateyasya suparṇasya ca kampitam
kailāsaśikharākāraṃ yat kṛtaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
raktatoyo bhīmavego lohito nāma sāgaraḥ
śubhaḥ pāṇḍurameghābhaḥ kṣīrodaś caiva sāgaraḥ
udayaś caiva śailendra ucchritaḥ śatayojanaḥ
suvarṇavedikaḥ śrīmān nāgapakṣiniṣevitaḥ
bhrājamāno 'rkasadṛśair jātarūpamayair drumaiḥ
sālais tālais tamālaiś ca karṇikāraiś ca puṣpitaiḥ
ayomukhaś ca vipulaḥ parvato dhātumaṇḍitaḥ
tamālavanagandhaś ca parvato malayaḥ śubhaḥ
surāṣṭrāś ca subāhlīkāḥ śūrābhīrās tathaiva ca
bhojāḥ pāṇḍyāś ca vaṅgāś ca kaliṅgās tāmraliptakāḥ
tathaivāndhrāś ca pauṇḍrāś ca vāmacūḍāḥ sakeralāḥ
kṣobhitās tena daityena sadevāḥ sāpsarogaṇāḥ
agastyabhavanaṃ caiva yad agastyakṛtaṃ purā
siddhacāraṇasaṃghaiś ca sevitaṃ sumanoharam
vicitranānāvihagaṃ supuṣpitalatādrumam
jātarūpamayaiḥ śṛṅgair apsarogaṇasevitam
giriḥ puṣpitakaś caiva lakṣmīvān priyadarśanaḥ
utthitaḥ sāgaraṃ bhittvā vayasyaś candrasūryayoḥ
rarāja sumahāśṛṅgair gaganaṃ vilikhann iva
candrasūryāṃśusaṃkāśaiḥ sāgarāmbusamāvṛtaḥ
vidyutvān parvataḥ śrīmān āyataḥ śatayojanam
vidyutāṃ yatra saṃpātā nipātyante nagottame
ṛṣabhaḥ parvataś caiva śrīmān vṛṣabhasaṃsthitaḥ
kuñjaraḥ parvataś caiva yatrāgastyagṛhaṃ mahat
viśālarathyā durdharṣā sarpāṇām ālayā purī
teṣāṃ bhogavatī cāpi daityendreṇābhikampitā
mahāmegho giriś caiva pāriyātraś ca parvataḥ
cakravāṃś ca giriśreṣṭho vārāhaś caiva parvataḥ
prāgjyotiṣapuraṃ caiva jātarūpamayaṃ śubham
yasmin vasati duṣṭātmā narako nāma dānavaḥ
meghaś ca parvataśreṣṭho meghagambhīranisvanaḥ
ṣaṣṭis tatra sahasrāṇi parvatānāṃ viśāṃ pate
taruṇādityasaṃkāśo meruś caiva mahāgiriḥ
devāvāsaḥ śubhaḥ puṇyo girirājo hiraṇmayaḥ
hemaśṛṅgo mahāśailas tathā meghasakho giriḥ
kailāsaś cāpi śailendro dānavendreṇa kampitaḥ
yakṣarākṣasagandharvair nityaṃ sevitakaṃdaraḥ
śrīmān manoharaś caiva nityaṃ puṣpitapādapaḥ
hemapuṣkarasaṃchannaṃ tena vaikhānasaṃ saraḥ
kampitaṃ mānasaṃ caiva rājahaṃsair niṣevitam
triśṛṅgaparvataś caiva kumārī ca saridvarā
tuṣāracayasaṃkāśo mandaraś caiva parvataḥ
uśīrabījaś ca girī rudropasthas tathādrirāṭ
prajāpateś ca nilayas tathā puṣkaraparvataḥ
devāvṛtparvataś caiva tathā caivāluko giriḥ
krauñcaḥ saptarṣiśailaś ca dhūmavarṇaś ca parvataḥ
ete cānye ca girayo deśā janapadās tathā
nadyaś ca sāgarāś caiva dānavendreṇa kampitāḥ
kapilaś ca mahīputro vyāghrākṣaś caiva kampitaḥ
khecarāś ca niśāputrāḥ pātālatalavāsinaḥ
gaṇas tathāparo raudro meghanādāṅkuśāyudhaḥ
ūrdhvago bhīmavegaś ca sarva evābhikampitāḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tatrādityāś ca sādhyāś ca viśve ca marutas tathā
rudrā devā mahātmāno vasavaś ca mahābalāḥ
āgamya te mṛgendrasya sakāśaṃ sūryavarcasaḥ
ūcuḥ saṃtrastamanaso devalokakṣayārditāḥ
jahi deva diteḥ putraṃ dānavaṃ lokanāśanam
durvṛttam asadācāraṃ saha sarvair mahāsuraiḥ
tvaṃ hy eṣām antako nānyo daityānāṃ daityanāśanaḥ
tan nāśaya hitārthāya lokānāṃ svasti vai kuru
tvaṃ guruḥ sarvalokānāṃ tvam indras tvaṃ pitāmahaḥ
ṛte tvadanyaḥ śaraṇaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati
tac chrutvā vacanaṃ devo devānām ādisaṃbhavaḥ
nanāda sumahānādam atigambhīranisvanaḥ
pāṭitāny asurendrāṇāṃ mṛgendreṇa mahātmanā
siṃhanādena mahatā hṛdayāni manāṃsi ca
gaṇaḥ krodhavaśo nāma kālakeyas tathāparaḥ
vegaś ca vegaleyaś ca saiṃhikeyaś ca vīryavān
saṃhṛādīyo mahānādī mahāvegas tathāparaḥ
kapilaś ca mahīputro vyāghrākṣaḥ kṣitikampanaḥ
khecarāś ca niśāputrāḥ pātālatalacāriṇaḥ
gaṇas tathāparo raudro meghanādo 'ṅkuśāyudhaḥ
ūrdhvago bhīmavegaś ca bhīmakarmārkalocanaḥ
vajrī śūlī karālaś ca hiraṇyakaśipus tataḥ
jīmūtaghanasaṃkāśo jīmūtaghanavegavān
jīmūtaghananirghoṣo jīmūtasadṛśadyutiḥ
devārir ditijo dṛpto nṛsiṃhaṃ samupādravat
samutpatya tatas tīkṣṇair mṛgendreṇa mahānakhaiḥ
tatroṃkārasahāyena vidārya nihato yudhi
mahī ca lokaś ca śasī nabhaś ca
grahāś ca sūryaś ca diśaś ca sarvāḥ
nadyaś ca śailāś ca mahārṇavāś ca
gatāḥ prakāśaṃ ditiputranāśāt
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tataḥ pramuditā devā ṛṣayaś ca tapodhanāḥ
tuṣṭuvur vidhaiḥ stotrair ādidevaṃ sanātanam
yat tvayā vihitaṃ deva nārasiṃham idaṃ vapuḥ
etad evārcayiṣyanti parāvaravido janāḥ
mṛgendratvaṃ ca lokeṣu sarvasattveṣu vā vibho
gāsyanti tvāṃ ca munayo mṛgendra iti nityaśaḥ
tvatprasādāt svakaṃ sthānaṃ pratipannāḥ sma vai vibho
evam ukto devasaṃghair narasiṃho mahāmanāḥ
brahmā ca paramaprīto viṣṇoḥ stotram udairayat
bhavān akṣaram avyaktam acintyaṃ guhyam uttamam
kūṭastham akṛtaṃ kartṛ sanātanam anāmayam
sāṃkhye yoge ca yā buddhis tattvārthapariniṣṭitā
bhagavān deva vidyātmā puruṣaḥ śāśvato dhruvaḥ
tvaṃ vyaktaś ca tathāvyaktas tvattaḥ sarvam idaṃ jagat
bhavan mayā vayaṃ devā bhavān ātmā bhavān prabhuḥ
caturvibhaktamūrtis tvaṃ sarvalokavibhur guruḥ
caturyugasahasreśaḥ sarvalokāntakāntakaḥ
pratiṣṭhā sarvabhūtānām anantabalapauruṣaḥ
kapilaprabhṛtīnāṃ ca yatīnāṃ paramā gatiḥ
anādimadhyanidhanaḥ sarvātmā puruṣottamaḥ
sraṣṭā tvaṃ tvaṃ ca saṃhartā tvam eko lokabhāvanaḥ
bhavān brahmā ca rudraś ca mahendro varuṇo yamaḥ
bhavān kartā vikartā ca lokānāṃ prabhavo 'vyayaḥ
parāṃ ca siddhiṃ paramaṃ ca devaṃ
paraṃ ca mantraṃ paramaṃ tapaś ca
paraṃ ca dharmaṃ paramaṃ yaśaś ca
tvām āhur agryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam
paraṃ ca satyaṃ paramaṃ haviś ca
paraṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ ca mārgam
paraṃ ca yajñaṃ paramaṃ ca hotraṃ
tvām āhur agryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam
paraṃ śarīraṃ paramaṃ ca dhāma
paraṃ ca yogaṃ paramām ca vāṇīm
paraṃ rahasyaṃ paramām gatiṃ ca
tvām āhur agryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam
paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ padaṃ yat
paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ ca devam
paraṃ parasyāpi param prabhuṃ ca
tvām āhur agryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam
paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ pradhānaṃ
paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ ca tattvam
paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ ca dhātṛ
tvām āhur agryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam
paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ rahasyaṃ
paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ paraṃ yat
param parasyāpi paraṃ tapo yat
tvām āhur agryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam
paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ parāyaṇaṃ
paraṃ ca guhyaṃ paramaṃ ca mantram
pareṇa yogena paraṃ suguptaṃ
tvām āhur agryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
evam uktvā tu bhagavān sarvalokapitāmahaḥ
stutvā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ brahmalokaṃ gataḥ prabhuḥ
tato nadatsu tūryeṣu nṛtyantīṣv apsaraḥsu ca
kśīrodasyottaraṃ kūlaṃ jagāma prabhur īśvaraḥ
nārasiṃhīṃ tanum tyaktvā sthāpayitvā ca tad vapuḥ
paurāṇaṃ rūpam āsthāya yayau sa garuḍadhvajaḥ
aṣṭacakreṇa yānena bhūtiyuktena śobhinā
avyaktaprakṛtir devaḥ svasthānam agamat prabhuḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
nārasiṃho mayā prokto vāmanaṃ śṛṇvataḥ param
janamejaya uvāca
yatra vāmanam āsthāya rūpaṃ rūpavatāṃ varaḥ
baler balavato yajñe balinā viṣṇunā purā
vikramais tribhir ākramya trailokyam akhilaṃ hṛtam
samudravasanā corvī nānānagavibhūṣitā
hṛtvā dattā surendrāya śakrāya prabhaviṣṇunā
janamejaya uvāca
atra me saṃśayo brahmann atra me vismayo mahān
kathaṃ nārāyaṇo devo vāmanatvam upāgataḥ
yaḥ purāṇe purāṇātmā bhūtvā nārāyano vibhuḥ
padmanābho mahāyogī lokānāṃ prakṛtir vibhuḥ
anādimadhyanidhanas trailokyādiḥ sanātanaḥ
havyakavyavahaḥ śrīmān havyakavyabhug avyayaḥ
adityā devamātuś ca kathaṃ garbhe 'bhavat prabhuḥ
sraṣṭā yo vāsavasyāpi sa kathaṃ vāsavānujaḥ
prasūto divi deveśo viṣṇutvaṃ prāptavān katham
etad ācakṣva me vipra prādurbhāvaṃ mahātmanaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
śṛṇu rājan kathāṃ divyām arcitām ṛṣipuṃgavaiḥ
purāṇaiḥ kavibhiḥ proktāṃ brahmoktāṃ brahmaṇeritām
mārīcasya sureśasya kaśyapasya prajāpateḥ
aditir ditir dve bhārye bhaginyau janamejaya
adityāṃ jajñire devāḥ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ
dhātāryamā ca mitraś ca varuṇo 'ṃśo bhagas tathā
indro vivasvān pūṣā ca parjanyo daśamas tathā
tathaikādaśamas tvaṣṭā dvādaśo viṣṇur ucyate
dityāṃ jāto hi bhagavān hiraṇyakaśipuḥ prabhuḥ
tasyānujaś ca daityendro hiraṇyākṣo mahābalaḥ
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāḥ pañca ghoraparākramāḥ
prahrādaś cānuhrādaś ca jambhaḥ saṃhrāda eva ca
virocanas tu prāhrādis tasya putro baliḥ smṛtaḥ
putrapautraṃ ca balavat teṣām akṣayam avyayam
tejasvināṃ surārīṇāṃ daityendrāṇāṃ manasvinām
gaṇāḥ subahuśo rājan deśe deśe sahasraśaḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nārasiṃhena hiraṇyakaśipuṃ hatam
daityā devavadhārthāya balim indraṃ pracakrire
dṛṣṭvā dharmaparaṃ nityaṃ satyavākyaṃ jitendriyam
śauryādhyayanasaṃpannaṃ sarvajñānaviśāradam
parāvaragṛhītārthaṃ tattvadarśinam avyayam
tejasvinaṃ suraripuṃ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ yathā
abhiṣekeṇa divyena baliṃ vairocaniṃ tadā
daityādhipatye ditijās tadā sarve nyayojayan
abhiṣiktas tu daityais tair balir balivatāṃ varaḥ
brahmaṇā caiva tuṣṭena hiraṇyakaśipoḥ pade
abhiṣikto 'suragaṇair balir vairocanis tathā
kāñcanaiḥ kalaśaiḥ sphītaiḥ sarvatīrthāmbusaṃbhṛtaiḥ
jayaśabdaṃ tataś cakrur abhiṣiktasya dānavāḥ
baler atulavīryasya siṃhāsanagatasya vai
kṛtvendraṃ dānavāḥ sarve baliṃ balavatāṃ varam
tato vijñāpayām āsuḥ śirobhiḥ patitāḥ kṣitau
viditaṃ tava daityendra hiraṇyakaśipor yathā
trailokyam āsīd akhilaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam
pitāmahaṃ tu hatvā te suraiḥ suraniṣūdana
hṛtaṃ tad eva trailokyaṃ śakraś caivābhiṣecitaḥ
tat pitāmaharājyaṃ svaṃ pratyāhartum ihārhasi
asmābhiḥ sahito nātha trailokyam idam avyayam
pratyānayasva bhadraṃ te rājyaṃ paitāmahaṃ vibho
asuragaṇasahasrasaṃvṛtas tvaṃ
jaya divi devagaṇān sahānujas tvam
amitabalaparākramo 'si rājann
atiśayase svaguṇaiḥ pitāmahaṃ svam
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
niśamya teṣāṃ vacanaṃ mahāmatir
balis tadā prītamanā mahābalaḥ
ājñāpayām āsa sa daityakoṭīs
trailokyam adyaiva jayāma sarvam
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā baler vairocanasya tu
udyogaṃ paramaṃ cakrur dānavā yuddhadurmadāḥ
mahāpadmo nikumbhaś ca kumbhakarṇaś ca vīryavān
kāñcanākṣaḥ kapiskandho mainākaḥ kṣitikampanaḥ
sitakeśordhvavastraś ca vajranābhaḥ śikhī jaṭī
sahasrabahur vikaco vyāghrākṣaḥ priyadarśanaḥ
ekākṣa ekapānmuṇḍo vidyudakṣaś caturbhujaḥ
gajodaro gajaśirā gajaskandho gajekṣaṇaḥ
aṣṭadaṃṣṭraś caturvaktro meghanādī jalaṃdhamaḥ
karālo jvālajihvaś ca śatāṅgaḥ śatalocanaḥ
sahasrapāt kṛṣṇamukhaḥ kṛṣṇaś caiva mahāsuraḥ
raṇotkaṭo dānapatiḥ śailakampī kulākuliḥ
samudro rabhasaś caṇḍo dhūmraś caiva priyaṃkaraḥ
govrajo gokṣuro raudro godantaḥ svastiko dhruvaḥ
māṃsapo māmsabhakṣaś ca vegavān ketumāñ śiniḥ
pañkadigdhaśarīraś ca bṛhatkīrtir mahāhanuḥ
samaprabho vikumbhāṇḍo virūpākṣo harāharau
śvetaśīrṣaś candrahanuś candrahā candratāpanaḥ
vikṣaro dīrghabāhuś ca madyapo mārutāśanaḥ
kālakañjo mahākrodhaḥ sarabhaḥ śalabhaḥ krathaḥ
samudramathano nādī vitataś ca mahābalaḥ
pralambo narako vālī dhenukaḥ kālalocanaḥ
variṣṭhaś ca gaviṣṭhaś ca bhūtalonmathano vibhuḥ
duṣprasādaḥ kirīṭī ca sūcīvaktro mahāsuraḥ
subāhuḥ kubjabāhuś ca karuṇaḥ kalaśodaraḥ
somapo devayājī ca pravaro vīramardanaḥ
śuśrūṣuḥ khaṇḍaśaktiś ca kuṇinetraḥ śaśidhvajaḥ
yathāsmṛti mayā proktā marīceḥ kīrtivardhanāḥ
ete cānye ca bahavo nānābhūśaṇabhūṣitāḥ
rathaughair bahusāhasrair yayur yoddhum ariṃdamāḥ
divyāmbaradharā daityā divyamālyānulepanāḥ
divyaiś ca kavacair naddhā divyaiś caivocchritair dhvajaiḥ
divyāyudhadharā daityā garjamānā yathāmbudāḥ
bhṛhadbhī rathanirghoṣaiś cālayanto vasuṃdharām
mahābalā divyabalāstradhāriṇo
bhujaṃgabhogapratimair mahābhujaiḥ
sudurjayā daityavṛṣāḥ surārayo
ditipriyā lohitalohitekṣaṇāḥ
te jagmur arkajvalanogravīryā
mahendravajrāśanitulyavegāḥ
vivṛddhadaṃṣṭrā haridhūmakeśā
vinardamānāḥ śaradīva meghāḥ
sahasrabāhur bāṇaś ca baleḥ putro mahāsuraḥ
rathātirathakoṭyāsau saṃnahyata mahābalaḥ
sarve māyādharā daityāḥ sarve divyās trayodhinaḥ
sarve madabalotsiktāḥ sarve labdhavarās tathā
sarve kañcanaśailābhāḥ pītakauśeyavāsasaḥ
kirīṭoṣṇīṣamukuṭā divyabhūṣaṇabhūṣitāḥ
hiraṇyakavacāḥ sarve hiraṇyadhvajaketavaḥ
syandanasthā vyarājanta śāradāḥ khe grahā iva
tāpanīyair varair niṣkair analajvalitaprabhaiḥ
hemaparvataśṛṅgasthāḥ puṣpitā iva kiṃśukāḥ
teṣāṃ madhyagato bāṇaḥ prāvṛṣīvotthito ghanaḥ
sthitaḥ śaktigadāpāṇis trinalvapratime rathe
citrākṣeṣādhvajayuge citrabhaktivirājite
gadāparighasaṃpūrne hemajālavibhūṣite
anvīyamāno ditijair vālakhilyair ivāṃśumān
nānāpraharaṇair ghorais tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrair ivoragaiḥ
pañca tasya mahāvīryā dānavā yuddhadurmadāḥ
rarakṣū ratham avyagrā vyāditāsyā bhayāvahāḥ
subāhur meghanādaś ca bhīmavegaś ca vīryavān
tathā gaganamūrdhā ca vegavān ketumān api
kanakarajatabhakticitrapārśve
patagapatipratime rathe sthito 'bhūt
jaladaninadatulyanemighoṣe
suragaṇasainyavadhāya dānavendraḥ
anāyuṣāyāḥ putras tu balo nāma mahāsuraḥ
vṛtaḥ śatasahasreṇa rathānāṃ bhīmavarcasām
yuktam ṛkṣasahasreṇa ratham āruhya vīryavān
nīlāyasamayaṃ ghoraṃ vāyasāṅkaṃ sudurjayam
nīlāmbaradharaḥ śrīmān vaiḍūryācalasaṃnibhaḥ
mahatā rathavṛndena prayayau dānavas tadā
tatraikārṇavasaṃkāśe sainyamadhye vyarājata
prabhātasamaye śrīmān samudrastha ivāṃśumān
sutaptajāmbūnadatulyavarcasā
niśākarākārataḍidguṇākaraḥ
kirīṭamukhyena vibhāti śobhinā
yathā giriḥ śṛṅgavareṇa bhāsvatā
ṣaṣtiṃ rathasahasrāṇi namucer asurasya vai
kharayuktāṇi sarvāṇi meghatulyaravāṇi ca
nānāpraharaṇāḥ sarve sarve te citrayodhinaḥ
mahābhraghanasaṃkāśā vegavanto mahābalāḥ
ratho vyāghrasahasreṇa yuktaḥ paramavegavān
namucer asurendrasya sarvaratnavibhūṣitaḥ
śārdūlacihnaḥ śuśubhe tasya ketur hiraṇmayaḥ
rathamadhye 'sureśasya madhyaṃdinaravir yathā
sa bhīmavegaś ca mahābalaś ca
pragṛhya cāpaṃ himavān iva sthitaḥ
nīlāmbaraḥ kāñcanapaṭṭanaddho
diśāgajo yadvad upetakakṣaḥ
kiṃkiṇījālanirghoṣaṃ tapanīyavibhūṣitam
sapatākadhvajopetaṃ sasaṃdhyam iva toyadam
cakraiś caturbhiḥ saṃyuktaṃ aṣṭanalvāyatāntaram
hemajālākulaṃ dīptaṃ kālacakram ivodyatam
nānāyudhadharaṃ divyaṃ vyāghracarmapariṣkṛtam
īhāmṛgagaṇākīrṇaṃ citrabhaktivirājitam
tūṇīraśatasaṃpūrṇaṃ śaktitomarasaṃkulam
gadāmudgarasaṃbādhaṃ dhanūratnavibūṣitam
yuktam ṛkṣasahasreṇa lambakesaravarcasā
rājatena vikīrṇena śobhitaṃ simhaketunā
sa tena śuśubhe daityo viśvakarmā mayo balī
ratharatne sthitaḥ śrīmān udayastha ivāṃśumān
himarajatasucāruśobhitāṅgaṃ
maṇikanakojjvalacārubhakticitram
ayutaśatasahasram ūrjitānām
ayam anuyāti mahāhave rathānām
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
pulomā tu mahādaityas timirākāragahvaraḥ
ārurohāyasaṃ ghoraṃ rathaṃ pararathārujam
utkīrṇaparvatākāraṃ lohajālāntarāntaram
nemighoṣeṇa mahatā kṣubhyantam iva sāgaram
gadāparighanistriṃsaiḥ satomaraparaśvadhaiḥ
śaktim udgarasaṃkīrṇaṃ satoyam iva toyadam
ratham uṣṭrasahasreṇa saṃyuktaṃ vāyuvegiṇā
pulomāruhya yuddhāya prasthito yuddhadurmadaḥ
ṣaṣṭiṃ rathasahasrāṇi pulomānaṃ mahāratham
anvayuḥ sūryavarṇāṇi pradīptānīva tejasā
khaḍgadhvajena mahatā taptakāñcanavarcasā
bhrājate rathamadhyasthaḥ parvatastha ivāṃśumān
sa cārucāmīkarapaṭṭanaddhāṃ
mahāgadāṃ kālanibhāṃ mahābalaḥ
pragṛhya babhrāja sa sainyamadhye
kārṣṇāyasaḥ ketur ivotthitorvyām
hayagrīvas tu balavān hayagrīvo mahābalaḥ
vṛtaḥ śatasahasreṇa rathānāṃ rathasattamaḥ
dharādharanibhākāraṃ sapatnānīkamardanam
syandanaṃ bhīmam āsthāya yuddhāyābhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ
śvetaśailapratīkāśaḥ śvetakuṇḍalabhūṣaṇaḥ
śuśubhe rathamadhyasthaḥ śvetaśṛṅga ivācalaḥ
mahatā saptaśīrṣeṇa śobhinā nāgaketunā
vaidūryamaṇicitrena pravālāṅkuraśobhinā
amitabalaparākramadyutīnām
vararathinām anujagmur ūrjitānām
asuragaṇaśatāṇi gacchamānaṃ
tridaśagaṇā iva vāsavaṃ prayāntam
prahrādas tu mahāprājñaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ
sarvamāyādharaḥ śrīmān yaṣṭā kratuśatair api
samanahyata tejasvī pāvakārciḥ samaprabhaḥ
rathānīkena mahatā durdināmbhodanādinā
śūreṇāmitavīryeṇa hemakuṇḍaladhāriṇā
vṛto daityasahasreṇa devair iva pitāmahaḥ
svavīryād agraṇīr dṛpto mattavāraṇavikramaḥ
surasainyasya sarvasya pratirodha iva sthitaḥ
sa dhairyeṇodadhes tulyo vapuṣāgnir iva jvalan
tejasā bhāskarākāraḥ kṣamayā pṛthivīsamaḥ
tāladhvajena dīptena rathenātivirājatā
taṃ yāntam anuyānti sma dānavāḥ śatasaṃghaśaḥ
sarve hiraṇyakavacāḥ sarve ratnavibhūṣitāḥ
divyāṅgarāgābharaṇāḥ samareṣv anivartinaḥ
jāmbūnadavicitrāṅgā vaidūryavikṛtāṅgadāḥ
divyasyandanamadhyasthāḥ khasthā iva mahāgrahāḥ
ācāravāṃś caiva jitendriyaś ca
dharme rataḥ satyaparo 'nasūyaḥ
sthito 'gnitoyāmbudavāyukalpo
rūpī yathā sarvaharaḥ kṛtāntaḥ
śambaras tu mahāmāyo daityānāṃ rathayūthapaḥ
āruroha rathaṃ divyaṃ sarvayuddhaviśāradaḥ
lohitākṣo mahābāhuḥ prataptottamakuṇḍalaḥ
jīmūtaghanasaṃkāśo divyasraganulepanaḥ
vidyuddyotanikāśena mukuṭenārkavarcasā
maṇiratnavicitreṇa vaidūryāntaraśobhinā
tāpanīyena mahatā kavacena virājatā
saṃdhyābhreṇeva saṃchannaḥ śrīmān astaśiloccayaḥ
triṃśacchatasahasrāṇi daityānāṃ citrayodhinām
balināṃ kālakalpānām anvayuḥ śambaraṃ tadā
yuktaṃ hayasahasreṇa śukavarṇena rājatā
krauñcadhvajena dīptena rathenāhavaśobhinā
vyāsaktavaidūryasuvarṇajālaṃ
nānāvihaṃgair api bhakticitram
vidyut prabhaṃ bhīmarathaṃ suvegaṃ
rathaṃ samāruhya rarāja daityaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
anuhrādas tu tatraiva daityaḥ paramadurjayaḥ
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putraḥ prayayau yuddhalālasaḥ
catuścakreṇa yānena trinalvapratimena tu
yuktenāśvair mahāvīryaiḥ siṃhavaktrair ajihmagaiḥ
bhīmagambhīranādena nemighoṣeṇa vīryavān
cālayan vasudhāṃ sarvāṃ saśailavanakānanām
vinardamānā daityaughā anuhrādaṃ yayuḥ śubhāḥ
śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ rathānāṃ hemamālinām
parighair bhiṇḍipālaiś ca bhallaiḥ prāsaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
vividhāyudhahastās te śūlamudgarapāṇayaḥ
suvarṇajālanirmuktair vajraiś ca samalaṃkṛtāḥ
rathaiś cakraiś ca kavacaiḥ sajjamānā mahāsurāḥ
tadā viśālocchritaśailarūpe
babhau rathe kāñcanacitritāṅge
daityādhipaḥ sarvabalānurūpe
samāsthitas tu apratime surūpe
virocanaś ca balavān vaiśvānarasamadyutiḥ
mahatā rathavaṃśena sarvāstrakuśalaḥ śuciḥ
vyūhānāṃ viniyogajño jñānavijñānatattvavit
baleḥ pitāsuravaraḥ surāṇām iva vāsavaḥ
sarvāyudhavaropetaṃ kiṃkiṇījālabhūṣitaṃ
yuktānāṃ vājimukhyānāṃ sahasreṇāśugāminām
ratham āruhya daityendro babhau merur ivāparaḥ
kiṃkiṇījālaparyantaṃ gajendradhvajaśobhitam
saṃdhyābhrasamavarṇābhiḥ patākābhir alaṃkṛtam
pravālajāmbūnadabhakticitraṃ
vyālaṃ vimuktāntaranemighoṣam
rathaṃ samāruhya kirīṭamālī
yayau sa yuddhāya mahāsurendraḥ
virocanānujaś caiva kujambho nāma dānavaḥ
syandanair bahusāhasrair maṇikāñcanabhūṣitaiḥ
vṛto madabalotsiktair devārir arimardanaḥ
prāsapāśagadāhastair dānavair yuddhakāṅkṣibhiḥ
sa parvatanibhākāro bhinnāñjanacayaprabhaḥ
mahatā bhrājamānena kirīṭena suvarcasā
sarvaratnavicitreṇa kavacena ca saṃvṛtaḥ
mahatā dīptavapuṣā rathenendur ivāṃśumān
śātakaumbhena mahatā tālavṛkṣeṇa ketunā
rarāja rathamadhyastho merustha iva bhāskaraḥ
asilomā ca tatraiva dānavaḥ parvatāyudhaḥ
dāruṇaṃ vapur āstāya dāruṇo dāruṇānanaḥ
raudraḥ śakaṭacakrākṣo mahāmāyo mahābalaḥ
kṛṣṇāvāsā mahādaṃṣṭro raktākṣo lohitānanaḥ
vṛto daityasahasraughair giripādapayodhibhiḥ
nānārūpadharair dīptair daityais tridaśaśatrubhiḥ
te śūlahastā gagane caranta
itas tatas toyadavṛndanādāḥ
khaṃ chādayantas tapanīyaniṣkā
yathotthitāḥ prāvṛṣi kālameghāḥ
anāyuṣāyāḥ putras tu vṛtro nāma mahāsuraḥ
devaśatrur mahākāyas tāmrāsyo nirṇatodaraḥ
dīptajihvo hariśmaśrur ūrdhvaromā mahāhanuḥ
nīlāṅgo lohitagrīvaḥ kirīṭī lohitāṅgadaḥ
ājānubāhur vikṛtaḥ śvetadaṃṣṭro vibhīṣaṇaḥ
mahāmāyo mahābhīmo hemakeyūrabhūṣaṇaḥ
mahatā maṇicitreṇa kavacena susaṃvṛtaḥ
hemamālādharo raudraś cakraketur amarṣaṇaḥ
kiṃkiṇīśatasaṃghuṣṭaṃ tapanīyavibhūṣitam
yuktaṃ hayasahasreṇa raktadhvajapatākinā
rathānīkena mahatā yuddhāyābhimukho yayau
divyaṃ syandanam āsthāya daityānāṃ nandivardhanaḥ
tapitakanakabindupiṅgalākṣo
dititanayo 'surasainyayuddhanetā
vikasitakamalābhacāruvaktraḥ
sitadaśanaḥ śuśubhe rathāsanasthaḥ
ekacakras tu tatraiva sūryacakra ivoditaḥ
kālacakrasamo raudraś cakrāyudha ivodyataḥ
sarvāyudhamayaṃ divyaṃ ratham āsthāya bhāsvaram
vṛto daityagaṇair dṛptaiḥ kālāyasaśilāyudhaiḥ
tasyāśītisahasrāṇi rathānāṃ citrayodhinām
sarve kālāntakaprakhyā rudhirākṣā mahābalāḥ
āyasaiḥ kāñcanaiś caiva saṃnaddhā varavarmiṇaḥ
vyarājantāntarikṣasthā nīlā iva payodharāḥ
sarve kālāntakaprakhyā vīrāḥ samaradurjayāḥ
sāgarodaragambhīrā nīlavaktrā durāsadāḥ
rejur yānto 'suravarā velātītā ivārṇavāḥ
te bhīmamāyāḥ susamṛddhakāyāḥ
kirīṭinaḥ kāñcanabhūṣitāṅgāḥ
yayus tadā svāyudhadīptahastā
nabhaḥ sapakṣā iva parvatendrāḥ
saṃdiṣṭo baliputreṇa vṛtrabhrātā mahāsuraḥ
vadhāya surasainyasya saṃnahyasveti vīryavān
hemamālī mahādaṃṣṭraḥ sragvī rucirakuṇḍalaḥ
raktamālyāmbaradharaś caṇḍaḥ samaradurjayaḥ
mahāvivṛttanayanaḥ sa kirīṭī dhanurdharaḥ
prabhinna iva mātaṅgaḥ śārdūlasamavikramaḥ
mahātālanibhaṃ cāpaṃ mahārucirasāyakam
visphārayan mahāvegaṃ vajraniṣpeṣanisvanam
rathena kharayuktena dhvajena bhujagena ca
śuśubhe syandanasthaḥ sa saṃdhyāgata ivāṃśumān
rathais tu bahusāhasrair hemapaṭṭavibhūṣitaiḥ
śūlamudgarasaṃpūrṇais toyapūrṇair ivāmbudaiḥ
sa daityendro 'bhicakrāma tasmin yuddha upasthite
pavanasamagatir viśālavakṣā
vikasitapaṅkajacārugarbhagauraḥ
pravararathagato yayau sa tūrṇaṃ
tridaśagaṇair abhilakṣitaprabhāvaḥ
siṃhikātanayaś caiva rāhur nāma mahāsuraḥ
vikaṭaḥ parvatākāraḥ śataśīrṣaḥ śatodaraḥ
pītamālyāmbaradharo jāmbūnadavibhūṣitaḥ
snigdhavaidūryasaṃkāśaḥ padmapatranibhekṣaṇaḥ
sarvakāñcanasaṃyuktaṃ maṇijālapariṣkṛtam
patākāśatasaṃkīrṇaṃ yuktaṃ paramavājibhiḥ
āruroha rathaṃ divyaṃ daityaḥ paramavīryavān
nanāda ca mahānādaṃ kampayan vasudhātalam
mayena vihito divyas tasya ketur hiraṇmayaḥ
mayūraṃ sūryasaṃkāśaṃ kavacaṃ cāyasaprabhaṃ
bhīmavegaravaiś cānyai rathair divyaiḥ subhāsuraiḥ
nānāpraharaṇākīrṇaiḥ sevyamāno mahābalaḥ
asuragaṇapatir gajendragāmī
gatir abhavat sugatir mahāsurāṇām
arigaṇam abhito vibhuḥ prayāto
girivaram astam ivāṃśumān prayātaḥ
vipracittis tu tatraiva danor vaṃśavivardhanaḥ
kaśyapasyātmajaḥ śrīmān brahmaṇas tejasā samaḥ
yaṣṭā kratusahasrāṇāṃ vedavit tapasānvitaḥ
svayaṃbhuvā dattavaro varadaś ca svayaṃprabhuḥ
īśitvaṃ ca vaśitvaṃ ca mahattvaṃ ca mahādyuteḥ
aiśvaryaguṇasaṃpanno brahmeva svayam urjitaḥ
sārdhaṃ putraiś ca pautraiś ca saṃnahyata mahābalaḥ
sarve māyādharāḥ śūrāḥ kṛtāstrā raṇadurjayāḥ
sarve kamalavarṇābhā hemakūṭocchrayocchritāḥ
sarve rajatasaṃkāśāḥ kailāsaśikharopamāḥ
mayena nirmitās teṣāṃ sarve māyāmayā rathāḥ
vicaranto vyarājanta śāradā iva toyadāḥ
sarve haṃsadhvajāḥ śvetāḥ śvetadaṇḍasamucchrayāḥ
śvetāmbaradharā daityāḥ śvetamālyavibhūṣitāḥ
śvetātapatrāḥ sarve te śvetakuṇḍalamaṇḍitāḥ
muktāhāravṛtoraskā bhānti nāgeśvarā iva
mahāgrahanibhākārāḥ śatrūṇāṃ lomaharṣaṇāḥ
raktacitrāmbaradharāś citrābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ
trailokyavijayaṃ nāma ratham āsthāya vīryavān
kailāsaśikharākāram aṣṭanalvāyatāntaram
yuktaṃ vājisahasreṇa sitena śaśivarcasā
patākāśatasaṃchannaṃ nānāyudhavikalpitam
haṃsāṃśukundapratimaṃ viśālaṃ
sitātapatraṃ danujeśvarasya
vibhāti tasyopari dhāryamāṇaṃ
śvetādrimūrdhāvagataḥ śaśāṅkaḥ
keśī dānavamukhyas tu jihmas tāmrākṣadarśanaḥ
nīlameghacayaprakhyaḥ kālaḥ puruṣavigrahaḥ
mahāgrahanibhākāraḥ śatrūnāṃ lomaharṣaṇaḥ
citramālyāmbaradharo raktābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
śatākṣaḥ śatabāhuś ca hariśmaśrur mahābalaḥ
śaṅkukarṇo mahānādo vapuṣā raudradarśanaḥ
yuktaṃ mahiṣakair divyair ghaṇṭākoṭikṛtasvanam
mahāvāridharākāram āsthāya ratham uttamam
dhvajenoṣṭreṇa mahatā nīlakesaravarcasā
nānārāgavicitrābhiḥ patākābhir vibūṣitam
dvipañcāśatsahasrāṇi rathānām ugratejasām
yayus tasyāsurendrasya prayātasya surān prati
bhānti bhinnāñjananibhāḥ prayātasya mahātmanaḥ
daṃṣṭrārdhacandravadanāḥ sabalākā ivāmbudāḥ
tat tasya vaidūryasuvarṇacitraṃ
vidyutprabhaṃ bhāskararaśmitulyam
kirīṭam ābhāty asurottamasya
dāvāgnidīptaṃ śikharaṃ yathādreḥ
vṛṣaparvāsuraś caiva śrīmān suraniṣūdanaḥ
āruroha rathaṃ divyaṃ meruśṛṅgam ivāṃśumān
pravālajāmbūnadacitrakūbaraṃ
mahārathaṃ bhārasahaṃ mahārham
svalaṃkṛtaṃ rājatahemamaṇḍalaṃ
gabhastinakṣatrataḍinnikāśam
keyūrayuktāṅgadanaddhabāhuḥ
sahasratāreṇa ca carmaṇā saḥ
sāṃgrāmikair ābharaṇaiś ca citrair
madhyāhnasūryapratimo babhūva
mahābalo baddhatalāṇgulitro
balotkaṭaḥ kiṃśukalohitākṣaḥ
pragṛhya cāmīkaracārucitraṃ
cāpaṃ sthito vṛttaviśālanetraḥ
mahāsurendraś ca mahāsurair vṛto
balis tadā syandanam āruroha
vaidūryahemopacitaṃ viśālaṃ
vidyutprabhaṃ ṣoḍaśanalvamātram
yuktaṃ sahasreṇa diteḥ sutānāṃ
gajānanānāṃ vikṛtānanānām
cāmīkaroraḥsthalabhūṣitānāṃ
pranardatāṃ prāvṛṣi cāmbudānām
mahārathaṃ devarathaprakāśaṃ
sahasramāyena mayena sṛṣṭam
īhāmṛgākrīḍitabhakticitraṃ
divyaṃ rathaṃ vīrarathānuyātam
sakiṃkiṇīkaṃ vimalaṃ suvistṛtaṃ
hiraṇmayaiḥ padmaśatair alaṃkṛtam
abhyādade vaijayantīṃ jayāya
srajaṃ balir hemavicitrapuṣpām
ābadhya mālāṃ prababhau vicitrāṃ
balis tadā bhāti bhujair viśālaiḥ
rarāja taiḥ sarvasamṛddhiyuktair
mahārciṣā sūrya ivāmbarasthaḥ
srajaṃ tadā badhyati cāsya durgāṃ
sarvāsurāṇām iva hārabhūtām
vairocaniḥ sarvaśriyābhijuṣṭo
vibhrājate 'sau śaradīva candraḥ
meros taṭaiḥ kāñcanarāgaraktair
ādityasaṃsaktam ivābhranīlam
prāsāś ca pāśāś ca hiraṇyanaddhāś
carmāṇi khaḍgāś ca paraśvadhāś ca
dhanūṃṣi vajrāyudhasaprabhāṇi
divyā gadā vajramukhāś ca śaktyaḥ
divyāś ca khaḍgā viśikhāś ca dīptā
nārācapūrṇā vividhāś ca tūṇāḥ
dhṛtā rathe daityavṛṣasya tasya
cakāśire prajvalitā yatholkāḥ
taṃ cāmarāpīḍadharāḥ sudaṃṣṭrāḥ
suvarṇamuktāmaṇihemacitrāḥ
vījanti vālavyajanair vinītāḥ
svalaṃkṛtāḥ syandanavedikāsthāḥ
ayaḥśirā aśvaśirā durāpaḥ
śibir mataṅgo vikaṭaḥ śatākṣaḥ
ajo nikumbhaḥ kupathaś ca dānavo
rarakṣur ete daśa dānavādhipam
puraḥsarāś caiva sahasraśo 'surāḥ
padātayo dānavarājarakṣiṇaḥ
śataghnicakrāśaniśaktipāṇayaḥ
prajagmur agre 'nilatulyaveginaḥ
ghaṇṭāsuśabdās tapanīyanaddhā
āḍambarā jharjharaḍiṇḍimāś ca
mahāravā dundubhayaś ca nedū
rathaprayāṇe ditijeśvarasya
tasyocchritaḥ kāñcanavedikāḍhyo
hiraṇmayo divyamahāpatākaḥ
mahādhvajo vai tapanīyanaddho
rarāja vīrasya yathā vivasvān
samucchritaṃ kāñcanamātapatraṃ
srakkāñcanī vakṣasi cāsya bhāti
samantataś cainam upācaranti
daityarṣayaḥ prāñjalayo yajanti
purohitāḥ śatruvadhe samāhitās
tathaiva cānye śrutaśīlavṛddhāḥ
japaiś ca mantraiś ca tathauṣadhībhir
mahātmanaḥ svastyayanaṃ pracakruḥ
sa tatra vastrāṇi śubhāś ca gāvaḥ
phalāni puṣpāṇi tathaiva niṣkān
balir daityo brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchan
virājate 'tīva yathā dhaneśaḥ
sahasrasūryo bahukiṃkiṇīkaḥ
parārdhyajāmbūnadahemacitraḥ
sahasracandrāyutatārakaś ca
ratho baler agnir ivāvabhāti
tam āsthito dānavasaṃgṛhītaṃ
mahābalaḥ kārmukadhṛksabāṇaḥ
udvartayiṣyaṃs tridaśendrasenām
atīva raudraṃ sa bibharti rūpam
sa vegavān vīrarathaughasaṃkulaḥ
prayāti devān prati daityasāgaraḥ
mahārṇavo vīcitaraṃgasaṃkulo
yathā jalaughair yugasaṃkṣaye tathā
trailokyavitrāsakarair vapurbhis
tāny agrato yānti bale rathasya
mahābalāny ucchritakārmukāṇi
saparvatānīva vanāni rājan
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
śrutas te daityasainyasya vistaro janamejaya
bhūyas tridaśasainyasya śṛṇu vistaram āditaḥ
surādhipas tu bhagavān ājñāpayata vai surān
marudgaṇāṃs tathādityān viśvedevāṃś ca vāsavaḥ
vasūnaṣṭau bhṛśaṃ sarvān yakṣarakṣomahoragān
vidyādharagaṇān sarvān gandharvāṃś ca mahābalān
mahārṇavāṃś ca śailāṃś ca tathā rudrān mahaujasaḥ
yamavaiśravaṇau cobhau varuṇaṃ ca jalādhipam
ye tu siddhā mahātmānaḥ pitaraś ca manasvinaḥ
rājarṣīṃś ca api śataśo yogasiddhāṃs tathaiva ca
tridaśājñāpakaḥ śakra ājñāpayati vīryavān
bhavanto daityanāśāya saṃnahyantām iti prabhuḥ
śakrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā tataḥ sarve divaukasaḥ
saṃnahyanta mahātmānaḥ śakrasya samavikramāḥ
nānākavacinaḥ sarve vicitrakavacadhvajāḥ
nānāyudhodyatakarā mattā iva mahāgajāḥ
kecid āruruhur vyāghrān kecid āruruhur gajān
kecid āruruhur nāgān kecid āruruhur vṛṣān
harinetro hariśmaśrur dviradairāvatadhvajam
rathaṃ harihayair yuktvā sa prāyāt samaraṃ prati
ādityavarṇaṃ virajaṃ sudhautaṃ
tvaṣṭrā svayaṃ nirmitam īśvarārtham
jālaiś ca jāmbūnadabhakticitrair
alaṃkṛtaṃ kāñcanadāmabhiś ca
sakūbaropaskaravandhureṣaṃ
vidyutprabhābhiḥ kṛtam ābhitāmram
kailāsaśṛṅgopamam indrayānaṃ
sucārucārupraticakracakram
tārāsahasrai rucirair jvaladbhir
devārdhamālyārcitasarvadeham
samucchritaśrīdhvajam akṣayākṣam
jājvalyamānaṃ vapuṣottamena
āsthāya taṃ bhāsvaram āśuvegaṃ
śacīpatir lokapatiḥ sureśaḥ
vajrasya bhartā bhuvanasya goptā
yayau mahātmā bhagavān mahendraḥ
āmucya varmātha sahasratāraṃ
hutāśanādityasamaprabhāvaṃ
sūryaprabhaṃ cāmumuce kirīṭaṃ
mālāṃ ca jāmbūnadavaijayantīm
tvaṣṭrā kṛtaṃ bhāsvararaśmidīptaṃ
sutīkṣṇaghorāmalatīkṣṇadhāram
mahāsurāṇāṃ rudhirārdram ugraṃ
pragṛhya vajraṃ śataparvamukhyam
mahāśanī dve ca mahāgrahābhe
dīptām amoghāṃ ca sa śaktim ugrām
cakraṃ tathaindraṃ sumahac ca cāpaṃ
pragṛhya śakraḥ prayayau raṇāya
sahasradṛgbhūtapatiḥ sanātanaḥ
sanātanānām api yaḥ sanātanaḥ
prayāti devādhipatir mahātmā
vaiyāghram ādāya ca carma citram
kṣīrodadhikṣobhasamutthitāni
purāmṛtād uttamabhūṣaṇāni
devāsurāṇāṃ śramanirjitāni
somārkanakṣatrataḍitprabhāṇi
dattāny adityā maṇikuṇḍalāni
yuddhaṃ prayātasya sureśvarasya
tair bhūṣito yāti sahasracakṣur
uddyotayan vai vidiśo diśaś ca
hariḥ prabhur netrasahasracitro
vibhāti yuddhābhimukhaḥ surendraḥ
yathā sitaṃ śāradam abhravṛndaṃ
nabhastalaṃ ṛkṣasahasracitram
stuvanti yāntaṃ vipulair vacobhir
jayāśiṣā corjitasattvavīryam
atrir vasiṣṭho jamadagnir aurvo
bṛhaspatir nāradaparvatau ca
samanvayur devagaṇā mahendraṃ
prayāntam ādityasamānavarcasam
viśve ca devā marutaś ca sarve
sādhyās tathā ādityagaṇāś ca sarve
te devarājasya puraṃdarasya
hayāś ca ye mātalisaṃgṛhītāḥ
prayānti deveśvaram udvahanto
nabhastalaṃ padbhir ivākṣipantaḥ
brahmarṣayaś caiva surarṣayaś ca
rājarṣayaś cākṣayapuṇyalokāḥ
sarve 'nujagmuḥ sahasā jvalantaṃ
tejonvitaṃ śakram amitrasāham
pragṛhya śūlāni paraśvadhāṃś ca
dīptāni cāpāny aśanīr vicitrāḥ
varmāṇi cāmucya hiraṇmayāni
prayānti sūryāṃśusamaprabhāṇi
tathā kubero 'śvasahasrayuktaṃ
śreṣṭhaṃ rathaṃ sarvasahaṃ mahārham
divyaṃ samāruhya raṇāya yāto
dhaneśvaro dīptagadāgrahastaḥ
niśācarāḥ pāvakadhūmrakāyā
rakṣovṛṣā rudrasakhasya tasya
viśālanānāyudhadīptahastā
yānty agrato vaiśravaṇasya rājñaḥ
te lohitākṣāḥ parivārya devaṃ
vrajanti bhinnāñjanacūrṇavarṇāḥ
yakṣottamā yakṣapatiṃ dhaneśaṃ
rakṣanti vai prāsagadāsihastāḥ
puṇyaḥ prabhuḥ prāṇapatir yatātmā
vaivasvato dharmabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
taḍidguṇābhaṃ śatavājiyuktaṃ
rathaṃ samārohata sūryakalpam
taṃ lokapālaṃ pitaro 'nujagmur
viviktapāpā jvalitā yaśobhiḥ
sarve ca bhūtā bhuvanapradhānā
nānāyudhavyagrakarāḥ subhīmāḥ
daṇḍaṃ mahāstraṃ parigṛhya devo
lokāṅkuśaṃ vigrahaniścitārthaṃ
hiraṇmayānāṃ kamalotpalānāṃ
mālāṃ manojñām avasajya kaṇṭhe
sthito 'sthimedāmiṣalohitārdraṃ
sarvāsurānāṃ nidhanaṃ vikāṅkṣan
tejomayaṃ mudgaram ugrarūpaṃ
vikarṣamāṇo 'ruṇadhūmranetraḥ
samanvito vyādhiśatair anekair
yayau hariśmaśrur udārasattvaḥ
mahāsurāṇāṃ nidhanāya buddhiṃ
cakre tadā vyādhipatiḥ kṛtāntaḥ
tatas triśīrṣair bhujagair bṛhadbhir
yuktaṃ rathaṃ hemacitaṃ mahātmā
āsthāya kundendunibhaṃ jaleśo
yayau raṇāyāsuradarpahantā
vaidūryamuktāmaṇibhūṣitāṅgas
tejomayaḥ pāśagṛhītahastaḥ
mahāsurāṇāṃ nidhanāya devaḥ
prayāti rūpyākaranaddhabāhuḥ
kailāsaśṛṅgapratimo 'prameyaḥ
samudranātho 'mṛtapo mahātmā
mahoragaiḥ svais tanayaiś ca gupto
yayau rathenārkasamaprabheṇa
yuddhāya taṃ yāntam adīnasattvaṃ
nabhastale candram ivātikāntam
paśyanti bhūtāni mahānubhāvaṃ
saṃhṛṣṭaromāṇi kṛtāñjalīni
dhātāryamāṃśo 'tha bhago vivasvān
parjanyamitrau ca śaśī ca devaḥ
tvaṣṭā tathaivorjitaviśvakarmā
pūṣā ca sākṣād iva devarājaḥ
soraśchadaiḥ sadhvajakiṃkiṇīkair
vaidūryaniṣkaiś citahemakaṇṭhaiḥ
hayair varaiḥ śakrahayaprakāśair
yuktān rathān āruruhuḥ surās te
divākarākāranibhāni kecid
dhutāśanārciḥpratimāni kecit
niśākarāṃśupratimāni kecit
taḍidguṇoddyotanibhāni kecit
nīlāṃśumeghapratimāni kecit
kārṣṇāyasākāranibhāni kecit
varmāṇi divyāni mahāprabhāṇi
tvaṣṭrā kṛtāny uttamabhānumanti
āmucya mālāś ca suvarṇapadmāḥ
prayānti toyānilatulyavegāḥ
dvāv aśvinau cāpi mahānubhāvau
rūpottamau dharmabhṛtāṃ variṣṭhau
rathaṃ samāruhya suvarṇacitraṃ
raṇaṃ gatau kāñcanatulyavarṇau
manoḥ sutā vai vasavaś ca sarve
balotkaṭā daityavadhāya devāḥ
rathāṃś ca nāgāṃś ca mahāpramāṇān
āsthāya jagmuḥ suśubhāstrahastāḥ
rudrāś ca sarve 'ruṇadhūmravarṇāḥ
śvetair yayur gopatibhir bṛhadbhiḥ
mahaujasaḥ sarvaguṇopapannā
dīptātmano bhābhir iva jvalantaḥ
nānāyudhavyagrakarair bhujais te
lokān samastān iva nirdahantaḥ
yayuḥ sasainyās tapanīyanaddhāḥ
savidyutas toyadharā yathaiva
viśve ca devās tapasā jvalanto
vīryottamāḥ sūryamarīcivarṇāḥ
yayuḥ sasainyā yudhi durnivāryā
balotkaṭāḥ padmasahasramālāḥ
rathaiḥ suyuktais tapanīyavarṇair
