vaidūryamuktāmaṇidāmacitraiḥ
nānāyudhākārasamākulās te
pāriplavaiś caiva sitātapatraiḥ
tejomayaiḥ kāñcanacārucitraiḥ
sunirmalaiḥ pāvakasaṃnibhais te
uraśchadaiḥ sadhvajakiṃkiṇīkair
hayaiś ca vāyoḥ samavegavadbhiḥ
diśāṃ gajaiś caiva mahābalais te
kailāsaśṛṅgapratimair mahadbhiḥ
prajagmur ugrāyudhadīptahastāś
caturyugānte jvalitā ivolkāḥ
sādhyāś ca devāḥ sumahāprabhāvāḥ
svādhīnacakrāḥ pratidīptavaktrāḥ
prayānti jāmbūnadabhūṣitāṅgā
gaṅgaughamārgair gagane balaughaiḥ
vidyotayanto vidiśo diśaś ca
mahābalās te jayatāṃ variṣṭhāḥ
variṣṭhapṛṣṭhauṣṭhabhujāḥ sudṛptā
vaiśvānarārkapratimaprabhāvāḥ
te brahmavidbhiś ca namasyamānāḥ
saṃpūjyamānāś ca suraiḥ saśakraiḥ
gandharvasaṃghair anugamyamānā
vadhāya teṣām asurādhipānām
vaidūryavajrasphaṭikāgracitrair
vastraiḥ suvarṇaiś ca pariṣkṛtānām
rūpaṃ babhūvotkaṭabhūṣaṇānām
daityendranāśāya vibhūṣitānām
ātmaprabhābhiś ca raṇotkaṭābhir
varmaprabhābhiś ca tamonudābhiḥ
vibhānti te devavarāḥ sasādhyāḥ
pradhmātaśaṅkhasvanasiṃhanādāḥ
mahārathasthās tridivaukasas te
mahābalāḥ śatrubalaṃ prayānti
mahāstrahastā yayur ugrarūpā
mahāsurāṇāṃ nidhanāya devāḥ
tathaiva sarve maruto 'tivīryā
balotkaṭāḥ khe samarapratītāḥ
yayur mahāmeghasamānavarṇā
bahvāyudhās toyadanādanādāḥ
mahendraketupratimā mahābalāḥ
pragṛhya sarvāsurasūdanāṃ gadām
raṇotkaṭā lohitacandanāktāḥ
sahemamālyāmbarabhūṣitāṅgāḥ
te yuddhaśauṇḍāḥ subhujāstravīryā
balotkaṭāḥ krodhavilohitākṣāḥ
yayuḥ sajāmbūnadapadmamālā
yatheṣṭanānāvidhakāmarūpāḥ
vaidūryacāmīkaracārurūpāṇy
ābadhya gātreṣu mahāprabhāṇi
varmāṇi daityāstranivāraṇāni
prayānti yuddhāya sapatnasāhāḥ
tair ucchritaiḥ kāñcanavedikāḍhyair
varadhvajair bhāskararaśmivarṇaiḥ
yayau surāṇāṃ pṛtanogratejāḥ
samunnadantī yudhi siṃhanādān
ity evam ugraṃ tridaśeśvarasya
sainyaṃ tad āsīt sumahāprabhāvam
yoddhuṃ prayātasya jayāvahasya
vadhāya teṣām asurādhipānām
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tataḥ pravṛtto 'suradevavigrahas
tadādbhuto bhāti surāsurākulaḥ
velām atikramya yugāntakāle
mahārṇavānyonyam ivāśrayantaḥ
nānāyudhoddyotavidīpitāṅgā
mahābalā vyāyatakārmukās te
madotkaṭā vāraṇahastahastāḥ
sudurjayās toyadanādanādāḥ
visphārayantaḥ sahasā dhanūṃṣi
cakrāṇi cādityasamaprabhāṇi
samutkṣipanto hy aśanīś ca ghorāḥ
khaḍgāṃś ca te vajramukhāś ca śaktīḥ
mahāgadāḥ kāñcanapaṭṭanaddhās
tathāyasān kārmukamudgarāṃś ca
śūlāṃś ca vṛkṣāṃś ca vigṛhya dīptān
nadanti śūrāḥ śataśo raṇasthāḥ
marutāṃ pañcamo yas tu sa bāṇenābhyayudhyata
mahābalaḥ suravaraḥ sāvitra iti yaṃ viduḥ
anāyuṣāyāḥ putras tu balo nāma mahāsuraḥ
so 'yudhyata raṇe 'tyugro dhruveṇa vasunā saha
namuciś cāsuraśreṣṭho dhareṇa samayudhyata
sārdhaṃ sarveṇa sainyena vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥ
viśvakarmā suraśreṣṭho mayena samayudhyata
pravarau viśvakarmānau khyātau devāsureśvarau
pulomā tu mahādaityo vāyunā samayudhyata
sasainyaḥ parvatākāro raṇe 'yudhyata daṃśitaḥ
hayagrīvas tu ditijaḥ saha pūṣṇā tv ayudhyata
śūreṇāmitavīryeṇa bhāskarākāravarcasā
śambaras tu mahāvīryo mahāmāyo mahāsuraḥ
bhagenāyudhyata tadā sahito yuddhadurmadaḥ
śarabhaḥ śalabhaś caiva daityānāṃ candrabhāskarau
prayuddhau saha somena śiśirāstreṇa dhīmatā
virocanas tu balavān baler balavataḥ pitā
viṣvaksenena sādhyena devena samayudhyata
kujambhas tu mahātejā hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ
aṃśenāyudhyata tadā prāsapraharaṇena vai
asilomā tu balinā mārutena samaṃ vibho
tadāyudhyata dīptāsyo vikṛtaḥ parvatāyudhaḥ
anāyuṣāyāḥ putras tu vṛtro nāma mahāsuraḥ
aśvibhyāṃ devavaidyābhyāṃ sahāyudhyata saṃyuge
ekacakras tu ditijaś cakrahasto durāsadaḥ
sahāyudhyata devena sādhyena ditijāriṇā
balas tu madhupiṅgākṣo vṛtrabhrātā mahāsuraḥ
mṛgavyādhena rudreṇa sahāyudhyata vīryavān
rāhus tu vikṛtākāraḥ śataśīrṣaḥ śatodaraḥ
ajaikapādena raṇe sahāyudhyata daṃśitaḥ
keśī tu dānavaśreṣṭhaḥ prāvṛṭkālāmbudaprabhaḥ
dhaneśvareṇa bhīmena sahāyudhyata saṃyuge
vṛṣaparvā tu balinā saha niṣkambhunā raṇe
viśvedevena viśveśaḥ sahāyudhyata vīryavān
prahrādas tu mahāvīryo vīraiḥ svais tanayair vṛtaḥ
yuyudhe saha kālena raṇe kāla iva sthitaḥ
anuhrādaḥ kubereṇa dhanadena mahāraṇe
gadāhastena yuyudhe kṣobhayan ripuvāhinīm
vipracittis tu daiteyo varuṇena mahātmanā
pravṛtto vai raṇaṃ kartuṃ daityānāṃ nandivardhanaḥ
balis tu saha śakreṇa sureśena mahātmanā
yuyudhe devarājena balinā balavān raṇe
śeṣā devāś ca daityāś ca jaghnur anyonyam āhave
vinadanto mahānādān prāsāsiśaraśaktibhiḥ
adṛśyanta mahotpātā ye proktā jagataḥ kṣaye
marutaḥ sapta te kṣubdhā vyaśīryanta mahīdharāḥ
sapta caivotthitāḥ sūryāḥ śoṣayanto mahārṇavān
bahudhābhidyata dharā vāyunā mathitā yathā
vyutthitāś ca mahāmeghāḥ śakracāpāṅkitodarāḥ
praṇeduḥ sarvabhūtāni sarvāḥ satimirā diśaḥ
devānām ajayo ghoro dṛśyate kālanirmitaḥ
na hy antarikṣaṃ na diśo na bhūmir
na bhāskaro 'dṛśyata reṇujālaiḥ
vavuś ca vātās tumulāḥ sadhūmā
diśaś ca sarvās timiropagūḍhāḥ
ete cānye ca bahavo dṛśyante devanirmitāḥ
bhūmau tathāntarikṣe ca ghorotpātāḥ samantataḥ
tad yuddhaṃ devadaityānāṃ bhīmānāṃ bhīmadarśanam
apaśyata gurur brahmā sarvair eva suraiḥ saha
vedaiś caturbhiḥ sāṅgaiś ca vidyābhiś ca sanātanaḥ
padmayonir vṛtaḥ śrīmān siddhaiś ca paramarṣibhiḥ
nānāmaṇistambhasahasracitram
āruhya yānaṃ dadṛśe svayaṃbhūḥ
subhāsvaraṃ bhūtasahasrayuktaṃ
pradīpyamānaṃ vapuṣā pareṇa
sutaptajāmbūnadacārucitram
ānandabherīśatasaṃpraṇādam
nakṣatracandrāṃśubhir aṃśumantaṃ
vaidūryasomārkavibhūṣitāṅgam
tam ātmajo vai pulahaḥ pulastyas
tathā marīcir bhṛgur aṅgirāś ca
ṛksāmabhiḥ samyag abhiṣṭuvantaḥ
sevanti devaṃ varadaṃ vimāne
taṃ pāvakā lokaguruṃ svayaṃbhuvaṃ
sāṅgāś ca vedā makhadevatāś ca
sevanti devaṃ bhuvaneśvareśaṃ
bhūtāni cānyāni mahānubhāvam
ete ca bhūyaś ca manuṣyasaṃghā
vaikhānasāḥ pāvakayonayaś ca
sarve yayur devapurohitāś ca
yuddhotsukāḥ sarvasurāsurāṇām
yogeśvarāḥ ṣaṭ ca divākarābhā
vāgbhūṣaṇair bhūṣitasarvadehāḥ
antarhitā vai dadṛśur nabhaḥsthā
nārāyaṇaś caiva naraś ca devaḥ
vaktraiś caturvedadharaiś caturbhiḥ
saṃpūrṇacandrapratimaiḥ sukāntaiḥ
sarvā diśo nistimirāś cakāra
navodito 'sau śaradīva candraḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
ubhayoḥ senayo rājaṃs tayor yuddham avartata
nādena saṃcālayatā trailokyam idam avyayam
gomukhāḍambarāṇāṃ ca bherīṇāṃ murajaiḥ saha
jharjharīḍiṇḍimāṇāṃ ca vyaśrūyanta mahāsvanāḥ
pravṛtto yuddhayajñas tu tumulo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
raṇabhūmau mahānādaḥ svargīyaḥ śūrasaṃmataḥ
sa yuddhayajñasya mukhe prahrādo daityasattamaḥ
virocanas tathādhvaryur yuddhayajñapravartakaḥ
hotā caivātra namucir vṛtraḥ stotropakalpakaḥ
mantrā daityāḥ samākhyātā yajñakarmaṇi tatra vai
anuyātaś ca pitaram adhiko vā parākrame
yaṣṭā tatrābhavad bāṇaḥ saṃyuge copatiṣṭhati
aindraṃ pāśupataṃ brāhmaṃ sthūṇākarṇaṃ sudurjayam
mantrās tatrābhyavartanta sādhvanuhrādayojitāḥ
udgātā ca mayaḥ śrīmān sthitaḥ sarvabhayaṃkaraḥ
vinadan ditijaśreṣṭho devānīkaṃ vyadārayat
balis tu rājā dyutimāñ śaśvat tatra mahāsuraḥ
japair homaiś ca saṃyukto brahmatvam akarot prabhuḥ
raṇāgnir jvalito ghoro vairendhanasamīritaḥ
devo viṣṇuḥ surais tatra rathavedyāṃ susaṃskṛtaḥ
śaṅkhaśabdaiḥ sutumulair bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaiḥ
udghuṣṭaṃ vipulaṃ caiva subrahmaṇyaṃ prayujyate
balaś ca balakaś caiva pulomā ca mahāsuraḥ
praśāntarūpaṃ kṛtvā tu mantraṃ samyak pravartayan
kalmāṣadaṇḍā vimalā vipulā rathapaṅktayaḥ
yūpāś ca samakalpyanta yuddhayajñe mahāphale
karṇinālīkanārācavatsadantopabṛṃhakāḥ
tomarāḥ somakalaśā vicitrāṇi dhanūṃṣi ca
asthīny atra kapālāni puroḍāśāḥ śirāṃsi ca
ājyaṃ ca rudhiraṃ raudraṃ tasmin yajñe 'bhihūyate
idhmāḥ paridhayas tatra prastārā vipulā gadāḥ
hayagrīvo 'silomā ca rāhuḥ keśī ca dānavāḥ
virocanaś ca jambhaś ca kujambhaś ca mahābalaḥ
sadasyās tatra tu makhe vipracittiś ca vīryavān
iṣavas tu sruvās tatra rathākṣasadṛśāḥ śubhāḥ
dhanuṣkoṭyo dhanurjyāś ca sruvas tatra mahāmakhe
pratiprasthānikaṃ karma vṛṣaparvākarot tadā
dīkṣitas tatra tu balis tasya patnī mahācamūḥ
śambaras tatra śāmitram akarod ditinandanaḥ
atirātre mahābāhur vitate yajñakarmaṇi
dakṣiṇās tasya yajñasya kālanemir mahāsuraḥ
vaitāne karmaṇi vibho yaḥ khyāto havyavāḍ iva
tridaśānāṃ tu sainyasya śarīrair gatajīvitaiḥ
tasmin yajñe tu savanaṃ vardhate daityanirmitam
devānāṃ rudhiraṃ saṃkhye papur ugrā diteḥ sutāḥ
nardamānāḥ pramuditāḥ somapānaṃ raṇādhvare
yadā balir mahādaityo vijetā samare surān
tadā hy avabhṛthaṃ yajñe bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
mahāsurendrapatayo yajvāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥ
vedavanto vṛttavantaḥ śūrāḥ sarve tanutyajaḥ
trailokyaharaṇe sṛṣṭā yuddhayajñāya dīkṣitāḥ
baddhakṛṣṇājināḥ sarve vratino muñjadhāriṇaḥ
ekaniścayakāryāś ca trailokyajayakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
suradānavasainyānāṃ śabdaḥ samabhavan mahān
nānāyudhanihastānāṃ tvaritānāṃ pradhāvatām
kṣveḍitotkruṣṭaninadair gajabṛṃhitanisvanaiḥ
rathanemisvanair ghorais tumulaḥ sarvato 'bhavat
śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣair hayaheṣitanisvanaiḥ
hayānāṃ heṣamāṇānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca garjatām
kṣveḍitotkruṣṭaninadaiḥ pāṇipādaravais tathā
dānavānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca śastravanti mahānti ca
samare bhīmakarmāṇi sainyāni pracakāśire
tato nāgā rathāś caiva jāmbūnadavibhūṣitāḥ
bhrājamānā hy adṛśyanta meghā iva savidyutaḥ
ṛṣṭikhaḍgagadās tīkṣṇāḥ śūlaśaktiparaśvadhāḥ
cāru bibhrājire tatra sveṣv anīkeṣu bhāgaśaḥ
rathā bahuvidhākārāḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
hemasaṃchannaśikharā jvalanta iva pāvakāḥ
dānavānāṃ surāṇāṃ ca samālokyanta sainikāḥ
kāṇcanaiḥ kavacaiḥ sarve jvalitārkasamaprabhaiḥ
saṃnaddhāḥ samadṛśyanta jyotīṃṣi gagane yathā
udyatair āyudhaiś citrais talabaddhāḥ patākinaḥ
ṛṣabhākṣāḥ suragaṇāś camūmukhagatā babhuḥ
nānāvarṇāḥ patākāś ca dhvajamālāś ca saṃyuge
yudhyatāṃ raṇaśauṇḍānām īrayām āsa mārutaḥ
dhvajālaṃkāravastrāṇi varmāṇi kavacāni ca
raśmibhir bhāsayām āsa raśmivarṇāni raśmimān
ubhābhyām aprameyābhyāṃ balābhyāṃ pādacāriṇām
rajaḥ pracchādayām āsa patrorṇāḥ pāṇḍurā diśaḥ
divyāyudhadharāḥ sarve dīptāyudhaparicchadāḥ
pratitastambhire 'nyonyam anīkaṃ pratyanīkataḥ
girikūṭocchrayāḥ sarve tadā te devadānavāḥ
anyonyam abhinighnanto raṇasthāś citrayodhinaḥ
bāṇaiḥ surucirais tīkṣṇaiḥ patravājair durāsadaiḥ
mudgarair musalaiḥ śūlair ayastuṇḍair ulūkhalaiḥ
vajrair aśanikalpaiś ca khaḍgavṛkṣādibhis tathā
tathā pravartite teṣāṃ vimarde 'dbhutavikrame
sāvitrasya vadhaṃ prepsur bāṇo jagrāha kārmukam
śarajālena divyena chādayānaḥ surottamam
mantrair huta ivārciṣmān sa prajajvāla tejasā
sāgarābhyāṃ mahāsenāṃ devānāṃ daityapuṃgavaḥ
saṃśoṣayati bāṇaughair arkāṃśubhir ivārṇavam
mārutaḥ sa mahāvegaḥ sāvitraḥ śaktim uttamām
cikṣepa baliputrāya śakro 'śanim ivādraye
āpatantī ca sā śaktir maholkā jvalitā iva
dvidhā chinnā kṣurapreṇa bāṇenādbhutakarmaṇā
hatāyām atha śaktyāṃ tu sāvitro devasattamaḥ
viśvakarmakṛtaṃ divyaṃ sutīkṣṇaṃ dānavārdanam
supītadhāraṃ vipulaṃ vimalaṃ candravarcasam
agṛhṇān niśitaṃ khaḍgam āśīviṣam ivoragam
taṃ gṛhītvā raṇamukhe prajvalantaṃ mahāprabham
bāṇābhyāśe mahātejāḥ khaḍgapāṇir avasthitaḥ
sa taṃ sthitam athālakṣya sāvitraṃ balinandanaḥ
lohitākṣaṃ mahākāyaṃ cikṣepa ca nanāda ca
tato 'rkakiraṇākārān aśanipratimāñ śitān
saṃdadhe cāśu bāṇaughān āśīviṣasamān balī
rukmapuṅkhān pradīptāgrān ugravegān alaṃkṛtān
ākarṇapūrṇāṃś cikṣepa śarān ugrān samantataḥ
dṛḍhacāpapramuktās te śarā vaiśvānaraprabhāḥ
sāvitraṃ chādayām āsuḥ kailāsam iva toyadāḥ
saṃchādyamānaḥ śastraughair bāṇena balisūnunā
parāṅmukhaḥ suravaraḥ prayātaḥ sarathadhvajaḥ
parājitya ca sāvitraṃ bāṇaḥ paramaharṣitaḥ
pragṛhya kārmukaṃ ghoraṃ gataḥ śakrarathaṃ prati
balaś cāpy asuraśreṣṭhaḥ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadām
dhruvāya vasave mūrdhni raudrāṃ cikṣepa dānavaḥ
tasya nirmathito deho hemacitraṃ ca varma vai
gadāvegena bhīmena dhruvasya samare tadā
śeṣaś ca vasavaḥ sarve divyāstrair ghoradarśanaiḥ
prācchādayan raṇe daityam ādityam iva toyadāḥ
tataḥ so 'marṣito bāṇair balo dānavasattamaḥ
avātarad rathāt tasmād gadām udyamya vegavān
pātayām āsa śatrūṇāṃ samāvidhya mahāsuraḥ
diśaḥ prādrāvayat sarvāṃs stridaśān sā mahāgadā
indrāśanir ivendreṇa pravṛddhāḥ sumahāsvanāḥ
tasyāḥ suvidyudghoṣāyās tena śabdena vejitāḥ
vyadravanta paribhraṣṭā rathebhyo rathinas tadā
tadudīrṇaṃ rathānīkaṃ sūryābhaṃ meghanisvanam
devānāṃ śaradhārābhiḥ samantād abhyavarṣata
kṣuraprair viśikhair bhallair vatsadantaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
muhur muhur mahātejāḥ pratyavidhyan mahāsuraḥ
balas tu sa gadāpāṇir vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥ
taḍidguṇārkasadṛśo vaiśvānara ivāparaḥ
pibann iva śaraughāṃs tān devacāpasamutthitān
abhyadravata daityendro mahārṇava ivāparaḥ
avasphūrjan diśaḥ sarvāḥ svena vīryeṇa dānavaḥ
arujaṃs tridaśān daityaḥ sindhuvegho nagān iva
samṛddhas tarasā devān vāyur vṛkṣān ivaujasā
śamayaṃś ca maheṣvāsāṇ vasubhyāṃ samasajjata
āpaś caivānilaś caiva vavarṣatur ariṃdamau
śaravarṣāṇi dīptāni meghāv iva paraṃtapau
kṣiptāṃs tān viśikhān dīptān antarikṣe sa cicchide
amṛṣyamāṇas tat karma dhruvas tam abhidudruve
tau pṛthak śaravarṣābhyām anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ
uttamābhijanau śūrau devadaityayaśaskarau
tau nakhair iva śārdūlau dantair iva mahādvipau
rathaśaktibhir anyonyaṃ viśikhaiś cābhyakṛntatām
nirbhindantau ca gātrāṇi vilikhantau ca sāyakaiḥ
stambhayantau ca balinau pratudantau sthitau raṇe
carantau vividhān mārgān maṇḍalāni ca bhāgaśaḥ
mudgarair jaghnatuḥ kruddhāv anyonyam abhimāninau
asibhyāṃ carmaṇī divye vipule ca śarāsane
nikṛtyācalasaṃkāśau bāhuyuddhaṃ pracakratuḥ
byūḍhoraskau dīrghabhujau niyuddhakuśalāv ubhau
bāhubhiḥ samasajjetām āyasaiḥ parighair iva
tayor āsīd bhujāghātanigrahaḥ pragrahas tathā
atīva bhīmaḥ saṃhrādo vajraparvatayor iva
dvipāv iva viṣāṇāgraiḥ śṛṅgair iva mahāvṛṣau
anyonyam abhisaṃrabdhau muhūrtaṃ paryakarṣatām
tataḥ parājito devo balakena tadā dhruvaḥ
rathaṃ tyaktvā bhayāt tasya pranaṣṭaḥ prāṅmukho vasuḥ
punar eva ca tatrāsīn mahad yuddhaṃ sudāruṇam
kruddhasya namuceś caiva dharasya ca mahātmanaḥ
saṃrabdhau ca mahābāhū maheṣvāsāv ariṃdamau
parasparam udīkṣetāṃ dahantāv iva locanaiḥ
visphārya ca mahac cāpaṃ hemapṛṣṭhaṃ dūrāsadam
saṃrambhāt sa vasuśreṣṭhas tyaktvā prāṇān ayudhyata
sa sāyakamayair jālair vṛto daityarathaṃ prati
bhānumadbhiḥ śilādhautair bhānoḥ pracchādayat prabhām
tataḥ prahasya namucir dharasya ca śilāśitān
asṛjat sāyakān dīptān bhīmavegān durāsadān
mahātejā mahābāhur mahāvego mahārathaḥ
vivyādhātiratho daityo navabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
sa totrair iva mātaṅgo dāryamāṇaḥ patatribhiḥ
abhyadhāvata saṃkruddho namuciṃ vasusattamaḥ
tam āpatantaṃ vegena saṃrambhān namucī raṇe
daityaḥ pratyasarad devaṃ matto mattam iva dvipam
tataḥ prādhmāpayac chaṅkhaṃ bherīśatanināditam
vikṣobhya tad balaṃ harṣād uddhūtārṇavasaprabham
aśvān ṛkṣasavarṇābhān haṃsavarṇaiḥ suvājibhiḥ
bhiśrayan samare daityo vasuṃ prācchādayac charaiḥ
samāśliṣṭāv athānyonyaṃ vasudānavayo rathau
dṛṣṭvā prākampata muhus tridaśānāṃ mahad balam
krodhasaṃraktatāmrākṣau prekṣamāṇau muhur muhuḥ
garjantāv iva śārdūlau prabhinnāv iva vāraṇau
mahāmeghopamaṃ raudram āsīd āyodhanaṃ tayoḥ
rathāśvanarasaṃbādhaṃ mattavāraṇasaṃkulam
samājam iva taṃ dṛṣṭvā prekṣamānau mahārathau
āśaṃsante jayaṃ tābhyāṃ yodhās te gaṇaśaḥ sthitāḥ
tayoḥ praikṣanta samaraṃ saṃnikṛṣṭaṃ mahāstrayoḥ
siddhagandharvamunayo devadānavayos tadā
tau chādayantāv anyonyaṃ samare niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
śarajālāvṛtaṃ vyoma cakratus tau mahābalau
tāv anyonyaṃ jighāṃsantau śarais tīkṣnair mahārathau
prekṣaṇiyatarāv āstāṃ vṛṣṭimantāv ivāmbudau
suvarṇavikṛtān bāṇān pramuñcantāv ariṃdamau
bhāskarābhaṃ tadākāśam ulkābhir iva cakratuḥ
tayoḥ śarāḥ prakāśante devadānavayos tadā
paṅktyaḥ śaradi mattānāṃ sārasānām ivāmbare
tridaśāśvagajānāṃ hi śarīrair gatajīvitaiḥ
kṣaṇena saṃvṛtā bhūmir meghair iva nabhastalam
tataḥ sudhāraṃ jvalitaṃ sūryamaṇḍalasaṃnibham
dharāya vasave muktaṃ cakraṃ namucinā raṇe
patatā tena cakreṇa dharasya syandanottamaḥ
sadhvajaḥ sapatākaś ca dagdho 'rkakiraṇaprabhaḥ
sa tyaktvā syandanaṃ devaḥ pradīptaṃ cakratejasā
bhayāt tasyāsurendrasya gataḥ svagṛham uttamam
parājitya suraṃ daityo namucir baladarpitaḥ
prayātaḥ svena sainyena bhūyaḥ suracamūṃ prati
yau tau mayaś ca tvaṣṭā ca devadaityeṣu viśrutau
pravarau viśvakarmāṇau māyāśataviśāradau
ghoras tayoḥ saṃprahāraḥ prāvartata sudāruṇaḥ
anyonyaspardhinos tatra cirāt prabhṛti saṃyuge
tvaṣṭā tu niśitair bāṇair daityaṃ tu baladarpitam
parākrāntaṃ parākramya vivyādha triṃśatā śaraiḥ
mayas tu prativivyādha tvaṣṭāraṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
sudhautaiḥ suprasannāgraiḥ śātakumbhavibhūṣitaiḥ
nanāda ditijaśreṣṭho hatas tvaṣṭuḥ śarair mayaḥ
saṃkruddho daityasainyasya vicinvann iva jīvitam
śaktiṃ kanakacitrākṣāṃ citradaṇḍāṃ mahāprabhām
devo gṛhītvā samare daityendre saṃnyapātayat
bhīmāṃ sarvāyasīṃ tvaṣṭā puraṃdara ivāśanim
tāṃ tvaṣṭur bhujanirmuktām arkavaiśvānaraprabhām
mayaś ciccheda tīkṣṇāgrais tūrṇaṃ saptabhir āśugaiḥ
tataḥ kṣiṇvann iva prāṇāṃs tvaṣṭuḥ kopān mahāsuraḥ
preṣayām āsa saṃrabdhaḥ śarān barhiṇavāsasaḥ
ciccheda bāṇāṃs tvaṣṭā tāñ jvalitair nataparvabhiḥ
daityasya sumahāvegaiḥ suvarṇavikṛtaiḥ śaraiḥ
tau vṛṣāv iva nardantau balinau vāśitāntare
śārdūlāv iva cānyonyaṃ prasaktāv abhijaghnatuḥ
anyonyaṃ pratividhyantāv anyonyavadhakāṅkṣiṇau
anyonyam abhivīkṣantau kruddhāv āśīviṣāv iva
mahāgajāv ivāsādya viṣāṇāgraiḥ parasparam
śaraiḥ pūrṇāyatotsṛṣṭair anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ
tataḥ sa vipulāṃ dīptāṃ mayo rukmāṅgadāṃ gadām
tvaṣṭuḥ saṃprāhiṇotkruddhaḥ sarvaprāṇaharāṃ raṇe
tayā jaghānātirathas tvaṣṭur uttamavājinaḥ
gadayā dānavaḥ kruddho vajreṇendra ivācalān
tataḥ kruddho mahādaityaḥ kṣurābhyāṃ tasya saṃyuge
dhvajaṃ tvaṣṭur atha cchittvā sūtaṃ ninye yamakṣayam
dṛṣṭvā tvaṣṭā hataṃ sūtaṃ kṣurābhyāṃ vinipātitam
hatāśvaṃ ratham utsṛjya sūtaṃ ca patitaṃ bhuvi
visphārayan mahācāpaṃ sthito bhūmau mahābalaḥ
hatāśvasūtaṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā ripum avasthitam
jayaśriyā sevyamāno dīpyamāna ivācalaḥ
mayaḥ kālāntakaprakhyaś cāpapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
prādahad devasainyāni dāvāgnir iva kānanam
svaṣṭuḥ so 'kṣipatātyugrān nārācāṃs tigmatejasaḥ
caturdaśa śilādhautān sāyakān vividhākṛtīn
te papus tasya devasya śoṇitaṃ rukmabhūṣaṇāḥ
āśīviṣā iva kruddhā bhujagāḥ kālacoditāḥ
te kṣitiṃ samavartanta śobhante rudhirokṣitāḥ
ardhapraviṣṭāḥ saṃrabdhā bilānīva mahoragāḥ
te prakāśanta nārācāḥ praviśanto vasuṃdharām
astaṃ gacchantam ādityaṃ praviśanta ivāṃśavaḥ
taṃ pratyavidhyat tvaṣṭā tu jāmbūnadavibhūṣitaiḥ
caturdaśabhir atyugrair nārācair abhidārayan
te tasya daityasya bhujaṃ savyaṃ nirbhidya patriṇaḥ
vidārya viviśur bhūmiṃ bhujagā iva vegitāḥ
mayas tribhir athānarcchat tvaṣṭāraṃ tu patatribhiḥ
sapatravegair vikṛtair jvaladbhiḥ prāṇanāśanaiḥ
tvaṣṭātha mayanirmuktaiḥ sāyakair arditaḥ prabhuḥ
apayāto raṇaṃ hitvā vrīḍayābhisamanvitaḥ
taṃ tatra hatasūtāśvaṃ bhujaṃgam iva nirviṣam
tvaṣṭāraṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā muditaḥ sa tu dānavaḥ
visphārayan suruciraṃ cāpaṃ rukmāṅgadaṃ dṛḍham
raṇe 'bhyatiṣṭhad daityendro jvalann iva hutāśanaḥ
pulomā tu balaślāghī dṛpto dānavasattamaḥ
raṇe śvetāśvayuktena rathena pratyadṛśyata
sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṃ yaḥ prāṇaḥ kathyate dvijaiḥ
balinā kālakalpena vāyunā saha saṃgataḥ
pulomnas tatra pavanaḥ śrutvā jyātalanisvanam
nāmṛṣyata yathā matto gajaḥ pratigajasvanam
daityacāpacyutair bāṇaiḥ prācchādyanta diśo daśa
raśmijālair ivārkasya vitataṃ sāmbaraṃ jagat
sa tāmranayanaḥ kruddhaḥ śvasann iva mahoragaḥ
vṛto daityaśatair vāyū raśmivān iva bhāskaraḥ
daityacāpabhujotsṛṣṭāḥ śarā barhiṇavāsasaḥ
rukmapuṅkhā vyarājanta haṃsāḥ śreṇīkṛtā iva
cāpadhvajapatākābhyaḥ śastrā dīptamukhāś cyutāḥ
prapatantaḥ sma dṛśyante daityasyāyutaśaḥ śarāḥ
evaṃ sutīkṣṇān khacarāñ śalabhān iva pāvake
suvarṇavikṛtāṃś citrān mumoca ditijaḥ śarān
tam antakam iva kruddham āpatantaṃ sa mārutaḥ
tyaktvā prāṇān atikramya vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
tasya vegam asaṃhāryaṃ dṛṣṭvā vāyuḥ sanātanaḥ
uttamaṃ javam āsthāya vyadhamat sāyakavrajān
tato vidhamya balavāñ śarajālāni mārutaḥ
vivyādha daityaṃ viṃśatyā viśikhair nataparvabhiḥ
mārudgaṇānāṃ pravarā daśa divyā mahaujasaḥ
sādhu sādhv iti vegena siṃhanādaṃ pracakrire
tasmin samutthite śabde tumule lomaharṣaṇe
abhyadhāvanta ditijāḥ paulomāḥ krodhamūrchitāḥ
te samāsādya pavanaṃ samāvṛṇvañ śarottamaiḥ
parvataṃ vāridhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakāḥ
te pīḍayantaḥ pavanaṃ kruddhāḥ sapta mahārathāḥ
prajāsaṃharaṇe ghorāḥ somaṃ sapta grahā iva
tato dakṣiṇam akṣobhyaṃ nānāratnavibhūṣitam
karaṃ gajakarākāram udyamya yudhi mārutaḥ
teṣāṃ mūrdhasu daityānāṃ pātayām āsa vīryavān
nihatā vāyuvegena sapta tena mahārathāḥ
tyaktvā prāṇān pulomā tu vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥ
tasyāpi tam asaṃhāryaṃ dṛṣtvā vāyuḥ sanātanaḥ
asaṃcintya śaraughāṃs tāñ jvalitān vai pulomataḥ
teṣāṃ vidārya tejāṃsi dānavānāṃ mahātmanām
śoṇitaklinnamukuṭā gairikārdrā ivādrayaḥ
te bhinnavarmāsthibhujāḥ patanto bhānti dānavāḥ
mātaṅgayūthasaṃrugṇāḥ puṣpitā iva pādapāḥ
teṣāṃ vidāritair dehair dānavānāṃ mahātmanām
tataḥ prāvartata nadī raudrarūpā bhayāvahā
prasravantī raṇe raktaṃ bhīrūṇāṃ bhayavardhinī
devadaityagaṇaiś caiva rudhiraughapariplutā
raṇabhūmir abhūd raudrā tatra tatra sahasraśaḥ
saṃbhṛtā gatasattvaiś ca yakṣarākṣasakhecaraiḥ
sānukarṣapatākaiś ca sopāsaṅgair dhvajai rathaiḥ
śīrṇakumbhais tathā nāgair ghaṇṭābhiḥ suvibhūṣitaiḥ
suvarṇapuṅkhair jvalitair nārācais tigmatejasaiḥ
devadānavanirmuktaiḥ saviṣair uragair iva
prāsatomaranārācaiḥ śaktikhaḍgaparaśvadhaiḥ
suvarṇavikṛtaiś cāpair gadāmusalapaṭṭisaiḥ
kanakāṅgadakeyūrair maṇibhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥ
tanutraiḥ satalatraiś ca hārair niṣkaiś ca śobhanaiḥ
hataiś ca ditijais tatra śastrasyandanavarjitaiḥ
patitair apaviddhaiś ca śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
nipātitadhvajaratho hatavājirathadvipaḥ
vimardo devasainyānāṃ sadṛśaḥ karmaṇāṃ babhau
atha daityasahasreṇa paulomena mahārathaḥ
saṃvṛtaḥ pavanaḥ śrīmān gadāmusalapāṇinā
te jaghnuḥ śatasāhasrāḥ pavanaṃ dānavottamāḥ
tair vadhyamānaḥ sa babhau samantād arpitaiḥ śaraiḥ
hatvāṣṭau tatra yodhānāṃ śatāni pavanaḥ prabhuḥ
kṛtvā mārgaṃ suraśreṣṭhaḥ prayātaḥ sa mahārathaḥ
adyāpi ca suvistīrṇaḥ panthāḥ saṃdṛśyate divi
nāmnā vāyupatho nāma siddhāḥ paśyanti taṃ divi
hayagrīvas tu ditijaḥ pūṣāṇaṃ prati vīryavān
nanāda sumahānādaṃ siṃhanādaṃ mahārathaḥ
visphārya sumahac cāpaṃ hemajālavibhūṣitam
pūṣāṇaṃ ditijo 'paśyat kruddho ghoreṇa cakṣuṣā
bhujābhyām ādadānasya saṃdadhānasya vai śarān
muñcataḥ karṣato vāpi dadṛśus tatra nāntaram
agnicakropamaṃ dīptaṃ maṇḍalīkṛtakārmukam
tadāsīd dānavendrasya savyadakṣiṇam agrataḥ
rukmapuṅkhais tatas tasya cāpamuktaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
prācchādyanta śilādhautair diśaḥ sūryasya ca prabhāḥ
tataḥ kanakapuṅkhānāṃ śarāṇāṃ nataparvaṇām
nabhaścarāṇāṃ nabhasi dṛśyante bahavo vrajāḥ
girikūṭanibhāc cāpāt prabhavantaḥ śarottamāḥ
śreṇībhūtāḥ prakāśante yāntaḥ śyenā ivāmbare
gṛdhrapatrāñ śilādhautān kārtasvaravibhūṣitān
mahāvegān prasannāgrān mumoca ditijaḥ śarān
tataś cāpabaloddhūtāḥ śātakumbhavibhūṣitāḥ
dehe samavakīryanta pūṣṇaḥ suniśitāḥ śarāḥ
te vyomni vikṛtākārāḥ saṃprakāśanta sarvaśaḥ
khadyotā iva gharmānte khe carantaḥ samantataḥ
śilādhautāḥ prasannāgrāḥ pūṣaṇaṃ vikṛtāḥ śarāḥ
parvataṃ vāridhārābhir yathā prāvṛṣi toyadāḥ
tatas tu pūṣṇo devasya balaṃ vīryaṃ parākramam
vyavasāyaṃ ca sattvaṃ ca paśyanti tridaśādbhutam
tāṃ samudrād ivodbhūtāṃ śaravṛṣṭiṃ samutthitām
nācintayat tadā pūṣā daityāṃś cābhyadravad raṇe
hemapṛṣṭhaṃ mahānādaṃ pūṣṇa āsīn mahad dhanuḥ
vikṛtaṃ maṇḍalībhūtaṃ śakrāśanim ivāparam
tataḥ śarāḥ prādur āsan pūrayanta ivāmbaram
suvarṇapuṅkhāḥ pūṣṇas te prabhavantaḥ śarāsanāt
māleva rukmapuṅkhānāṃ vitatā vyomni patriṇām
prādur āsīn mahāghorā bṛhataḥ pūṣakārmukāt
tato vyomni vibhaktāni śarajālāni sarvaśaḥ
āhatāni vyaśīryanta śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
tataḥ kanakapuṅkhānāṃ chinnānāṃ kaṅkavāsasām
patatāṃ pātyamānānāṃ kham āsīt saṃvṛtaṃ vrajaiḥ
pūṣā prāpūrayad bāṇair hayagrīvaṃ śilāśitaiḥ
nāmāṅkair arkasadṛśair divyahemapariṣkṛtaiḥ
tato vyasṛjad ugrāṇi śarajālāni dānavaḥ
amarṣī balavān kruddho didhakṣann iva pāvakaḥ
pūṣṇas tv ājau dhvajaṃ caiva patākāṃ dhanur eva ca
raśmīn yoktrāṇi cāśvānāṃ hayagrīvo raṇe 'cchinat
athāsyāśvān punar hatvā caturbhiḥ sāyakottamaiḥ
sārathiṃ sa mahātejā rathopasthād apātayat
kṛtas tu virathaḥ pūṣā hayagrīveṇa saṃyuge
pūṣā tasya rathābhyāśāt sa yayau tena vai jitaḥ
tatrādbhutam ito bhūyo yuddhaṃ vartata dāruṇam
kṛtapratikṛtaṃ ghoraṃ śambarasya bhagasya ca
saptakiṣkuparīṇāhaṃ dvādaśāratnikārmukam
vāsavāśaninirghośaṃ dṛḍhajyaṃ bhārasādhanam
vikṣipann akṣasadṛśān vyasṛjat sāyakān bahūn
krodhasaṃraktanayanaḥ śambaraḥ sarvayogavit
tena vitrāsyamānāni devasainyāni sarvaśaḥ
samakampanta bhītāni sindhor iva mahormayaḥ
tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya virūpākṣaṃ vibhīṣaṇam
bhagaḥ prasphuramāṇauṣṭhas tvaramāṇo nyavārayat
tato bhago maheṣvāso divyaṃ visphārayan dhanuḥ
avākirad daityagaṇāñ śarajālena chādayan
tam abhyayād bhago daityaṃ tūrṇam asyantam antikāt
mātaṅgam iva mātaṅgo vṛṣaḥ prativṛṣaṃ yathā
tau pragṛhya mahāvegau dhanuṣī bhārasādhane
prācchādayetām anyonyaṃ takṣamāṇau raṇe śaraiḥ
tayoḥ sutumulaṃ yuddham āsīd ghoraṃ mahāraṇe
bhagaśambarayor bhīmam aprameyaṃ mahātmanoḥ
atha pūrṇāyatotsṛṣṭaiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
vyadārayetām anyonyaṃ kārṣṇe nirbhidya varmaṇī
tau tu vikṣatasarvāṅgau rudhireṇa samukṣitau
takṣamānau śitair bāṇair nānvīkṣitum aśaknutām
atha vivyādha samare tvaramāṇo 'suro bhagam
nārācaiḥ krodhatāmrākṣaḥ kālāntakayamopamaḥ
garutmān iva cākāśe pothayāno mahoragān
nārācā nyapatan dehe tūrṇaṃ śambaracoditāḥ
tān antarikṣe nārācān bhagaś ciccheda patriṇā
jvalantam acalaprakhyaṃ vaiśvānarasamaprabhān
tato bhagaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā vivyādhāsurasattamaḥ
śilīmukhair mahāvegair jāmbūnadavibhūṣitaiḥ
tadā tat suciraṃ kālaṃ yuddhaṃ samam ivābhavat
śambarasya ca māyābhir nādṛśyata tato 'mbaram
dorbhyāṃ vikṣipataś cāpaṃ rathaṃ viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhataḥ
śrūyate dhanuṣaḥ śabdo visphūrjitam ivāśaṇeḥ
sa bhagasya hayān hatvā chittvā ca dhvajam āhave
abhyavarṣac charair enaṃ parjanya iva vṛṣṭimān
na tasyāsīd anirbhinnaṃ gātre dvyaṅgulam antaram
bhagadevasya daityena śambareṇāstraghātinā
daityasya cādbhutaṃ divyam astram astreṇa vārayan
māyāyuddhena māyāvī śambaras tam ayodhayat
avañcayad bhagaṃ daityo māyābhir lāghavena ca
sahasramāyo dyutimān devasenāṃ niṣūdayan
adṛśyata śaraiś channaḥ śambaraḥ śatadhā raṇe
adṛśyat patito bhūmau gatacetā ivāsuraḥ
atha sma yudhyate bhūyaḥ śatadhā śailasaṃnibhaḥ
diśāgajendram ārūḍho dṛśyate sma punar balī
pādeśamātraś ca punar bhūtvā bhavati śailavat
mahāmegha iva śrīmāṃs tiryag ūrdhvaṃ ca so 'bhavat
punaḥ kṛtvā virūpāṇi vikṛtāni ca sarvaśaḥ
sarvāṃ bhīṣayate senāṃ devānāṃ bhīmadarśanaḥ
tataḥ so 'nyaṃ navaṃ dehaṃ kṛtvā prāṃśutaraṃ punaḥ
gacchaty ūrdhvagatiṃ ghoro diśaḥ śabdena pūrayan
nabhastalagataś cāpi varṣate vāsavo yathā
saṃvartakāmbudaprakhyaḥ pūrayan pṛthivītalam
saṃvartako 'nalaś caiva bhūtvā bhīmaparākramaḥ
śatavartmā śataśikho dadāha ca punaḥ surān
muhūrtāc ca mahāśailaḥ śataśīrṣaḥ śatodaraḥ
adṛśyata divaṃ stabdhvā śataśṛṅga ivācalaḥ
yo 'nye daityāś ca sādhyāś ca ye ca viśve ca devatāḥ
kṣipanty astrāṇi divyāni tāni so 'grasatāsuraḥ
yudhyamānaś ca samare sarathaḥ so 'surottamaḥ
gandharvanagarākāras tatraivāntaradhīyata
te bhītāḥ samudaikṣanta tridaśā bhīmavikramam
sahasramāyaṃ samare śambaraṃ citrayodhinam
sa bhago bhayasaṃtrasto dānavendrasya saṃyuge
rathaṃ tyaktvā mahābhāgo mahendraṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
parājitya tu taṃ devaṃ dānavendraḥ pratāpavān
gato yatra mahātejā jātavedā mahāprabhaḥ
sa vahnir vāgbhir ugrābhiḥ kruddhas tarjayate balī
bhavāmy eṣa hi te mṛtyur ity uktvāntaradhīyata
etasminn antare caiva brāhmaṇendro mahābalaḥ
jaghāna somaḥ śītāstro dānavānāṃ camūṃ raṇe
kailāsaśikharākāro dyutimadbhir gaṇair vṛtaḥ
avadhīd dānavān dṛptān daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
pothayan rathavṛndāni vājivṛndāni cābhibhūḥ
daityeṣu vyacarac chrīmān yugānte kālavac chaśī
sa karṣan rathajālāni ūruvegena candramāḥ
dadāha dānavān sarvān dāvāgnir iva coditaḥ
mṛdgan rathebhyo rathino gajebhyo gajayodhinaḥ
sādinaś cāśvapṛṣṭhebhyo bhūmau cāpi padātinaḥ
śītena vyadhamat sarvān vāyur vṛkṣān ivaujasā
candramāḥ sumahātejā dānavānāṃ mahācamūm
tad astram abhavat tasya pradigdhaṃ śatruśoṇitaiḥ
pinākam iva rudrasya kruddhasyābhighnataḥ paśūn
yugāntakopamaḥ śrīmān daityeṣu vyacarad balī
āvārya mahatīṃ senāṃ pradravantīṃ punaḥ punaḥ
candraṃ mṛtyum ivāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā yodhā visiṣmiyuḥ
yato yataḥ prakṣipati śiśirāstraṃ tamonudaḥ
tatas tato vyaśīryanta daityasainyāni saṃyuge
vyadārayata sainyāni svabalenābhisaṃvṛtaḥ
grasamānam anīkāni vyāditāsyam ivāntakam
taṃ tathā bhīmakarmāṇaṃ gṛhītāstraṃ mahāhave
dṛṣṭvā śaśāṅkam āyāntaṃ daityānāṃ candrabhāskarau
tālamātrāṇi cāpāni karṣamānau mahābalau
chādayetāṃ śaraiś candraṃ vṛṣṭim antāv ivāmbudau
atha visphāryamāṇānāṃ kārmukāṇāṃ surāsuraiḥ
abhavat sumahāśabdo diśaḥ saṃnādayann iva
vinadadbhir mahānāgair heṣamānaiś ca vājibhiḥ
bherīśaṅkhaninādaiś ca tumulaṃ sarvato 'bhavat
yuyutsavas te saṃrabdhā jayagṛddhā yaśasvinaḥ
anyonyam abhigarjanto goṣṭheṣv iva mahāvṛṣāḥ
śirasāṃ pātyamānānāṃ samare niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
aśmavṛṣṭir ivākāśe hy abhavat senayos tayoḥ
kuṇḍaloṣṇīṣadhārīṇī jātarūpasrajāṃsi ca
patitāni sma dṛśyante śirāṃsi raṇamūrdhani
viśikhonmathitair gātrair bāhubhiś ca sakārmukaiḥ
sahasrābharaṇaiś cānyair vicchinnai ruciraiḥ karaiḥ
kavacair āvṛtair gātrair urubhiś candanokśitaiḥ
mukhaiś ca candrasaṃkāśais taptakuṇḍalabhūṣanaiḥ
gajavājimanuṣyāṇāṃ sarvagātraiḥ samantataḥ
āsīt sarvā samākīrṇā muhūrtena vasuṃdharā
cāpameghāś ca vipulāḥ śastravidyutprakāśinaḥ
vāhanānāṃ ca nirghoṣaḥ stanayitnusamo 'bhavat
sa saṃprahāras tumulaḥ kaṭukaḥ śoṇitodakaḥ
prāvartata surāṇāṃ ca dānavānāṃ ca saṃyuge
tasmin mahāhave raudre tumule lomaharṣaṇe
vavarṣuḥ śaravarṣāṇi saṃrabdhā devadānavāḥ
vyakrośanta gajās tatra śaravarṣaprapīḍitāḥ
aśvāś ca paryadhāvanta hatārohā diśo daśa
utpatya nipatanty anye śaravarṣaprapīḍitāḥ
devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca gajāśvarathināṃ raṇe
samare tatra śūrāṇāṃ pravarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
dhanurjyātalaśabdena na prājñāyata kiṃcana
śaraśaktigadābhis te khaḍgaiś cāmitatejasaḥ
nirjaghnur mahatīṃ senām anyonyasya paraṃtapāḥ
bāhūnām uttamāṅgānāṃ kārmukānāṃ ca saṃyuge
rāśayas tatra dṛśyante devadaityasamāgame
aśvānāṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ ca rathānāṃ ca varūthināṃ
nāntaṃ samadhigacchanti nihatānāṃ surāsuraiḥ
gadābhir asibhiḥ prāsair bhallaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
yodhās tatrābhyahanyanta hastyaśvam api tad bahu
prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇitaughataraṃgiṇī
tadā madhyena sainyānāṃ keśaśaivalaśāḍvalā
hāhākāro mahāśabdo yodhānām abhavat tadā
dānavair hanyamānānāṃ tridaśānāṃ mahāraṇe
evaṃ tad abhavad yuddhaṃ devānām asuraiḥ saha
vibhīṣaṇaṃ mahāraudraṃ vikṛtaṃ bhīmadarśanam
virocanas tu tatraiva viṣvaksenaṃ mahāhave
jaghāna rudhirābhākṣaṃ sādhyaṃ paramadhanvinām
tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya viṣvaksenaḥ surair vṛtaḥ
ameyātmā suraśreṣṭhaḥ pratyavidhyat stanāntare
sādhyasya bāṇābhihatas totrārdita iva dvipaḥ
virocanaḥ prajajvāla krodhenāgnir ivādhvare
sa kārmukavinirmuktaiḥ śarair dānavasattamaḥ
viṣvaksenaṃ bibhedājau dīptaiḥ saptabhir āśugaiḥ
so 'tividdho balavatā dānavena surottamaḥ
mūrcchām abhijagāmāśu dhvajaṃ cāpy āśrayat prabhuḥ
tataḥ sa punar āśvasya sādhyo yuddhe mano dadhe
visphārya ca mahācāpaṃ daityamadhye vyavasthitaḥ
virocanaś ca balavān abhyayudhyata sarvaśaḥ
kṣobhayan surasainyāni samantān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
tatas tasyāsurendrasya yudhyamānasya saṃyuge
śrūyate tumulaḥ śabdo jīmūtasyeva garjataḥ
jagarja ca mahāghoṣo vinighnan devavāhinīm
caṇḍamegho 'śmavarṣī ca savidyut stanayitnumān
diśo vidrāvayām āsa śaravarṣeṇa dānavaḥ
sarvasainyāni devānām udyatāstro mahāhave
te prādravanta vitrastā rathebhyo rathinas tadā
sādinaś cāśvapṛṣṭhebhyo bhūmau cāpi padātayaḥ
śrutvā kārmukanirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥ
sarvasainyāni bhītāni nivyalīyanta saṃyuge
virocanabhayatrastā rathebhyo rathinas tadā
padātīnāṃ yayuḥ saṃghā yatra devaḥ śacīpatiḥ
viṣvaksenasya sādhyasya sarvataḥ sa mahābalaḥ
pādarakṣasahasrāṇi nijaghāna caturdaśa
aśvavṛndeṣu nāgeṣu rathānīkeṣu cābhibhūḥ
padātīnāṃ ca saṃgheṣu vinighnan pratyadṛśyata
vitatya śyenavat pakṣau sarvataḥ sa varūthinīm
bhittvā bhittvā mahābāhuḥ śirāṃsy ājāv akṛntata
sādinaś ca padātāś ca hataśeṣā rathās tathā
viṣvaksenena sahitā virocanam abhidravan
te 'sicarmagadāśaktiparighaprāsatomaraiḥ
tam ekam abhyadhāvantaṃ siṃhanādaṃ pracakrire
tataḥ so 'siṃ samudyamya javam āsthāya dānavaḥ
cakarta rathinām ājau śirāṃsi ca dhanūṃṣi ca
rathanāgāśvavṛndeṣu balavān arisūdanaḥ
virocanaś caran mārgān prakārān ekaviṃśatim
bhrāntam udbhrāntam āviddham āplutaṃ viplutaṃ plutam
saṃpātaṃ samudīrṇaṃ ca darśayām āsa dānavaḥ
kecid varāsinā rugṇā dānavena mahātmanā
vineduś chinnavarmāṇo nipetuś ca gatāsavaḥ
chinnapṛṣṭhā hatārohā dānavena mahātmanā
vidrutāḥ svāny anīkāni jaghnus tridaśavāraṇāḥ
nipetur urvyām ākāśān nikṛttā dṛḍhadhanvinā
vividhās tomarāś cāpā mahāmātraśirāṃsi ca
pratīpam āharan nāgān aśvāṃś ca dṛḍhavikramān
cakarta rathinām ājau śirāṃsi ca dhanūṃṣi ca
āplutya rathinaḥ kāṃścit parāmṛśya mahābalaḥ
sūtāṃś ciccheda khaḍgena rathān api ca dānavaḥ
muhur utpatato dikṣu dhāvataś ca yaśasvinaḥ
mārgāṃś carita vai citrān vyasmayanta tato 'surāḥ
nijaghāna padā kāṃścid ākṣipyānyān apothayat
khaḍgena cānyāṃś ciccheda nādenānyāṃś ca bhīṣayat
ūrustambhagṛhītāś ca prapatanty apare bhuvi
apare daityam ālokya bhayāt prāṇān avāsṛjan
tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne yuddhe mahati dāruṇe
rathaughavājināgānāṃ surāṇāṃ ca mahākṣaye
kujumbho dānavaśreṣṭho hy aṃśam ādityam āhave
jaghānācalasaṃkāśo mattavāraṇavikramaḥ
devasenāsahasrāṇi sarathāni mahāhave
tasya bāṇapathaṃ prāpya nābhyavartanta sarvaśaḥ
praṇeduḥ sarvabhūtāni babhuḥ satimirā diśaḥ
devānām ajayaḥ kruraḥ pratyapadyata dāruṇaḥ
aṃśaś ca dānavendrasya jaghānottamavikramaḥ
anīkaṃ daśasāhasraṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ tarasvinām
āpatantaṃ gajānīkaṃ kujambho vīkṣya dānavaḥ
gadāpāṇir avārohad rathopasthād ariṃdamaḥ
adrisāramayīṃ gurvīṃ pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadāṃ
abhyadravad gajānīkaṃ vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥ
sa gajān gadayā nighnan vyacarat samare balī
kujambho dānavaśreṣṭho gadāpāṇir balādhikaḥ
viśīrṇadantāṃś ca bahūn bhinnakumbhāṃś ca vāraṇān
akarod dānavaśreṣṭha uddiśyoddiśya tān balī
kujambhasya ca ye 'mātyā dānavā ghoravikramāḥ
nārācair vividhais tīkṣṇair apāsya gajayodhinaḥ
kṣuraiḥ kṣuraprair bhallaiś ca pītair añjalikaiḥ śitaiḥ
ciccheda cottamāṅgāni kujambho dānavottamaḥ
śirobhiḥ prapatadbhiś ca gaganaṃ pratyapūryata
aśmavṛṣṭir ivābhāti bāhubhiś ca sahāṅkuśaiḥ
hṛtottamāṅgāḥ skandheṣu gajānāṃ gajayodhinaḥ
adṛśyanta mahārāja tālā viśiraso yathā
āpatantaṃ mahānāgam aṃśasyāsurasattamaḥ
jaghānaikeṣuṇā kruddhas tataḥ sa vimukho 'bhavat
vigāhyaivaṃ gajānīkaṃ kujambho dānavottamaḥ
vinighnan pravarān sainyān gadayā balināṃ varaḥ
ekapraharābhihatān kujambhena mahāgajān
apaśyanta surāḥ sarve parvatān iva pātitān
kujambhasya ca mārgeṣu viśīrṇās te mahāgajāḥ
vajrāhatā ivendreṇa viśīrṇā iva parvatāḥ
apaśyaṃs tridaśāḥ sarve mūrtimantam ivāntakam
gandhādevāsya dīryante siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥ
sa babhau tāṃ gadāṃ bibhrat prokṣitāṃ gajaśoṇitaiḥ
vyāditāsyo 'nadat kruddho raudrarūpo bhayānakaḥ
vikrīḍamāno gadayā raṇamadhye mahāsuraḥ
gopāla iva daṇḍena kālayan sa mahāgajān
kruddhaṃ kālam ivākāśe daṇḍam udyamya dānavam
apaśyanta surāḥ sarve kujambhaṃ bhīmavikramam
hatārohās tu tatrānye prabhinnā vāraṇottamāḥ
te hanyamānā gadayā bāṇaiś ca bhṛśavikṣatāḥ
asahantaḥ kujambhasya gadāvegaṃ mahāhave
svāny anīkāni mṛdnantaḥ prādravanta mahāgajāḥ
mahāvāta ivābhrāṇi vidhaman gadayā gajān
atiṣṭat samare daityaḥ kālaḥ saṃvartako yathā
tataḥ sarvāṇi sainyāni devarājasya śāsanāt
abhyadravanta ditijān nandanto bhairavān ravān
taṃ balaugham aparyantaṃ devānāṃ sudurāsadam
rathanāgāśvakalilaṃ śaṅkhaduṃdubhinisvanam
āpatantaṃ suduṣpāraṃ rajasā sarvato vṛtam
sainyasāgaram akṣobhyaṃ veleva makarālayam
tad āścaryam apaśyanta aśraddheyam ivādbhutam
udīrṇāṃ pṛtanāṃ sarvāṃ sāśvāṃ sarathakuñjarām
āvārya samare 'tiṣṭhat kujambhas tarasā balī
sainyārṇavaṃ devatānāṃ girir merur ivācalaḥ
anīkinīṃ kujambhas tu gadayā saṃnyavārayat
tasmiṃs tathā vartamāne saṃprahāre sudāruṇe
asilomā hariś caiva jaghnatus tau parasparam
asilomā tu balavān dānavo dānavādhipaḥ
devasainyasya sarvasya dhūmaketur ivotthitaḥ
tapaty arka ivāmoghaḥ surasainyāni saṃyuge
sahasraraśmipratimo dānavasya rathottamaḥ
śarair megha ivāvarṣad devānīkaṃ pratāpavān
śaraugharaśmibhir dīptaiḥ pratapad ghoravikramaḥ
raudraḥ krūro durādharṣo durvāryo dhvajinīmukhe
yudhyate daivataiḥ sārdhaṃ grasamāna iva prabhuḥ
ugreṣur ugravadano mṛdyamāno mahāgajān
surāṇām uttamāṅgāni pracinoti mahābalaḥ
grasan daivatasainyāni śaradaṃṣṭraḥ pratāpavān
asijihvaś cakrahastaś cāpavyāttānano 'suraḥ
paraśvadhanakhaḥ śrīmān mṛdaṅgāpūritadhvaniḥ
tiṣṭhate dānavaśreṣṭhaḥ saṃyuge vyāghravad balī
maurvīghoṣaḥ stanayitnuḥ pṛṣatkaprathito mahān
dhanur vidyudguṇāṭopo mahāmegha ivāparaḥ
iṣvastrasāgaro ghoro bāhugrāho durāsadaḥ
kārmukormitaraṅgaugho bāṇāvartamahāhradaḥ
gadāsimakaro raudro jyāvelaḥ śikṣito 'rṇavaḥ
padātimīnaḥ sumahān garjitotkruṣṭaghoṣavān
hayān gajān padātīṃś ca rathāṃś ca tarasā bahūn
nyamajjayat sa samare paravīrān mahārathān
aplāvayat sa devaughān dāruṇo dānaveśvaraḥ
prāmardata yudhi śrīmān yudhi śreṣṭo yudhi sthitaḥ
apaṣyaṃs tridaśāḥ sarve śuddhajāmbūnadaprabham
saṃnaddhaṃ tatra yudhyantaṃ jvalantam iva pāvakam
madhyaṃdinagataṃ sūryaṃ jvalantam iva tejasā
na śekuḥ sarvabhūtāni dānavaṃ prasamīkṣitum
yathā prarūḍhe gharmānte dahet kakṣaṃ hutāśanaḥ
tathā suravarān daityo dahate balatejasā
devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca balaṃ nardati dāruṇam
vimūḍham abhavat sarvam ākulaṃ ca samantataḥ
tataḥ śūrā balodagrā hastyaśvarathadhūrgatāḥ
āryāṃ buddhiṃ samādāya na tyajanti mahāraṇam
tad utpiñjalakaṃ yuddhaṃ abhaval lomaharṣaṇam
devadānavayoḥ saṃkhye rudhirasrāvakardamam
na diśaṃ pratyajānanta bhayagrāhanipīḍitāḥ
astraghātāṃś ca vividhān dānavānāṃ tadā raṇe
anyonyaṃ mūḍhacittās te nijaghnur vyākulīkṛtāḥ
svān parān nābhijānanti vimūḍhāḥ śastrapāṇayaḥ
śiroruheṣu saṃgṛhya kaścic chūrasya saṃyuge
śūraś chinatti mūrdhānaṃ saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭānanam
bāhubhir muṣṭibhiś caiva vajrakalpaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ
praharanti raṇe vīrā āttaśastrāḥ parasparam
yodhaprāṇahare raudre svargadvāravighaṭṭane
saṃkule tumule yuddhe vartamāne mahābhaye
hayo hayaṃ gajo nāgaṃ vīro vīraṃ mahāhave
abhyadravañ jighāṃsanto hy asamañja samāhave
asurāś ca surāś caiva vikramāḍhyā mahārathāḥ
juhvataḥ samare prāṇān nijaghnur itaretaram
muktakeśā vikavacā virathāś chinnakārmukāḥ
hastaiḥ pādaiś ca yudhyante dānavās tridaśaiḥ saha
haris tu niśitaṃ bhallaṃ preṣayām āsa saṃyuge
sa tasya ghanuṣaḥ koṭiṃ chittvā bhūmāv apātayat
punaś cāpi pṛṣatkānāṃ śatāni nataparvaṇām
prāhiṇot sahasā tasya dānavendrasya saṃyuge
tasya dehe vimuktās te mārutena samīritāḥ
magnārdhakāyā viviśuḥ pannagā iva parvate
sa tair nipatitair gātraiḥ kṣaradbhir asṛg avyayam
babhau daityo mahābāhur merur dhātum ivotsṛjan
tato 'silomā saṃkruddhaḥ pragṛhyānyan mahad dhanuḥ
rukmapuṅkhāṃś ca niśitān preṣayām āsa sāyakān
tais tu marmasu vivyādha sarpānalaviṣopamaiḥ
gātraṃ saṃchādayām āsa mahābhrair iva parvatam
bhūyaḥ saṃdhāya ca śaraṃ mumocāntakasaṃnibham
supuṅkhaṃ sūryasaṃkāśaṃ bāṇam apratimaṃ raṇe
tena bāṇaprahāreṇa saṃyuge bhīmakarmaṇā
mumoha sahasā devo bhūmau cāpi papāta ha
tato hāhākṛtāḥ sarve deve bhūtalam āśrite
jagat sadevam āvignaṃ yathārkapatane tathā
parivāraṃ tu samare tasya hatvā mahāsuraḥ
ekatriṃśat sahasrāṇi yodhānāṃ dānavottamaḥ
tatraiva tu mahāyuddhe sasainyāv aśvināv ubhau
prayuddhau saha vṛtreṇa balinā devatāriṇā
bāṇakhaḍgadhanuṣpāṇiḥ samare tyaktajīvitaḥ
āsādya so 'śvinau daityaḥ sthito girir ivācalaḥ
tataḥ śaṅkham upādhmāya dviṣatāṃ lomaharṣaṇam
jyāghoṣatalaśabdaiś ca sarvabhūtāny amohayat
tataḥ saṃhṛṣṭaromāṇaḥ śaṅkhaśabdaṃ viśuśruvuḥ
yakṣarākṣasadevaughā vṛtrasyāpi ca nisvanam
gadātomaranistriṃśaśaktiśūlaparaśvadhāḥ
pragṛhītā vyarājanta yakṣarākṣasabāhubhiḥ
taiḥ prayuktān mahākāyaiḥ śūlaśaktiparaśvadhān
bhallair vṛtraḥ praciccheda bhīmavegaravais tathā
antarikṣacarāṇāṃ ca bhūmiṣṭhānāṃ ca garjatām
śarair vivyādha gātrāṇi devānāṃ priyadarśanaḥ
vṛtrāsurabhujotsṛṣṭair bahudhā yakṣarakṣasām
nikṛttāny eva dṛśyante śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca
atha raktamahāvṛṣṭir abhyavartata medinīm
gadāparighabhinnānāṃ devānāṃ gātrasaṃbhavā
pracchādayantaṃ bāṇaughair vṛtraṃ bhīmaparākramam
dadṛśuḥ sarvabhūtāni bhānumantam ivāṃśubhiḥ
tīkṣṇaraśmir ivādityaḥ pratapan sarvadevatāḥ
avidhyat sabalān kruddhaḥ sāyakair marmabhedibhiḥ
nadato vividhān nādān arditasyāpi sāyakaiḥ
na moham asurendrasya dadṛśus tridaśā raṇe
te 'sicarmagadābhiś ca parighaprāsatomaraiḥ
paraśvadhaiś ca śūlaiś ca pravavarṣur mahārathāḥ
tato vṛtraḥ susaṃkruddhas tais tadābhyardito balāt
abhyavarṣac chitair bāṇais tān sarvān satyavikramaḥ
tena vitrāsitā devā viprakīrṇamahāyudhāḥ
ghoram ārtasvaraṃ cakrur vṛtrāsurabhayārditāḥ
utsṛjya te gadāśaktiśūlarṣṭiparighāśanīn
uttarāṃ diśam ājagmus trāsitā dṛḍhadhanvanā
tataḥ śūlagadāpāṇir vyūḍhorasko mahābhujaḥ
prāvartata raṇe vṛtras trāsayānaś carācarān
tatraikas tu mahābāhur asiśūladharaḥ prabhuḥ
abhyadhāvata daityendraṃ vṛtram apratimaṃ raṇe
tam āpatantaṃ saṃprekṣya prabhinnam iva vāraṇam
vatsadantais tribhiḥ pārśve vivyādhāsurasattamam
so 'tividdho maheṣvāsaḥ śarair amitavikramaḥ
gadāṃ jagrāha balavān gadāyuddhaviśāradaḥ
tāṃ pragṛhya mahābhīmām adrisāramayīṃ dṛḍhām
aśvinaṃ sahasāgamya tāḍayām āsa vīryavān
dīpyamānaṃ tataḥ śūlam aśvī suvipulaṃ dṛḍham
prāsṛjad vṛtradaityāya sa haropamavikramaḥ
bhaṅktvā śūlaṃ gadāgreṇa gadāyuddhaviśāradaḥ
aśvinaṃ sahasā bhartsya garutmān iva pannagam
so 'ntarikṣāt samutpatya vidhūya mahatīṃ gadām
nāsatyopari cikṣepa giriśṛṅgopamāṃ balī
gadayābhihataḥ so 'śvī tyaktvā śūlam anuttamam
prayātaḥ sahasā tatra yatra yudhyati vāsavaḥ
parājitya tu saṃgrāme so 'śvinaṃ bhīmavikramam
jayaśriyā sevyamāno vṛtro yuddhe vyavasthitaḥ
tatraiva tu mahāyuddhe raṇājir devasattamaḥ
yudhyate saha daityena ekacakreṇa dhīmatā
pracchādya rathapanthānam utkrośantaṃ mahāravam
ekacakrasya sainyaṃ tac charavarṣair avākirat
mahāsurā mahāvīryā mahāpaṭṭasayodhinaḥ
śūlāni ca bhuśuṇḍīś ca kṣipanti sma mahāraṇe
tac chūlavarṣaṃ sumahad gadāśaktisamākulam
aśivaṃ ditijair muktaṃ durnivāryaṃ carācaraiḥ
anyonyam abhyavarṣanta devāsuragaṇā yudhi
mahādriśikharākārā vīryavanto mahābalāḥ
turaṃgamāṇāṃ tu śataṃ tasya yuktaṃ mahārathe
mahāsuravarasyeva hiraṇyakaśipor yudhi
teṣāṃ ca raṇapātena cakranemisvanena ca
tasya bāṇanipātaiś ca hatā vai śataśaḥ surāḥ
tataḥ sa laghubhiś citraiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
āyudhān acchinat kruddhaḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
vadhyamānāḥ śarais tīkṣṇai rathadviradavājinaḥ
gamitāḥ prakṣayaṃ kecit tridaśair dānavā raṇe
tataḥ prakṣīyamāṇāṃs tān utprekṣya ca dite sutāḥ
tyaktvā prāṇān nyavartanta pragṛhītavarāyudhāḥ
te diśo vidiśaś caiva pratirudhya prahāriṇaḥ
abhyaghnan niśitaiḥ śastrair devān ditisutā raṇe
raṇājir jvalitaṃ ghoraṃ paramaṃ tigmatesam
mumocāstraṃ mahābāhur mathanaṃ nāma saṃyuge
tataḥ śastrāṇi śūlāni niśitāni sahasraśaḥ
astravīryeṇa mahatā ditijaḥ saṃpracicchide
chittvā śūlāṃś ca tān sarvān ekacakro mahāsuraḥ
abhyavidhyata taṃ sādhyaṃ daśabhir niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
astravegaṃ nihatyaivaṃ so 'strais tasyānusainikān
jvalitair aparaiḥ śīghrais tān avidhyat sahasraśaḥ
teṣāṃ chinnāni gātrāṇi visṛjanti sma śoṇitam
prāvṛṣīvātivṛṣṭāni śṛṅgāni dharaṇībhṛtām
indrāśanisamasparśair vegavadbhir ajihmagaiḥ
ditijaiḥ kālyamānās te vitresuḥ surasattamāḥ
ekacakro raṇe tiṣṭhann apaśyad gajayūthapān
varābharaṇanirhrādān samudrasamanisvanān
mattān suvihitān dṛptān mahāmātrair adhiṣṭhitān
kulīnān vīryasaṃpannān pratidviradaghātinaḥ
śikṣitān gajaśikṣāyām airāvatasamān yudhi
nyahanat surasainyasya gajān gaja ivāsuraḥ
vikṣaranto mahānāgān bhīmavegāṃs tridhā madam
meghas tanitanirghoṣān mahādrīn iva cotthitān
sahasrasaṃmitān divyāñ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtān
suvarṇajālair vitatāṃs taruṇādityavarcasaḥ
ekacakro gadāpāṇir balavān gadinām varaḥ
utsārayām āsa gajān mahābhrāṇīva mārutaḥ
nihatya gadayā sarvāṃs tān gajān gajamardanaḥ
bhūyo 'śvasaṃghān balino niraikṣata mahāsuraḥ
śukavarṇān ṛśyavarṇān mayūrasadṛśāṃs tathā
pārāvatasavarṇāṃś ca haṃsavarṇāṃs tathaiva ca
mallikākṣān virūpākṣān krauñcavarṇān manojavān
aśvasainyaṃ mahābāhus tad apratimapauruṣaḥ
niṣūdayām āsa balī gadayā bhīmavikramaḥ
raṇājis tasya samare sarvān dṛṣṭvāsuradviṣaḥ
acintyavikramaḥ śrīmān abhyayād devavāhinīm
gadāyuddheṣu kuśalo rathena rathayūthapaḥ
hṛṣṭasainyo mahābāhuḥ prasthitaḥ śakrasaṃnidhau
triṃśacchatasahasrāṇi prāṇināṃ vinihatya saḥ
raṇe 'tiṣṭhata daityendro vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ
tasminn eva tu saṃgrāme balodrikto mahāsuraḥ
mṛgavyādhaṃ mahātmānaṃ yodhayaty ajitaṃ raṇe
mṛgavyādhasya rudrasya mahāpāriṣadās tataḥ
samutpetur balaṃ dṛṣṭvā hutāgnisamatejasaḥ
gajair mattai rathair divyair vājibhiś ca mahājavaiḥ
astraiś ca niśitais tīkṣṇaiḥ śaraiś cānalasaṃnibhaiḥ
tatas te dadṛśur vīrā dīpyamānaṃ mahāsuraṃ
raśmivantam ivodyantaṃ svatejoraśmimālinam
saṃgrāmasthaṃ mahāvegaṃ mahāsattvaṃ mahābalam
mahāmatiṃ mahotsāhaṃ mahākāyaṃ mahāsuram
taṃ saṃīkṣya mahāyodhaṃ dikṣu sarvāsv avasthitam
tataḥ praharaṇair ghorair abhipetuḥ samantataḥ
tasya sarvāyasās tīkṣṇāḥ śarāḥ pītamukhāḥ śitāḥ
śirasy adripratīkāśe mṛgavyādhena pātitāḥ
taiś ca saptabhir āviṣṭaḥ śaraiḥ śirasi cārpitaiḥ
utpapāta tadā vyomni diśo daśa vinādayan
tatas taṃ tridaśo vīraḥ sarathaḥ sajyakārmukaḥ
anuvavrāja saṃhṛṣṭaḥ khaṃ tadā sa mahābalaḥ
asuraṃ chādayām āsa taṃ vyomni śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
vṛṣṭimān iva jīmūto nidāghānte dharādharam
ardyamānas tatas tena mṛgavyādhena dānavaḥ
cakāra ninadaṃ ghoram ambare jalado yathā
sa dūraṃ sahasotpatya mṛgavyādharathaṃ prati
nipapāta mahāvegaḥ pakṣavān vai girir yathā
babhañja ca tato daityo bhagneṣākūbaraṃ rathaṃ
mṛgavyādhaḥ parityajya sthito bhūmau mahābalaḥ
virathaṃ prekṣya rudraṃ tu tasya pāriṣadāḥ śubhāḥ
utthitā ghoraraktākṣā vyomni mudgarapāṇayaḥ
sa tu taiḥ sahasotthāya viṣṭhito vimale 'mbare
mudgarair ardito bhīmair vṛkṣaḥ paraśubhir yathā
teṣāṃ vegavatāṃ vegaṃ nihatya sa mahāsuraḥ
nipapāta punar bhūmau suparṇasamavikramaḥ
sa sālavṛkṣam utpāṭya mahāśākhaṃ mahābalaḥ
sarvān pāriṣadān saṃkhye sūdayām āsa dānavaḥ
sa tair vikṣatadehas tu rudhiraughapariplutaḥ
śuśubhe dānavaśreṣṭho bālasūrya ivoditaḥ
athotpāṭya gire śṛṇgaṃ samṛgavyālapādapam
jaghāna tān pāriṣadān samare dānaveśvaraḥ
tatas teṣv avasanneṣu mahāpāriṣadeṣu vai
balaṃ tad avaśeṣaṃ sa nāśayām āsa vīryavān
aśvair aśvān gajair nāgān yodhān yodhai rathān rathaiḥ
dānavaḥ sūdayām āsa yugānte 'ntakavat prajāḥ
hatair aśvaiś ca nāgaiś ca bhagnākṣaiś ca mahārathaiḥ
tridaśaiś cābhavad bhūmī ruddhamārgā samantataḥ
evaṃbalaḥ sa daityendro mṛgavyādhaś ca vīryavān
yudhi prayuddhau balinau prabhinnāv iva vāraṇau
tatraiva yudhyate rudro dvitīyo rāhuṇā saha
viśrutas triṣu lokeṣu krodhātmā aja ekapāt
tat tadā sumahad yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
āsīt pratibhayaṃ raudraṃ vīrāṇāṃ jayam icchatām
devadānavadehais tu dustarā keśaśāḍvalā
śarīrasaṃghātavahā prasṛtā lohitāpagā
ājaghānātha saṃkruddho rudro raudrākṛtiḥ prabhuḥ
rāhuṃ śatamukhaṃ yuddhe śatrusainyavidāraṇam
tasya kāñcanacitrāṅgaṃ rathaṃ sāśvaṃ sasārathim
jaghāna samare śrīmān kruddho daityasya sāyakaiḥ
tasya pāriṣadas tv eko rathaśaktyā mahābalaḥ
bibheda samare hṛṣṭo dānavaṃ taṃ stanāntare
sa bhinnagātro rudreṇa tathā pāriṣadair api
rudrasya ratham āyāntaṃ sa rāhur dānavottamaḥ
pramamātha talenāśu sahasā krodhamūrchitaḥ
bhinnagātraḥ śarais tīkṣṇai rudreṇāmitatejasā
rudrapāriṣadān sarvān nijaghāna mahāsuraḥ
sṛjantaṃ śaravarṣāṇi dānavaṃ ghoradarśanam
bibheda samare rudraḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ
vartamāne mahāghore saṃgrāme lomaharṣaṇe
rudhiraughā mahāvegā mahānadyaḥ prasusruvuḥ
dānavaḥ samare rudraṃ nīlāñjanacayopamaḥ
nirbibheda śarais tīkṣṇair meruṃ sūrya ivāṃśubhiḥ
hatair dānavamukhyaiś ca śaktiśūlaparaśvadhaiḥ
patitaiḥ parvatābhaiś ca dānavaiḥ kāmarūpibhiḥ
vartamāne mahāghore saṃgrāme lohamarṣaṇe
mahābherīmṛdaṅgānāṃ paṇavānāṃ ca nisvanaiḥ
śaṅkhaveṇusvanonmiśraḥ saṃbabhūvādbhutopamaḥ
hatānāṃ svanatāṃ tatra daityānāṃ cāpi nisvanaiḥ
surāṇām asurāṇāṃ ca saṃbabhūva mahāsvanaḥ
turaṃgamakhurotkīrṇaṃ rathanemisamuddhatam
rurodha mārgaṃ yodhānāṃ cakṣūṃṣi ca dharārajaḥ
śastrapuṣpopahārā sā tatrāsīd yuddhamedinī
durdarśā durvigāhyā ca māṃsaśoṇitakardamā
bhagnaiḥ khaḍgair gadābhiś ca śaktitomarapaṭṭiśaiḥ
apaviddhaiś ca bhagnaiś ca rathaiḥ sāṃgrāmikair hataiḥ
nihataiḥ kuñjarair mattais tathā tridaśadānavaiḥ
cakrākṣayugaśastraiś ca bhagnair avanipātitaiḥ
babhūvāyodhanaṃ ghoraṃ piśitāśanasaṃkulam
utpetuś ca kavandhāni dikṣu sarvāsu saṃyuge
anyonyabaddhavairāṇāṃ daityānāṃ jayagṛddhinām
saṃprahāras tadā yuddhe vartate 'tibhayaṃkaraḥ
sainyānāṃ saṃprayuktānāṃ śūrāṇām anivartinām
ajasya caikapādasya rāhoś caiva mahātmanaḥ
teṣāṃ tu tatra patatāṃ kruddhānām atinisvanaḥ
udvarta iva bhūtānāṃ samudrāṇāṃ ca śuśruve
tatraikas tu sadhūmrākṣaḥ śrīmān rudro munīśvaraḥ
bibheda keśinaṃ śaktyā gadāpaṭṭisaśūladhṛk
nānāpraharaṇā ghorā bhīmākṣā bhīmadarśanāḥ
nipetū rudradayitā mahāpāriṣadās tadā
ratham āsthāya ca śrīmāṃs taptakāñcanakuṇḍalaḥ
dānavaiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ keśī yudhyate yudhi durjayaiḥ
tasya saṃgrāmaśauṇḍasya saṃgrāmāgre yuyutsavaḥ
niṣpetur ugravīryasya jvālā hi prasṛtā mukhāt
sa tu siṃhāñcitaskandhaḥ śārdūlasamavīkramaḥ
mahājaladasaṃkāśo mṛdaṅgadhvaninisvanaḥ
tasya niṣpatamānasya dānavaiḥ saṃvṛtasya vai
babhūva sumahānādaḥ kṣobhayaṃs tridivaṃ tadā
tena śabdena vitrastā tridaśānāṃ mahācamūḥ
drumaśailapraharaṇā yoddhum evābhyavartata
teṣāṃ yuddhaṃ mahāghoraṃ saṃjajñe lomaharṣaṇam
devadānavasaṃghānāṃ prāṇāṃs tyaktvā mahāhave
sarve hy atibalāḥ śūrāḥ sarve parvatasaṃnibhāḥ
tridaśā dānavāś caiva parasparajighāṃsavaḥ
teṣāṃ ninadatāṃ śabdaḥ saṃyuge meghanisvanaḥ
śuśruve 'timahāghoraś carasthāvarakampanaḥ
reṇuś cāruṇasaṃkāśaḥ sabhīmaḥ samapadyata
udbhūto devadaityaughaiḥ saṃrurodha diśo daśa
anyonyaṃ rajasā tena kauśeyāruṇapāṇḍunā
saṃvṛtā bahurūpeṇa dadṛśur na sma kiṃcana
na dhvajo na patākā vā na varma turago 'pi vā
āyudhaṃ syandanaṃ vāpi dṛśyate naiva sārathiḥ
sa śabdas tumulas teṣām anyonyam abhidhāvatām
nipetur ugravīryasya jvālā hi prasṛtā mukhāt
sa tu siṃharṣabhaskandhaḥ śārdūlasamavikramaḥ
mahājaladasaṃkāśo mahājaladanisvanaḥ
tasya niṣpatamānasya dānavaiḥ saṃvṛtasya ca
śrūyate tumulaḥ śabdo na rūpāṇi cakāśire
dānavās tatra saṃkruddhā dānavān eva jaghnire
tridaśās tridaśāṃś caiva nijaghnus tumule tadā
te parāṃś ca vinighnantaḥ svāṃś ca yuddhe mahāsurān
rudhirārdrāṃ tathā cakrur medinīm asurāḥ surāḥ
tatas tu rudhiraugheṇa saṃsiktaṃ mṛditaṃ rajaḥ
śarīraśatasaṃkīrṇaṃ babhūva sumahāraṇam
śūlaśaktigadākhaṅgaparighaprāsatomaraiḥ
tridaśā dānavāś caiva jaghnur anyonyam āhave
bāhubhiḥ parighākārair nighnantaḥ parvatais tadā
rudrapāriṣadān sarvān sūdayanti sma dānavāḥ
rudrapāriṣadāś caiva mahādrumamahāśmabhiḥ
vyadārayann atikramya śastraiś cādityavarcasaiḥ
etasminn antare kruddhaḥ keśī dānavasattamaḥ
saṃgrāmamarṣī ghoraḥ sa svāny anīkāni harṣayan
teṣāṃ paramasaṃkruddho vajram astram udīrayat
vajreṇāstreṇa divyena śastreṇa ca mahātmanā
mahāpāriṣadāḥ sarvaṃ nihatā yudhi durjayāḥ
vajrāstrapīḍitā bhrāntā rudrapāriṣadā yudhi
viprakīrṇadrumāḥ petuḥ śailā vajrahatā iva
evaṃ tat tumulaṃ yuddham abhaval lomaharṣaṇam
keśinaḥ saha rudreṇa tad adbhutam ivābhavat
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
vṛṣaparvā tu daityendro viśvam adbhutadarśanam
niṣkumbhaṃ yodhayām āsa lohitārkasamadyutim
krodhamūrchitavaktras tu dhunvan paramakārmukam
dhvajinīṃ prekṣya śatrūṇāṃ sārathiṃ tvarito 'bravīt
atraiva tāvat tvaritaṃ nayemaṃ sārathe ratham
ete hi devāḥ sahitā ghnanti naḥ samare balam
etān nihantum icchāmi samaraślāghino raṇe
etair hi dānavānīkaṃ kṛtacchidram idaṃ mahat
tataḥ prajavitāśvena rathena rathināṃ varaḥ
arīn abhyahanat kruddhaḥ śarajālair mahāsuraḥ
na sthātuṃ devatāḥ śaktāḥ kiṃ punar yoddhum āhave
vṛṣaparvavinirbhinnāḥ sarva evābhidudruvuḥ
tān mṛtyuvaśam āpannān vaivasvatavaśaṃ gatān
samīkṣya nihatāñ jñātīn avatasthe mahāsuraḥ
niṣkumbhaṃ tatra taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te tridaśottamāḥ
sametya sahitāḥ sarve taṃ drutaṃ paryavārayan
vyavasthitaṃ ca niṣkumbhaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā tridaśottamāḥ
babhūvur balavanto vai tasyāstrabalatejasā
vṛṣaparvā tu śailābhaṃ niṣkumbhaṃ samare sthitam
mahendra iva dhārābhiḥ śaravarṣair avākirat
acintayitvā tu śarāñ śarīre patitān bahūn
sthitaś ca pramukhe śrīmān sasainyaḥ sa mahābalaḥ
sa prahasya mahātejā vṛṣaparvāṇam āhave
abhidudrāva vegena kampayann iva medinīm
tasya tv ādhāvamānasya dīpyamānasya tejasā
babhūva rūpaṃ durdharṣaṃ dīptasyeva vibhāvasoḥ
rathaṃ tyaktvā sa tu śrīmān sakrodhaḥ kamalekṣaṇaḥ
vṛkṣam utpāṭayām āsa mahāśākhaṃ mahocchrayam
tataś cikṣepa taṃ vṛkṣaṃ niṣkumbho vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ
taṃ gṛhītvā mahāvṛkṣaṃ pāṇinaikena dānavaḥ
vinadya sumahānādaṃ bhrāmayitvā ca vīryavān
sagajān sagajārohān sarathān rathinas tathā
jaghāna dānavas tena śākhinā tridaśāṃs tadā
tam antakam iva kruddhaṃ samare prāṇahāriṇam
vṛṣaparvāṇam āsādya tridaśā vipradudruvuḥ
tam āpatantaṃ saṃkruddhaṃ tridaśānāṃ bhayāvaham
ālokya dhanvī niṣkumbhaś cukrodha ca nanāda ca
sa tatra niśitair bāṇair viṃśadbhir marmavedhibhiḥ
nirbibheda mahāvīryo niṣkumbho dānavādhipam
śaraśaktibhir ugrābhir daityānām adhipaṃ prabhum
viddhaḥ samaramadhyastho rudhiraṃ prāsravad bahu
udvignā muktakeśāś ca bhagnadarpāḥ parājitāḥ
śvasanto dudruvuḥ sarve bhayād vai vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ
anyonyaṃ pramamanthus te trāsitā vṛṣaparvaṇā
pṛṣṭhatas trāsasaṃvignāḥ prekṣamāṇā muhur muhuḥ
tyaktapraharaṇāḥ sarve kṛtās te vṛṣaparvaṇā
saṃgrāme yuddhaśauṇḍena tadā niṣkumbhasainikāḥ
tatraiva tu mahāvīryaḥ prahrādaḥ kālam āhave
yodhayām āsa raktākṣo hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sutaḥ
tasya dānavavīrasya yuddhakāle jayakriyāḥ
cakāra tvarayā yukto bhārgavo vijayāvahāḥ
hutāśanaṃ tarpayato brāhmaṇāṃś ca namasyataḥ
ājyagandhaprativaho mārutaḥ surabhir vavau
srajaś ca vividhāś citrā jayārtham abhimantritāḥ
prahlādasya śubhe mūrdhni ābabandhośanāḥ svayam
kālena saha saṃgrāme prayuddhaḥ sa mahāsuraḥ
prahrādasyātivīryasya śāntiṃ cakre sa bhārgavaḥ
daśa śiṣyasahasrāṇi bhārgavasya mahātmanaḥ
tāni dānavavīrāṇāṃ jepuḥ śāntim anuttamām
atharvāṇam atho divyaṃ brahmasaṃstavacoditam
raṇapraveśasadṛśaṃ karma vaijayikaṃ kṛtam
tataḥ sarvāstraviduṣaḥ samareṣv anivartinaḥ
vidyātapaḥsamāyuktāḥ kṛtasvastyayanakriyāḥ
dhanurhastāḥ kavacino vegenāplutya dānavāḥ
balim abhyarcya rājānaṃ prahradāṃ paryavārayan
āsthāya vipulaṃ divyaṃ rathaṃ pararathārujam
nānāpraharaṇākīrṇaṃ sacakram iva parvatam
tad babhūva muhūrtena kṣveḍitāsphoṭitākulam
meroḥ śikharam ākīrṇaṃ dyaur ivāmbudharāgame
srajaḥ padmapalāśānām āmucya suvibhūṣītāḥ
bāndhavān saṃparityajya nipatanti raṇapriyāḥ
mahāyudhadharaḥ śrīmāñ śubhavarmadharaḥ prabhuḥ
śirastrāṇatanutrāṇī dhanvī paramadurjayaḥ
siṃhaśārdūladarpāṇāṃ nadatāṃ kiṃkiṇīkinām
tasya daityasahasrāṇi prayānty agre mahāraṇe
sainyapakṣahatās tasya rathāḥ paramadurjayāḥ
saptatir vai sahasrāṇi gajās tāvanta eva ca
madhye vyūhodarasthas tu kālanemir mahāsuraḥ
dhanur visphārayan ghoraṃ nanāda prajahāsa ca
tasmiñ śatasahasrāṇi puro yānti mahādyuteḥ
dānavānāṃ balavatāṃ śakrapratimatejasām
sa samaṃ vartamānas tu pakṣābhyāṃ vistṛto mahān
abhavad dānavavyūho durbhedyaḥ sarvadevataiḥ
ṣaṣtiṃ rathasasharāṇi dānavānāṃ dhanurbhṛtām
nānāpraharaṇānāṃ ca parimāṇaṃ na vidyate
gadāparighanistriṃśaśūlam udgarapaṭṭisaiḥ
pragṛhītair vyarājanta dānavāḥ parvatopamāḥ
garjanto vinadantaś ca vikrośantaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
ayudhyanta mahāvīryāḥ samareṣv anivartinaḥ
tatra tūryasahasrāṇāṃ saṃjajñe nisvano mahān
hayānāṃ ca gajānāṃ ca garjatām abhitaujasām
duṃdubhīnāṃ ca nirghoṣaḥ parjanyaninadopamaḥ
śuśruve śaṅkhaśabdaś ca paṭahānāṃ ca nisvanaḥ
tena śaṅkhaninādena bherītūryaraveṇa ca
nirghoṣeṇa rathānāṃ ca krośatīva nabhaḥsthalam
sāgarapratimaughena balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
prahrādo 'yudhyata kruddhaḥ kālāntakayamopamaḥ
tasya nādena raudreṇa ghoreṇāpratimaujasaḥ
vineduḥ sarvabhūtāni trailokyavisṛtaiḥ svaraiḥ
antarikṣāt papātolkā vāyuś ca paruṣo vavau
vamantyaḥ pāvakaṃ ghoraṃ śivāś caiva vavāśire
prahrādas tu mahāvīryaḥ prahasan yuddhadurmadaḥ
uvāca vacanaṃ śrīmāṃs tatkālakṣamam uttamam
adyāhaṃ darśayiṣyāmi svabāhubalam ūrjitam
adya madbāṇanihatān devān drakṣyatha saṃyuge
bāndhavā nihatā yeṣāṃ tridaśair iha saṃyuge
adya te nirvapiṣyanti śatrumāṃsāni dānavāḥ
imam adya samudbhūtaṃ reṇuṃ samaramūrdhani
ahaṃ saṃśamayiṣyāmi śatruśoṇitavisravaiḥ
timiraughahatārkaṃ ca sainyareṇvaruṇīkṛtam
ākāśaṃ saṃpatiṣyanti khadyotā iva me śarāḥ
hṛṣṭāḥ saṃparimodadhvaṃ devebhyas tyajyatāṃ bhayam
adyāhaṃ nihaniṣyāmi kālendraṃ dhanuṣā raṇe
toṣayiṣyāmi rājānaṃ baliṃ balavatāṃ varam
tridaśān sagaṇān hatvā raṇe cāntakasaṃnibhān
akṣayāḥ santi me tūṇāḥ śarāś cāśīviṣopamāḥ
sthātuṃ me purataḥ śaktāḥ ke raṇe jīvitepsavaḥ
hatvā ripugaṇāṃs tuṣṭir anurāgaś ca rājasu
hatasya tridive vāso nāsti yuddhasamā gatiḥ
te bhayaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā raṇe dānavasattamāḥ
nihatyemān arīn sarvān modadhvaṃ nandane vane
evam uktvā mahāsainyaṃ prahrādo dānavottamaḥ
kālasainyaṃ mahāraudraṃ tarasāmardatāsuraḥ
sarvāstravidvāñ śūraś ca nityaṃ cāpy aparājitaḥ
yuddheṣv abhimukho nityaṃ svabāhubaladarpitaḥ
ṣaṣtiṃ rathasahasrāṇi vividhāyudhadhāriṇām
prahrādasyātivīryasya ye tasya tanayā nijāḥ
tais tu kratuśatair iṣṭaṃ vipulair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ
kṣāntā dharmaparā nityaṃ satyavrataparāyaṇāḥ
dātāraḥ priyavaktāro vaktāraḥ śāstravastuṣu
svadāraniratā nityaṃ brahmaṇyāḥ satyasaṃgarāḥ
yaṣṭāraḥ kratubhir nityaṃ nityaṃ cādhyayane ratāḥ
iṣvastrakuśalāḥ sarve bahuśo dṛṣṭavikramāḥ
mattavāraṇavikrāntāḥ śatrusainyapramardakāḥ
dārayantaḥ padākṣepaiḥ sughorān vātarecakān
yuddhotsukadhiyo nityaṃ krodharañjitalocanāḥ
saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭā daityā vinedur bhīmavikramāḥ
kṣveḍitāsphoṭitaravair anyonyaṃ samaharṣayan
veṇuśaṅkharavaiś caiva siṃhanādaiś ca puṣkalaiḥ
āplutyāplutya sahasā raṇe vavrur anekaśaḥ
tālamātrāṇi cāpāni vikṛṣya sumahābalāḥ
amṛṣyamāṇāḥ sahasā dānavā bāṇapāṇayaḥ
mahāsurair apy ajitā yodhayanti raṇe 'ntakam
prataptahemābharaṇāḥ sarve te śvetavāsasaḥ
dānavā māninaḥ sarve sarve svargābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ
śuśubhe sā camūr dīptā patākādhvajamālinī
gajāśvarathasaṃbādhā svargamārgābhikāṅkṣiṇī
tataḥ kālas tu niryāto bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
vinadan sumahākāyo vyādhibhir bahubhir vṛtaḥ
dadarśa mahatīṃ senāṃ dānavānāṃ balīyasām
abhisaṃjātaharṣāṇāṃ kālaṃ samabhigarjatām
āpatantaṃ tadānīkaṃ dānavānāṃ tarasvinām
pratilomaṃ cakārāśu vyādhibhiḥ sahito 'ntakaḥ
praviśya dhvajinīṃ caiṣāṃ ghātayām āsa vīryavān
kālo rudhiraraktākṣaḥ svenānīkena saṃvṛtaḥ
prahrādabalam atyugraṃ prahrādaṃ ca mahābalam
ājaghāna raṇe kālo daṇḍam udgarapaṭṭisaiḥ
śaraśaktyṛṣṭikhaḍgāṃś ca śūlāni musalāni ca
gadāś ca parighāś caiva vividhāś ca paraśvadhāḥ
dhanūṃṣi ca vicitrāṇi śataghnīś ca sthirāyasīḥ
pātyante vyādhibhir yuddhe dānavānāṃ camūmukhe
bahavo vyādhayo yuddhe bahūn asurapuṅgavān
vyādhīn api ca daityaughā nijaghnur bahavo bahūn
śūlaiḥ pramathitāḥ kecit kecic chinnāḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
parighair āhatāḥ kecit kecic ca paramāyudhaiḥ
kecid dvidhākṛtāḥ khaḍgaiḥ sphurantaḥ patitā bhuvi
vyādhayo dānavair evaṃ nānāśastrair vidāritāḥ
te cāpi vyādhibhiḥ sarve vividhair āyudhottamaiḥ
khaḍgaiś ca vipulais tīkṣṇaiḥ prāsatomaramudgaraiḥ
bhinnāś ca dānavāḥ śūlair nikṛttāś ca paraśvadhaiḥ
mudgaraiḥ paṭṭisaiś caiva vyādhibhiś ca mahābalaiḥ
kṣatāḥ śastrair anekaiś ca muṣṭibhiś ca mahāmṛdhe
vemuḥ śonitam akṣobhyaṃ viṣṭhabdhadaśanekṣaṇāḥ
ārtasvaraṃ ca nadatāṃ siṃhanādāṃś ca garjatām
babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ saṃgrāme lomaharṣaṇaḥ
muṣṭibhiś cottamāṅgāni talair gātrāṇi cāsakṛt
sāditāni mahīṃ jagmus tiṣṭhatām eva saṃyuge
astraphenā dhvajāvartā chinnabāhumahoragā
śūlaśaktimahāmatsyā cāpagrāhasamākulā
ratheṣūpalasaṃbādhā dhvajadrumasamāvṛtā
saśabdaghoravistārā lohitodābhavan nadī
sadhanuḥśakradhanuṣau kāñcanāṅgadavidyutau
tau daityakālajaladau śaradhārāṃ vyamuñcatām
tau mahāmeghasaṃkāśau rathanāgagatau tadā
babhūvatur atikruddhau sāmbugarbhāvivāmbudau
taptakāñcanasaṃnāhau divyahāravibhūṣitau
tau virejatur āyastau sūryavaiśvānaropamau
tau mahācalasaṃkāśāv anyonyasya camūmukhe
vajrāśanisamasparśair bāṇair jaghnatur āhave
parasparaṃ samāsādya tayor yudhi durāsadam
nāśaṃsanta tadā yodhā jīvitāny api saṃyuge
śaranirbhinnasarvāṅgā yudhi prakṣīṇajīvitāḥ
nipetur yodhamukhyās tu rudhirokṣitavakṣasaḥ
patitair nipatadbhiś ca pātyamānaiś ca saṃyuge
babhūva bhūḥ samākīrṇā yodhair udgatajīvitaiḥ
na gṛhṇatoḥ śarān ghorān na ca saṃdadhatos tayoḥ
antaraṃ dadṛśe kaścit prayatnād api saṃyuge
laghutvāc ca mahābāhū yuddhaśauṇḍau mahābalau
maṇḍalībhūtadhanuṣau sakṛd eva babhūvatuḥ
prahrādasya ca bāṇaughair dudrāvāntakavāhinī
tudyamānā balavatā vāyunevābhramaṇḍalam
hatadarpaṃ tu vijñāya prahrādaḥ kālam āhave
apayātaṃ ca samarād dviṣantaṃ saṃpratarkya tam
matvā vaśagataṃ caiva prahrādo yuddhadurmadaḥ
tatraivānyāṃ camūṃ bhūyaḥ sa mamarda mahāsuraḥ
kālaprahrādayo yuddham abhavad yādṛśaṃ purā
tādṛśaṃ sarvalokeṣu na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati
evam adbhutavīryaujā mahāraṇakṛtavraṇaḥ
prahrādaḥ parivṛddho 'tra kālas tv apasṛto raṇāt
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
dhanādhyakṣam anuhrādaḥ prahrādasyānujo balī
sasainyo yodhayām āsa kṣobhayan yakṣavāhinīm
mahatā ca balaughena anuhrādo 'surottamaḥ
ardayām āsa saṃkruddho dhanādhyakṣaṃ pratāpavān
amṛṣyamāṇas tridaśān āhavasthān udāyudhān
cakāra kadanaṃ ghoraṃ dhanuṣpāṇir mahāsuraḥ
āvarta iva saṃjajñe balasya mahato mahān
kṣubhitasyāprameyasya sāgarasyeva saṃplavaḥ
tridaśānāṃ śarīrais tu dānavānāṃ ca medinī
babhūva nicitā ghoraiḥ parvatair iva saṃplave
merupṛṣṭhaṃ tu raktena rañjitaṃ saṃprakāśate
sarvato mādhave māsi puṣpitair iva kiṃśukaiḥ
hatair vīrair gajair aśvaiḥ prāvartata mahānadī
śoṇitaughamahātoyā yamarāṣṭravivardhanī
śakṛnmedomahāpaṅkā viprakīrṇāntraśaivalā
chinnakāyaśiromīnā aṅgāvayavaśāḍvalā
gṛdhrahaṃsasamākīrṇā kaṅkasārasanāditā
vasāphenasamākīrṇā protkruṣṭastanitasvanā
tāṃ kāpuruṣadustārāṃ yuddhabhūmau mahānadīm
nadīm iva jalāpāye haṃsasārthopaśobhitām
tridaśā dānavāś caiva terus tāṃ dustarāṃ nadīm
yathā padmarajodhvas tāṃ nalinīṃ gajayūthapāḥ
tataḥ sṛjantaṃ bānaughān anuhrādaṃ rathe sthitam
dadarśa tarasā devo nighnantaṃ yakṣavāhinīm
kruddhas tato daityabalaṃ sūdayām āsa vittapaḥ
vikṣipann iva khe vāyur mahābhrapaṭalaṃ balāt
samīkṣya tumulaṃ yuddham anuhrādaś ca bhūpatiḥ
rathenādityavarṇena kuberam abhidudruve
sa dhanur dhanināṃ śreṣṭho vikṛṣya raṇamūrdhani
utsasarja śitān bāṇān vitteśasya mahātmanaḥ
kuberaṃ prāpya te bāṇā nirbhidya susamāhitāḥ
aparān pṛṣṭhato jaghnur vyāsaktān yakṣarākṣasān
devaḥ śarair abhihato niśitair jvalanopamaiḥ
anuhrādaṃ pratyudīyāt saṃkruddhaḥ paramāhave
tato vaiśravaṇo rājā kruddho yakṣagaṇaiḥ saha
vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi dānavaṃ prati vīryavān
tad yathā śāradaṃ varṣaṃ govṛṣaḥ śīghram āgatam
apārayan vārayituṃ pratigṛhṇan nimīlitaḥ
evam eva kuberasya śaravarṣaṃ mahāsuraḥ
nimīlitākṣaḥ sahasā daityaḥ sahati dāruṇam
roṣitaḥ śaravarṣeṇa dhanadena mahābalaḥ
indraketupratīkāśam abhito 'paśyata drumam
pravṛddhaśākhāviṭapaṃ taruṇāṅkurapallavam
utpāṭya kupito daityas taruṃ phalasamanvitam
nijaghāna hayāñ śreṣṭhān kuberasya mahājavān
tasya karma mahāghoraṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve mahāsurāḥ
siṃhanādaṃ nandanti sma anuhrādapraharṣitāḥ
tayos tu tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ saṃjajñe devadaityayoḥ
tatas tau krodharaktākṣāv anyonyavadhakāṅkṣiṇau
anyonyaṃ vividhaiḥ śastrair ghorair jaghnatur āhave
tridaśā dānavān yuddhe mathitvā prāṇadaṃs tadā
dānavais tridaśāś cāpi kruddhair bhuvi nipātitāḥ
dānavās tv atha saṃkruddhās tridaśān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ
vivyadhur vahnisaṃkāśaiḥ kaṅkapatrair ajihmagaiḥ
vidāryamāṇā daityaughais tridaśās tu mahābalāḥ
amarṣitatarā bhūyaś cakruḥ karmāṇy abhītavat
te gadābhiḥ subhīmābhiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ śūlam udgaraiḥ
parighaiś ca sutīkṣṇāgrair dānavāḥ pīḍitāḥ suraiḥ
śaranirbhinnagātrāś ca khaḍgavicchinnavakṣasaḥ
jagṛhus te śilāś caiva drumāṃś cāsurasattamāḥ
te bhīmavegā ditijā nardamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
mamanthus tridaśān vīrāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
tataḥ sutumulaṃ yuddhaṃ teṣāṃ samabhivartata
śilābhir vipulābhiś ca śataśākhaiś ca pādapaiḥ
parighaiḥ paṭṭisair bhallair bhiṇḍipālaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ
kecin nikṛttaśirasaḥ kecic ca vidalīkṛtāḥ
kecid vinihatā bhūmau rudhirārdrāḥ surāsurāḥ
kecid vidrāvitā naṣṭāḥ parasparavadhārditāḥ
vibhinnahṛdayāḥ kecic chinnapādāś ca śerate
vidāritās triśūlaiś ca kecit tatra gatāsavaḥ
tat subhīmaṃ mahāyuddhaṃ devadānavasaṃkulam
babhūva śastratumulaṃ śilāpādapasaṃkulam
dhanur jyātantrimadhuraṃ hikkātālasamanvitam
ārtastanitaghoṣāḍhyaṃ yuddhaṃ gāndharvam ābabhau
kuberaḥ sa dhanuṣpāṇir dānavān raṇamūrdhani
diśo vidrāvayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
kubereṇārditaṃ sainyaṃ vidrutaṃ prekṣya dānavaḥ
abhyadravad anuhrādaḥ pragṛhya vipulāṃ śilām
krodhād dviguṇaraktākṣaḥ pitus tulyaparākramaḥ
śilāṃ tāṃ pātayām āsa kuberasya rathottame
āpatantīṃ śilāṃ dṛṣṭvā gadāpāṇir dhanādhipaḥ
rathād āplutya vegena vasudhāyāṃ vyatiṣṭhata
sacakrakūbarahayaṃ sadhvajaṃ saśarāsanam
bhaṅktvā rathottamaṃ tasya nipapāta śilā bhuvi
vimathya tu kuberasya prahrādasyānujo ratham
surāṇāṃ kadanaṃ cakre saskandhaviṭapair drumaiḥ
vibhinnaśiraso bhagnās tridaśāḥ śoṇitokṣitāḥ
drumaiḥ pramathitāṅgāś ca nipetur dharaṇītale
vidrāvya vipulaṃ sainyam anuhrādo 'surottamaḥ
giriśṛṅgaṃ mahad gṛhya kuberam abhidudruve
tam āpatantaṃ dhanado gadām udyamya vīryavān
vinardann āhvayām āsa dānavendraṃ mahābalam
tasya kruddhasya saṃkruddho gadāṃ tāṃ bahukaṇṭakām
nyapātayata vitteśo dānavasyorasi prabhuḥ
daityas tu krodhatāmrākṣas taṃ prahāram acintayan
vitteśasyopari tadā giriśṛṅgam apātayat
sa vihvalitasarvāṅgo giriśṛṇgeṇa tāḍitaḥ
papāta sahasā bhūmau viśīrṇa iva parvataḥ
vitteśaṃ vihvalaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve te yakṣarākṣasāḥ
parivārya mahātmānaṃ rarakṣur bhīmavikramāḥ
muhūrtaṃ vihvalo bhūtvā prabhur viśravasaḥ sutaḥ
utthitaḥ sahasā bhūyaḥ piṅgākṣaḥ sa mahābalaḥ
nanāda ca mahānādaṃ trailokyam abhinādayan
janayann iva nirghoṣaṃ vidhamann iva parvatān
tam avadhyaṃ tu vijñāya nihataṃ punar utthitam
prekṣya piṅgākṣam āyāntaṃ dānavā vipradudruvuḥ
tāṃs tu vidravato dṛṣṭvā anuhrādo 'suro 'bravīt
kālanemiṃ ca nemiṃ ca mahānemiṃ ca dānavam
ātmānaṃ caiva vīryaṃ ca vismṛtyābhijanaṃ tadā
kva gacchata bhayatrastāḥ prākṛtā iva dānavāḥ
nivartadhvaṃ mahāvīryāḥ kiṃ prāṇān parirakṣatha
nālaṃ yuddhāya yakṣo 'yaṃ mahatīyaṃ vibhīṣikā
etāṃ samutthitām adya dānavānāṃ vibhīṣikām
vikramya vidham iṣyāmi nivartadhvaṃ mahāsurāḥ
te 'surāḥ saṃnivṛtyātha samadā iva kuñjarāḥ
nijaghnuḥ paramakruddhā devasainyaṃ mahāsurāḥ
kṣīṇapraharaṇāḥ kecin mahāmeghanibhasvanāḥ
darpotkaṭā bhujair eva saṃprahāraṃ pracakrire
pāṃsubhiś caiva kāṣṭhaiś ca śilābhiś ca mahābalāḥ
bāhubhiś ca tathānyonyam ākṣipanti sma vegitāḥ
muṣtibhiś ca talaiś caiva nakhapātair mahābalāḥ
pādapaiś ca mahāśākhair ayudhyanta raṇājire
anuhrādas tu saṃkruddho devatānāṃ mahācamūm
mamantha paramāyasto vanāny agnir ivotthitaḥ
rudhirārdrās tu bahavaḥ śerate yodhasattamāḥ
nikṛttāḥ patitā bhūmau tāmrapuṣpā iva drumāḥ
anuhrādas tu vikrānto devāṃs tv āśīviṣopamān
yudhyamānāṃś ca samare vyasṛjan niśitāñ śarān
dhanādhipena viddhasya anuhrādasya saṃyuge
aṅgāramiśrāḥ kruddhasya mukhān niścerur arciṣaḥ
atha bāṇasahasreṇa vitteśaṃ dānavottamaḥ
vivyādha samare kruddho daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
kuberas tu śarair bhinnaḥ samantāt kṣatajokṣitaḥ
rudhiraṃ parisusrāva giriḥ prasravaṇair iva
gadām atha samāsādya bhīmāṃ bhīmaparākramaḥ
cikṣeṣa daityam uddiśya balāt krodhena mūrchitaḥ
aprāptām antare so 'tha tāṃ gadāṃ gadayāsuraḥ
babhañja vinadan kruddhas tad āścaryam abhūt tadā
pragṛhya tu gadāṃ bhūyo hy abhidudrāva dānavam
tam āpatantaṃ dṛṣṭvaiva anuhrādo mahābalaḥ
giriśṛṅgam athotpāṭya kailāsācalasaṃnibham
dhanādhipaṃ pradudrāva vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥ
tam antakam ivāyāntam ajeyaṃ sakalaiḥ suraiḥ
grasantam iva taṃ daityaṃ trailokyam akhilaṃ ruṣā
tam ālokya tathārūpaṃ dhanādhyakṣo raṇaṃ bhayāt
apahāya yayau tatra yatra śakraḥ surādhipaḥ
tasya cāpi mahat karma dṛṣṭvā vittapatis tadā
jagāma bhayasaṃtrasto yatra devaḥ śacīpatiḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
vipracittis tu varuṇaṃ daityānām ādir avyayam
jaghāneṣugaṇaiḥ kruddho dīptair iva mahoragaiḥ
sa dahyamāno daityena dīptaiḥ śaragabhastibhiḥ
nābhyajānata kartavyaṃ saṃgrāme sa jaleśvaraḥ
sarvalokeśvarasyeva parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ
na śaknoty agrataḥ sthātuṃ vipracitter jalādhipaḥ
vajro nāma mahāvyūho nirbhayaḥ sarvatomukhaḥ
taṃ vyūhya pratyayudhyanta dānavā devavāhinīm
vahnijvālāsamaṃ tatra ravimaṇḍalasaṃnibham
mukham ābhāti daityasya vipracitter mahātmanaḥ
varuṇas tu mahātejā vipracittiṃ mahāsuram
pradahann iva tejobhir jigīṣuḥ pratyavaikṣata
sragdāmamālābharaṇaḥ keyūrāṅgadaśobhitaḥ
jagrāha parighaṃ daityaḥ kailāsaśikharopamam
pinaddhaṃ kāñcanaiḥ paṭṭair hemamālinam āyasam
yamadaṇḍopamaṃ ghoraṃ daityānāṃ bhayanāśanam
tam āvidhya mahātejā mahāśakradhvajopamam
vinanāda vivṛttāsyo vipracittir mahāsuraḥ
sa kaṇṭhasthena niṣkeṇa bhujasthair api cāṅgadaiḥ
kuṇḍalābhyāṃ vicitrābhyāṃ srajā caiva vicitrayā
dānavo bhūṣaṇair bhāti parigheṇāyasena ca
yathendradhanuṣā meghaḥ savidyut stanayitnumān
prasphoṭya parighāgreṇa vātaskandhān mahāsvanaḥ
prajajvāla sadhūmārciḥ saṃgharṣeṇa yathānalaḥ
vidyādharagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ gandharvanagarāṇy api
saha caivāmarāvatyā siddhalokais tathā saha
grahanakṣatracaritaṃ sārkacandravibhūṣitam
daityendraparighoddhūtaṃ bhramatīva nabhaḥsthalam
durāsadaḥ sa saṃjajñe parighābharaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
surendhano 'surendrāgnir yugāntāgnir ivotthitaḥ
tridaśā varuṇaś caiva na śekuḥ spandituṃ bhayāt
tatrāsīn nirbhayas tv ekaḥ kauśiko vāsavaḥ prabhuḥ
bhāskarapratimaṃ ghoraṃ parighaṃ raudradarśanam
pātayām āsa senāyāṃ jaleśasya mahātmanaḥ
patatā tena saṃgrāme jaleśasya mahātmanaḥ
bhūtānāṃ daśasāhasraṃ parigheṇa samāhatam
teṣāṃ gātrāṇi cāsādya vyaśīryata sahasraśaḥ
viśīryamāṇo vibabhāv ulkāśatam ivāmbare
bhūyaś cainaṃ tadā bhrāmya varuṇāya nyapātayat
sa bhinnaḥ parigho ghoro devagātre vyaśīryata
śīryamāṇasya cūrṇāni khadyotā iva cāmbare
sa tu tena prahāreṇa cacāla salilādhipaḥ
parigheṇāhataḥ saṃkhye yathā bhūmicale 'calaḥ
sa sainyeṣv atha bhagneṣu bhinnadeheṣu cāhave
muhūrtam agamat kṣobham apāṃ patir amarṣaṇaḥ
so 'marṣavaśam āpanno varuṇo 'mitavikramaḥ
sarvasaṃhāram akarot svapakṣasyārimardanaḥ
sa sāgaraiś caturbhis tu vṛto dīptaiḥ sapannagaiḥ
śaṅkhamuktāmaṇinibho bibhrat toyam ayaṃ vapuḥ
pāṇḍuroddhūtavasano nānāratnacitāṅgadaḥ
varuṇaḥ pāśadhṛk śrīmān kūrmamīnasamākulaḥ
varuṇas tu tadā kruddhas tān nirīkṣya svasainikān
uvāca hṛṣṭā yudhyadhvaṃ dānavānāṃ jighāṃsayā
tatas te pannagāḥ sarve mahārṇavajalāśrayāḥ
jaghnur daityān raṇamukhe nadanto jayagṛddhinaḥ
te tu nālīkanārācair gadābhiḥ parighair api
abhyaghnan dānavān dṛptān muditā varuṇānugāḥ
vipracittis tu saṃkruddho mahābalaparākramaḥ
pannagānāṃ śarīrāṇi vyadhamad raṇamūrdhani
gāruḍena tu so 'streṇa pannagān dānavottamaḥ
ghātayām āsa samare garuḍaiḥ pannagāśanaiḥ
sa śaraiḥ sūryasaṃkāśaiḥ śātakumbhavibhūṣitaiḥ
pannagān samare vīraḥ pramamātha sudurjayaḥ
te bhinnagātrāḥ samare pannagāḥ śarapīḍitāḥ
petur mathitasarvāṅgā gajā iva mahāgajaiḥ
pratapantam ivādityaṃ dīptair bāṇagabhastibhiḥ
abhyadhāvata saṃkruddhaḥ samare varuṇaḥ prabhuḥ
tatas tu dānavās tatra bhinnadehāḥ sahasraśaḥ
vyathitā vidravanti sma diśo daśa vicetasaḥ
indrasyārthe parākramya varuṇas tyaktajīvitaḥ
vinardamāno yuyudhe samare pāśabhṛd varaḥ
vāruṇāḥ pannagāś caiva muṣṭibhiḥ samarotkaṭāḥ
abhyavartanta samare vipracittiṃ mahāsuram
tato 'straiś ca śilābhiś ca praharan sa balotkaṭaḥ
vyapohata mahātejā vipracittir mahāsuraḥ
tataḥ pāvakasaṃkāśaiḥ sumuktaiḥ śīghragāmibhiḥ
varuṇasya mahāvegān bibheda samare hayān
karmaṇā tena mahatā vipracitter mahātmanaḥ
agner ājyāhutasyeva tejaḥ samabhivardhata
sa śaraiḥ sūryasaṃkāśaiḥ sumuktaiḥ śīghragāmibhiḥ
vāruṇīṃ tāṃ mahāsenāṃ nirmamantha mahāsuraḥ
kṣīṇāstrāṃ sāyakākrāntāṃ śarajālena mohitām
śūlaśaktyṛṣṭibhinnāṃ ca cakāra rudhirokṣitām
abhidruto 'tha daityena sasainyaḥ salilādhipaḥ
mahendraṃ śaraṇaṃ prāpto vipracitter bhayārditaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
parājayaṃ tu devānāṃ dṛṣṭvāgnis tridaśottamaḥ
cakāra buddhiṃ daityānāṃ vadhe brahmarṣibhiḥ stutaḥ
svayaṃprabhāyāḥ śāṇḍilyā yaḥ putro havyavāhanaḥ
hiraṇyaretāḥ piṅgākṣo devadūto hutāśanaḥ
lohito lohitagrīvo hartā dātā haviḥ kaviḥ
pāvako viśvabhug devaḥ sarvadevānanaḥ prabhuḥ
subrahmātmā suvarcaskaḥ sahasrārcir vibhāvasuḥ
kṛṣṇavartmā citrabhānur devāgryaś citra ekarāṭ
lokasākṣī dvijahuto vaṣaṭkārapriyo 'rcimān
havyabhakṣaḥ śamīgarbhaḥ svayoniḥ sarvakarmakṛt
pāvanaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tridaśānāṃ taponidhiḥ
śamanaḥ sarvapāpānāṃ lelihānas tapomayaḥ
pradakṣiṇāvartaśikhaḥ śucilomā makhākṛtiḥ
havyabhug bhūtabhavyeśo havyabhāgaharo hariḥ
somapaḥ sumahātejā bhūteśaḥ sarvabhūtahā
adhṛṣyaḥ pāvako bhūtir bhūtātmā vai svadhādhipaḥ
svāhāpatiḥ sāmagītaḥ somapūtāśano 'dridhṛk
devadevo mahākrodho rudrātmā brahmasaṃbhavaḥ
lohitāśvaṃ vāyucakraṃ ratham āsthāya bhūtakṛt
dhūmaketur dhūmaśikho nīlavāsāḥ surottamaḥ
udyamya divyam āgneyam astraṃ devo raṇe mahat
dānavāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni ca
dadāha bhagavān vahniḥ saṃkruddhaḥ pralaye yathā
prāṇo yaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ hṛdi tiṣṭhati pañcadhā
yantā yaś ca hutāśasya sakhā ca prabhur īśvaraḥ
prabhañjano yo lokānāṃ yugānte sarvanāśanaḥ
saptasvaragatā yasya yonir gīrbhir udīryate
yo hy ākāśagato devo dūragaḥ śabdasaṃbhavaḥ
yaś ca kartā vikartā ca gatir gatimatāṃ prabhuḥ
devakartā samo loke brahmaṇā yaḥ sanātanaḥ
amūrtimantaṃ yaṃ prāhur mahābhūtaṃ mahattaram
so 'gniṃ samīrayām āsa śamīgarbhaṃ samīraṇaḥ
tridivārohibhir jvālair jṛmbhamāṇo diśo daśa
dānavānām abhāvāya yugāntagnir ivotthitaḥ
medomajjāmahāpaṅkāṃ keśaśaivalaśāḍvalām
yodhaśīrṣopalavahāṃ mṛtadvipataṭotkaṭām
śoṇitodāṃ raṇe dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāmasaritaṃ vibhuḥ
vahniḥ praskandayām āsa daityānāṃ bhayavardhanaḥ
agnis tu sarvān ditijān prahrādapramukhāṃs tadā
parājayām āsa vibhuḥ krośamānān mahāhave
kecit pradīptair mukuṭaiḥ kecid dīptaiḥ śiroruhaiḥ
kecit pradīptair vasanaiḥ kecid dīptair bhujānanaiḥ
asurās tatra dṛśyante pradīptenāgninā vṛtāḥ
patākāś ca parāś cānye mukuteṣv aṅgadeṣu ca
sainyās te ca na dīpyante pāvakābhihatā raṇe
asurā bhayavitrastā vidrutāś ca diśo daśa
tyaktvāyudhāni sarvāṇi sadhvajāṃś ca rathottamān
dagdhāṅgāḥ samare bhītāḥ pāvakena parājitāḥ
na ca paśyanti te sarve rūpiṇaṃ dhvajinīmukhe
diśaḥ khaṃ gāṃ ca meghāṃś ca dīptān paśyanti dānavāḥ
dhruvaṃ svayaṃbhuvā sṛṣṭo yugāntas toyayoninā
ity evaṃ dānavāḥ sarve menire trastacetasaḥ
mayaś ca śambaraś caiva mahāmāyādharau tadā
pārjanyavāruṇī māye vyadhattāṃ vārivikṣare
tābhyāṃ vahniḥ sa māyābhyāṃ śāmyate vyutthitas tadā
toyaughaiḥ parvatanibhair mṛdvarcir abhavad raṇe
śāmyamāne tu samare pāvake daityanāśane
bṛhatkīrtir bṛhattejā vahnim āha bṛhaspatiḥ
hiraṇyaretaḥ suśikha jvalanākṣaya sarvabhuk
saptajihvānana kṣāma lelihāna mahābala
ātmā vāyus tava vibho śarīram uta vīrudhaḥ
yonir āpaś ca te śukre yonis tvam asi cāmbhasaḥ
ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca gacchanti saṃcaranti ca pārśvataḥ
arciṣas te mahābhāga sarvataḥ prabhavanti ca
tvam evāgne sarvam asi tvayi sarvam idaṃ jagat
tvaṃ dhārayasi bhūtāni bhuvanaṃ tvaṃ bibharṣi ca
tvam evāgne havyavāḍ ekas tvam eva paramaṃ haviḥ
yajanti ca sadā santas tvām eva paramādhvare
tvam annaṃ prāṇināṃ bhuṅkṣe jagdhapītāśitaṃ vibho
tvayi pravṛtto vijayas tvayi lokāḥ pratiṣṭḥitāḥ
sarvāṃl lokāṃs trīn imān havyavāha
prāpte kāle pacasi tvaṃ samiddhaḥ
tvam evaikas tapase jātavedo
nānyas taptā vidyate goṣu deva
vṛṣākapiḥ sindhupatis tvam agne
mahāmakheṣv agraharas tvam eva
viśvasya bhūmnas tvam asi prasūtis
tvaṃ ca pratiṣṭhā bhagavan prajānām
sṛjasy apo raśmibhir jātavedas
tathauṣadhīr oṣadhīnāṃ rasāṃś ca
viśvaṃ tvam ādāya yugāntakāle
sraṣṭā bhavasy ānala sargakāle
tvam agne sarvabhūtānāṃ yonir vedeṣu gīyase
tvayā devahitārthāya nihatā dānavā raṇe
svayonis te mahātejas toyaṃ nakhaśatārcitaḥ
tāṃ svayoniṃ samāsādya kiṃ viṣīdasi pāvaka
trāyasva devān samare daityebhyaḥ surasattama
piṅgākṣa lohitagrīva kṛṣṇavartman hutāśana
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
bṛhaspates tu vacanaṃ śrutvāgniḥ satyam īritam
bhūyaḥ prajajvāla raṇe haviṣeva mahāmakhe
hatās tu māyā daityānāṃ saṃpradīptāgninā raṇe
hatamāyā hatabalā baliṃ te samupasthitāḥ
parājiteṣu daityeṣu vahninādbhutakarmaṇā
prahrādas tūttaraṃ vākyam āha daityapatiṃ balim
bhavān agniś ca vāyuś ca bhāskaraḥ salilaṃ śaśī
nakṣatrāṇi diśo vyoma bhūś ca dānavasattama
bhaviṣyaṃ caiva bhūtaṃ ca bhavac cāsurasattama
dattaṃ hi te bhagavatā varahetoḥ svayaṃbuvā
indratvaṃ cāmaratvaṃ ca yuddhe cāpy aparājayaḥ
īśitvaṃ ca vaśitvaṃ ca balaṃ caivāmitaṃ tava
sarvabhūteśvaratvaṃ ca prabhutvaṃ ca sadā tava
mahāyogīśvaratvaṃ ca śūratvaṃ ca mahāmṛdhe
amitatvaṃ laghutvaṃ ca ye cānye sāttvikā guṇāḥ
tat parājaya devendraṃ devān sarvāṃś ca sānugān
yathoktaṃ brahmaṇā rājaṃs tat tathā na tad anyathā
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prahrādasya mahātmanaḥ
baliḥ paramasaṃhṛṣṭo gataḥ śatruratho yataḥ
tataḥ prayāntaṃ tridaśendrasaṃnidhau
mahāsurendraṃ balim uttamaśriyam
tam añjasā cakrur abhipradakṣiṇaṃ
dvijāś ca mukhyāḥ paśavaś ca maṅgalāḥ
mahājaṭābhāradharās tapasvinas
tadā tam āhur vidhimantramaṅgalaiḥ
abhiṣṭuvantaḥ kavayaḥ svalaṃkṛtaṃ
baliṃ prayāntaṃ raṇamūrdhani sthitam
prataptajāmbūnadacitrabhūṣaṇair
divyaiś ca ratnair vividhair alaṃkṛtaḥ
virājamānaḥ parameṇa varcasā
raṇe vibhāty agniśikheva dānavaḥ
sa vai tadā śatrubalārditaṃ balaṃ
balir dadarśottamavīryavikramaḥ
jalāgame śrīmad ivābhramaṇḍalaṃ
vikīryamāṇaṃ nabhasīva vāyunā
tato dadarśātha balāni sarvato
raṇe suguptāni hutāśanena vai
samutthitāny uttamavīryavanti
samudravegān iva parvasaṃdhiṣu
sa śūlaśaktyṛṣṭigadāsisāyakān
kṣipan ripūṇāṃ samudagratejasāḥ
nanāda siṃharṣabhamattanāgavaj
jalāgame toyadavac ca vīryavān
divyāstradhūmaḥ subhujaughavāyur
mahābalaḥ pauruṣavikramendhanaḥ
prajā didhakṣann iva kālavahniḥ
sughorarūpo vibabhau raṇe baliḥ
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
balinā tu surāḥ sarve varjayitvā surādhipam
raṇe śaraśatair bhinnāḥ sasainyā vai parājitāḥ
vimukhā sā tu daityendrair vadhyamānā mahācamūḥ
jitāś ca balinā devāḥ śakram āhur mahābalam
bhavān indraś ca dhātā ca lokānāṃ prabhur avyayaḥ
tvam apratimakarmā ca tathaivānupamadyutiḥ
vidrutānīha sainyāni sahāsmābhiḥ sureśvara
rathacakradhvajākṣāṇi vibhinnāni mahāsuraiḥ
rathahastyaśvayodhāś ca padātāś ca sahasraśaḥ
bhinnāś chinnāś ca śataśo gadāmusalapaṭṭisaiḥ
mahābhair avarūpaṃ hi daityendreṇa kṛtaṃ raṇe
kim upekṣasi daityendrair hanyamānāṃ mahācamūm
trāyasva tridaśaśreṣṭha śaraṇya śaraṇāgatān
śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣāṃ devānām amarādhipaḥ
saṃvartakam iva kruddhaḥ sarvān dahati dānavān
divākarakarākāraṃ kirīṭaṃ dhārayan prabuḥ
vaidūryavarṇasaṃkāśo nānāratnacitāṅgadaḥ
mayūralomā dhūmnākṣaḥ śatabāhuḥ sahasradṛk
harikeśo hariśmaśrur nāgaketur mahābalaḥ
vajrapraharaṇaḥ śrīmān yogī śataśirodharaḥ
sa dhanur baddhasaṃnāhaḥ śatādityasamaprabhaḥ
devagandharvayakṣaughair anuyātaḥ sahasraśaḥ
sāmagaiḥ sujapaiś cāpi stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
śataparva mahāraudraṃ sphoṭanaṃ sarvatomukham
pragṛhya ruciraṃ vajraṃ dīptaṃ raudrāṭṭahāsinam
daityān ayodhayat sarvān mahendraḥ pākaśāsanaḥ
adhṛṣyaḥ sarvabhūtānām adityā dayitaḥ sutaḥ
tataḥ pravṛttaḥ saṃgrāmo balivāsavayos tadā
ubhābhyāṃ devadaityābhyām acirān mahadadbhutaḥ
ativīryabalodagras tumulo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
mahādevastutiśataiḥ karmabhir jayasaṃmitaiḥ
prabodhito daityapatir agnir iddha ivābabhau
surāsurendrayor dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāmaṃ lomaharṣaṇam
devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca bhūyo yuddham abhūt tadā
tato 'vidhyan mahendras taṃ baliṃ śastrair mahābalaḥ
tāny astrāṇi mahābāhuś ciccheda śatadhā raṇe
tataḥ kruddhaḥ punas tatra nijaghne dānavaṃ mahat
āgneyam atha śatrughnaṃ cikṣependro mahābalaḥ
śātayām āsa tac caindraṃ vāruṇāstreṇa dhīmatā
saṃkruddho maghavā vajram agṛhṇāt parvatopamam
hantukāmo balaślāghī baliṃ daityādhipaṃ raṇe
tataḥ śuśrāva devendraḥ kauśiko harivāhanaḥ
aśarīrāṃ śubhāṃ vāṇīṃ tasmin mahati vaiśase
nivartasva mahābāho surāṇāṃ nandivardhana
puraṃdara suraśreṣṭha jeṣyasi baliṃ raṇe
tapasā hy uttamo daityo varadānena cādhikaḥ
svayaṃbhūparitoṣāc ca satyadharmāc ca vāsava
naiṣa śakyas tvayā jetuṃ tridaśair vā sureśvara
yo hy asya jetā bhagavāṃs taṃ śṛṇuṣva samāhitaḥ
brahmaṇaḥ sa hi sarvasvaṃ devānāṃ caiva sā gatiḥ
paraṃ rahasyaṃ dharmasya parasya ca parā gatiḥ
parāt parataraḥ śrīmāṇ parāvaragatiḥ prabhuḥ
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt
śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiḥ pītavāsāḥ surārihā
jetājeyo jayaḥ śrīmān so 'sya jetā bhaviṣyati
śrutvā divyāṃ tu madhurāṃ vāṇīṃ tām aśarīriṇīm
apayāto raṇāc chakraḥ sārdhaṃ sarvair marudgaṇaiḥ
apayāto tu devendre kauśike harivāhane
siṃhanādo mahān āsīd dānavānāṃ mahāmṛdhe
tataḥ kilakilāśabdaḥ kṣveḍitāsphoṭitasvanaḥ
śaṅkhānāṃ ninadaś cātra yodhānāṃ valgitasvanaḥ
vāditrāṇāṃ ca nirghoṣas tumulaś cābhavat tadā
jayaśabdaravaś caiva devānāṃ tu parājaye
sasainyo daityarājas tu stūyamānaḥ suhṛdgaṇaiḥ
balir indro babhau daityo hiraṇyakaśipur yathā
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
niṣprayatneṣu deveṣu trailokye daityapālite
jaye baler balavato mayaśambarayos tathā
śuddhāsu dikṣu sarvāsu pravṛtte dharmakarmaṇi
apāvṛte devapathe ayanasthe divākare
prahrādaśambaramayair anuhrādena caiva hi
dikṣu sarvāsu guptāsu gagane daityapālite
deveṣu makhaśobhāś ca svargārthaṃ darśayatsu ca
prakṛtisthe tadā loke vartamāne ca satpathe
abhāve sarvapāpānāṃ bhāve caiva tathā sthite
bhāve tapasi siddhānāṃ sarvatrāśramarakṣiṣu
catuṣpāde sthite dharme adharme pādavigrahe
prajāpālanayukteṣu bhrājamāneṣu rājasu
svadharmasaṃprayukteṣu sarvāśramanivāsiṣu
abhiṣikto 'suraiḥ sarvair devarājye balis tadā
hṛṣṭeṣv asurasaṃgheṣu nadatsu muditeṣu ca
athābhyupagatā lakṣmīr baliṃ padmāsane sthitā
padmodyatakarā devī varadāsurasevinī
śrīr uvāca
bale balavatāṃ śreṣṭha mahārāja mahādyute
prītāsmi tava bhadraṃ te devatānāṃ parājaye
yat tvayā yudhi vikramya devarājaḥ parājitaḥ
dṛṣṭvā te paramaṃ sattvaṃ tato 'haṃ svayam āgatā
nāścaryaṃ dānavaśreṣtha hiraṇyakaśipoḥ kule
prasūtasyāsurendrasya tava karmedam īdṛśam
viśeṣitas tvayā rājan daityendraḥ sa pitāmahaḥ
yena bhuktaṃ hi nikhilaṃ trailokyam idam avyayam
evam uktvā hi sā devī lakṣmīr daityapatiṃ balim
graviṣṭā varadā saumyā sarvabhūtamanoramā
śiṣṭāś ca divyaḥ pravarā hrīḥ kīrtir dyutir eva ca
prabhā dhṛtiḥ kṣamā bhūtir nītir vidyā dayā matiḥ
smṛtir meghā tathā lajjā lakṣmīr īḍā gatis tathā
śrutiḥ prītis tathā kāntiḥ śāntiḥ puṣṭiḥ kriyā tathā
sarvāś cāpsaraso divyā nṛtyagītaviśāradāḥ
upatasthur mahātmānaṃ baliṃ indraṃ mahāratham
pratipannaṃ tu daiteyais trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
prāptam aiśvaryam amitaṃ balinā brahmavādinā
janamejaya uvāca
parājitāḥ surā daityaiḥ kim akurvata vai mune
kathaṃ ca tridivaṃ labdhaṃ bhūyo devair dvijottama
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
śrutvā vāṇīṃ tu tāṃ divyāṃ saha devaiḥ surādhipaḥ
prāgdiśaṃ prasthitaḥ śrīmān adityālayam uttamam
prāpyādityālayaṃ śakraḥ kathayām āsa tāṃ giram
adityā sā yathā yuddhe tena vāṇī purā śrutā
aditir uvāca
