yady evaṃ putra yuṣmābhir na śakyo hantum āhave
balir virocanasutaḥ sarvaiś caiva marudgaṇaiḥ
sahasraśirasā hantuṃ kevalaṃ śakyate 'suraḥ
tenaikena sahasrākṣa na hy anyena śatakrato
tad vaḥ pṛcchāmi pitaraṃ kaśyapaṃ satyavādinam
parājayārthaṃ daityasya bales tasya mahātmanaḥ
tato 'dityā saha surāḥ saṃprāptāḥ kaśyapāntikam
apaśyan kaśyapaṃ tatra muniṃ dīptataponidhim
ādyaṃ devaguruṃ divyaṃ klinnaṃ triṣavaṇāmbubhiḥ
tejasā bhāskarākāraṃ gauram agniśikhāprabham
nyastadaṇḍaṃ tapoyuktaṃ baddhakṛṣṇājinottaram
valkalājinasaṃvītaṃ pradīptaṃ brahmavarcasā
hutāśam iva dīpyantam ājyamantrapuraskṛtam
svādhyāyanirataṃ nityaṃ vapuṣmantam ivānalam
taṃ brahmavādināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ surāsuraguruṃ prabhum
pratapantam ivādityaṃ mārīcaṃ dīptatejasam
yaḥ sraṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ prajānāṃ patir uttamaḥ
ātmabhāvaviśeṣeṇa tṛtīyo yaḥ prajāpatiḥ
tataḥ praṇamya te vīrāḥ sahādityā surarṣabhāḥ
ūcuḥ prāṅjalayaḥ sarve brahmāṇam iva mānasāḥ
yac chrutaṃ yudhi śakreṇa sarasvatyā samīritam
ajeyas tridaśaiḥ sarvair balir dānavasattamaḥ
śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣāṃ putrāṇāṃ kaśyapas tadā
cakāra gamane buddhiṃ brahmalokāya lokakṛt
kaśyapa uvāca
gacchāma brahmasadanaṃ brahmaghoṣanināditam
yathāśrutaṃ ca tatraiva brahmaṇe vadatānaghāḥ
tato 'dityā saha surā yāntaṃ kaśyapam anvayuḥ
prasthitaṃ brahmasadanaṃ devarṣigaṇasevitam
te muhūrtena saṃprāptā brahmalokaṃ divaukasaḥ
divyaiḥ kāmagamair yānair mahārhaiḥ sumanoharaiḥ
didṛkṣavas te brahmāṇaṃ tapaso rāśim avyayam
abhyagacchanta vistīrṇāṃ brahmaṇaḥ paramāṃ sabhām
ṣaṭpadodgītaninadāṃ sāmagītavimiśritām
śuśruvur madhurāṃ devā brahmaṇaḥ sadane sthitāḥ
ṛco bahvṛcamukhyaiś ca preryamāṇaiḥ padakramaiḥ
śuśruvus te 'maravyāghrā vitateṣu ca karmasu
yajñavedāṅgavidbhiś ca kramaśikṣāviśāradaiḥ
ghoṣeṇa paramarṣīṇāṃ sā babhūva vināditā
yajñasaṃstavavidbhiś ca śikṣāvidbhis tathā dvijaiḥ
śabdanirvacanārthajñair sarvavidyāviśāradaiḥ
vākyair nānārthasaṃyogaiḥ samavāyaviśāradaiḥ
hṛṣṭapuṣṭasvarais tatra dvijendrair valguvādibhiḥ
nāditaṃ brahmasadanaṃ pravaraṃ devasadmavat
te tatra samanuprāpya śṛṇvanto vai dhvaniṃ surāḥ
pūtāny ātmaśarīrāṇi menire te na saṃśayaḥ
tūṣṇībhūtā ekacittā brahmaṇyagatamānasāḥ
vismayotphullanayanā nirīkṣantaḥ parasparam
namaskurvanti ca punar guruṃ lokaguruṃ prabhum
manasaiva suraśreṣṭhāḥ puraskṛtya tu kaśyapam
punaḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ paramaṃ vedoccāraṇanisvanam
gambhīrodāramadhuraṃ susvaraṃ haṃsagadgadam
lokāyatikamukhyaiś ca śuśruvuḥ svanam īritam
tatra tatra ca viprendrān niyatān saṃśitavratān
japahomaparān mukhyān dadṛśuḥ kaśyapātmajāḥ
tasyāṃ sabhāyām āste sma brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
surāsuraguruḥ śrīmān vidhivad devamāyayā
upāsate ca tatrainaṃ prajānāṃ patayaḥ prabhum
dakṣaḥ pracetāḥ pulaho marīciś ca dvijottamaḥ
bhṛgur atrir vasiṣṭhaś ca gautamo nāradas tathā
mano dyaur antarikṣaṃ ca vāyus tejo jalaṃ mahī
śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhas tathaiva ca
prakṛtiś ca vikāraś ca yac cānyat kāraṇaṃ mahat
sāṅgopāṅgāś caturvedāḥ sarahasyapadakramāḥ
kriyāś ca kratavaś caiva saṃkalpaḥ prāṇa eva ca
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ svayaṃbhuvam upasthitāḥ
artho dharmaś ca kāmaś ca dveṣo harṣaś ca nityadā
śuko bṛhaspatiś caiva saṃvarto budha eva ca
śanaiś caraś ca rāhuś ca grahāḥ sarve hy aśeṣataḥ
maruto viśvakarmā ca nakṣatrāṇi ca bhārata
divākaraś ca somaś ca brahmāṇaṃ samupāsate
sāvitrī durgataraṇī vāṇī saptavidhā tathā
sarvāṇi śrutiśāstrāṇi gāthāś ca niyamās tathā
bhāṣyāṇi sarvaśāstrāṇi dehavanti viśāṃ pate
kṣaṇā lavā muhūrtāś ca divā rātriś ca bhārata
ardhamāsāś ca māsāś ca ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ tathaiva ca
saṃvatsarāś caturyugaṃ māsā rātriś caturvidhāḥ
kālacakraṃ ca yad divyaṃ nityam adhruvam avyayam
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ svayaṃbhuvam upasthitāḥ
te praviṣṭāḥ sabhāṃ divyāṃ brahmaṇaḥ sarvakāmadām
kaśyapas tridaśaiḥ sārdhaṃ putrair dharmaviśāradaiḥ
sarvatejomayīṃ divyāṃ brahmarṣigaṇasevitām
brāhmyā śriyā dīpyamānam acintyaṃ vigataklamam
brahmāṇaṃ vīkṣya te sarve āsīnaṃ paramāsane
jagmur mūrdhnā śubhau pādau brahmaṇas te divaukasaḥ
śirobhiḥ spṛśya caraṇau tasya te parameṣṭhinaḥ
vimuktāḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ śāntā vigatakalmaṣāḥ
dṛṣtvā tu tān surān sarvān kaśyapena sahāgatān
āha brahmā mahātejā devānāṃ prabhur īśvaraḥ
brahmovāca
yadartham iha saṃprāptā bhavantaḥ sarva eva hi
vijānāmy aham avyagram enam arthaṃ mahābalāḥ
bhaviṣyati ca vaḥ so 'rthaḥ kāṅkṣito yaḥ surottamāḥ
baler dānavamukhyasya yo vai jetā bhaviṣyati
na khalv asurasaṃghānām eko jetā sa viśvakṛt
trailokyasyāpi jetāsau devānām api cottamaḥ
dhātā caiva hi lokānāṃ viśvayoniḥ sanātanaḥ
pūrvadevaṃ sadā prāhur hemagarbhanidarśanam
ātmā vai yena vibhunā kṛto 'jeyo mahātmanā
baler asuramukhyasya viśvasya jagatas tathā
prabhavaḥ sa hi sarveṣām asmākam api pūrvajaḥ
acintyaḥ sa hi viśvātmā yogayuktaḥ paraṃ tapaḥ
taṃ devāpi mahātmānaṃ na viduḥ ko 'py asāv iti
vedātmānaṃ ca viśvaṃ ca sa devaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
tasyaiva tu prasādena tasya vakṣye parāṃ gatim
yatra yogaṃ samāsthāya tapaś carati duścaram
kṣīrodasyottare kūle udīcyāṃ diśi devatāḥ
amṛtaṃ nāma paramaṃ sthānam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ
bhavantas tatra vai gatvā tapasā saṃśitavratāḥ
amṛtaṃ sthānam āsādya tapaś carata duścaram
tatra śroṣyatha vispaṣṭāṃ snigdhagambhīranisvanām
uṣṇage toyapūrṇasya toyadasya samasvanām
yuktākṣarapadasnigdhāṃ ramyām abhayadāṃ śivām
vāṇīṃ paramasaṃskārāṃ varadāṃ brahmavādinīm
divyāṃ sarasvatīṃ satyāṃ sarvakilbiṣanāśinīm
sarvadevādhidevasya bhāṣitāṃ bhāvitātmanaḥ
tasya vratasamāptyāṃ tu yāvad vratavisarjanāt
amoghāṃ tasya devasya viśve devā mahātmanaḥ
svāgataṃ vaḥ suraśreṣṭhā matsakāśe vyavasthitāḥ
kasya kaṃ vā varaṃ devā dadāmi varadaḥ sthitaḥ
taṃ kaśyapo 'ditiś caiva varaṃ gṛhṇīta vai tataḥ
praṇamya śirasā pādau tasmai yogātmane tadā
bhagavān eva naḥ putro bhavatv iti na saṃśayaḥ
uktaś ca parayā bhaktyā tathāstv iti sa vakṣyati
devā bruvantu te sarve bhrātā nas tvaṃ bhaveti ca
tathāstv iti ca sa śrīmān vakṣyate sarvalokakṛt
tasmād evaṃ gṛhītvā tu varaṃ tridaśasattamāḥ
kṛtakṛtyāḥ punaḥ sarve gacchadhvaṃ svaṃ svam ālayam
tathāstv iti surāḥ sarve kaśyapo 'ditir eva ca
vanditvā brahmacaraṇau gatāḥ saumyāṃ diśaṃ prati
te 'cireṇaiva saṃprāptāḥ kṣīrodasyottaraṃ taṭam
yathoddiṣṭhaṃ bhagavatā brahmaṇā brahmavādinā
te 'tītya sāgarān sarvān parvatāṃś ca bahūn kṣaṇāt
nadīś ca vividhā divyāḥ pṛthivyāṃ surasattamāḥ
paśyanti ca sughorāṃ vai sarvasattvavivarjitām
abhāskarām amaryādāṃ tamasā saṃvṛtāṃ diśam
amṛtaṃ sthānam āsādya kaśyapena surāḥ saha
dīkṣitāḥ kāmadaṃ divyaṃ vrataṃ varṣasahasrakam
prasādārthaṃ sureśāya tasmai yogāya dhīmate
nārāyaṇāya devāya sahasrākṣāya bhūtaye
brahmacaryeṇa maunena sthānavīrāsanena ca
damena ca sūrāḥ sarve tapo duścaram āsthitāḥ
kaśyapas tatra bhagavān prasādārthaṃ mahātmanaḥ
udīrayati vedoktaṃ yam āhuḥ paramaṃ stavam
kaśyapa uvāca
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
nārāyaṇas tu bhagavāñ śrutvemaṃ paramaṃ stavam
brahmajñena dvijendreṇa kaśyapena samīritam
snigdhagambhīranirghoṣaṃ jīmūtasvananisvanam
manasā prītiyuktena vibudhānāṃ mahātmanām
uvāca vacanaṃ samyag hṛṣṭapuṣṭapadākṣaram
ākāśāc chuśruvur devā darśanaṃ nopalabhyate
śrīmān prītamanā devaḥ provāca prabur īśvaraḥ
prīto 'smi vaḥ suraśreṣṭhāḥ sarve matto viniścayan
varaṃ vṛṇuta bhadraṃ vo varado 'smi surottamāḥ
kaśyapa uvāca
yadaiva bhagavān prītaḥ sarveṣām amarottama
tadaiva kṛtakṛtyāḥ sma tvaṃ hi naḥ paramā gatiḥ
yadi prasanno bhagavān dātavyo vā paro yadi
vāsavasyānujo bhrātā jñātīnāṃ nandivardhanaḥ
adityāṃ vai mama śrīmān bhagavān astu vai sutaḥ
iśaṃpāyana uvāca
aditir devamātā ca etam evārtham uttamam
putrārthe varadaṃ prāha bhagavantaṃ varārthinī
yācate putrakāmā vai bhavān putro bhavatv iti
niḥśreyasārthaṃ sarveṣāṃ devānāṃ hi mahātmanām
bhrātā bhartā ca dhātā ca śaraṇaṃ ca bhavasva naḥ
adityāḥ putratāṃ yāte tvayi devāḥ savāsavāḥ
devaśabdaṃ vahiṣyanti kaśyapasyātmajo bhava
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tatas tān abravīd viṣṇur devān kaśyapam eva ca
sarveṣām eva yuṣmākaṃ ye bhaviṣyanti śatravaḥ
muhūrtam api te sarve na sthāsyanti mamāgrataḥ
hatvāsuragaṇān sarvān ye cānye devaśatravaḥ
kariṣye devatāḥ sarvā yajñabhāgāgrabhojinaḥ
havyādāṃś ca surān sarvān kavyādāṃś ca pitṝn api
kariṣye vibudhaśreṣṭhāḥ pārameṣṭhyena karmaṇā
yathāgatena mārgeṇa nivartadhvaṃ surottamāḥ
devamātus tathādityāḥ kaśyapasyāmitātmanaḥ
yathāmanīṣitaṃ kartā gacchadhvaṃ tvaṃ svam ālayam
evam ukte tu vacane viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
devāḥ prahṛṣṭamanasaḥ pūjayanti sma sarvaśaḥ
viśve devā mahātmānaḥ kaśyapo 'ditir eva ca
namaskṛtya sureśāya tasmai devāya raṃhase
prayātāḥ prāgdiśaṃ divyaṃ vipulaṃ kaśyapāśramam
gatvā tam āśramaṃ tatra brahmarṣigaṇasevitam
ceruḥ svādhyāyaniratā adityā garbham īpsavaḥ
aditir devamātā ca garbhaṃ dadhre 'titejasam
bhūtātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ divyaṃ varṣasahasrikam
pūrṇe varṣasahasre tu prasūtā garbham uttamam
surāṇāṃ śaraṇaṃ devam asurāṇāṃ vināśanam
garbhasthena tu devena paritrātāḥ surās tadā
ādadānena tejāṃsi trailokyasya mahātmanā
tasmiñ jāte tu deveśe trailokyasya sukhāvahe
bhayade daityasaṃghānāṃ surāṇāṃ nandivardhane
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sapta sapta caiva maharṣayaḥ
tasya devasya jātasya namaskāraṃ pracakrire
bharadvājaḥ kaśyapo gautamaś ca
viśvāmitro jamadagnir vasiṣṭhaḥ
yaś codito bhāskaro vipranaṣṭe
so 'py atrātrir bhagavān ājagāma
marīcir aṅgirāś caiva pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
dakṣaḥ prajāpatiś caiva namaskāraṃ pracakrire
aurvo vasiṣṭhaputraś ca stambaḥ kaśyapa eva ca
kapīvān akapīvāṃś ca datto niścyavanas tathā
vasiṣṭhaputrāḥ saptāsan vāsiṣṭhā iti viśrutāḥ
hiraṇyagarbhasya sutāḥ aurvāj jātāḥ sutejasaḥ
gārgyaḥ pṛthus tathaivāgryo yāmyo vāmana eva ca
devabāhur yadudhraś ca parjanyaś caiva somajaḥ
hiraṇyaromā vedaśirāḥ satyanetras tathaiva ca
viśvo 'tiviśvaś cyavanaḥ sudhāmā virajās tathā
atināmā sahiṣṇuś ca namaskāram akurvata
vidyotamānā vapuṣā sarvābharaṇabhūśitāḥ
upanṛtyanti deveśaṃ viṣṇum apsarasāṃ varāḥ
tato gandharvatūryeṣu praṇadatsu vihāyasi
bahubhiḥ saha gandharvaiḥ prāgāyata ca tumburuḥ
mahāśrutiś citraśirā ūrṇāyur anaghas tathā
gomāyuḥ sūryavarcāś ca somavarcāś ca saptamaḥ
yugapas tṛṇapaḥ kārṣṇir nandiś citrarathas tathā
trayodaśaḥ śāliśirāḥ parjanyaś ca caturdaśa
kaliḥ pañcadaśaś cātra nāradaś caiva ṣoḍaśaḥ
ṣaṭpañcāśad ime proktās tatraiva tu mahīpate
hāhā hūhūś ca gandharvau haṃsaś caiva mahādyutiḥ
sarve te devagandharvā upagāyanti keśavam
tathaivāpsaraso hṛṣṭāḥ sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitāḥ
vapuṣmantyaḥ sujaghanāḥ sarvāṅgaśubhadarśanāḥ
nanṛtuś ca mahābhāgā jaguś cāyatalocanāḥ
sumadhyāś cārumadhyāś ca priyamukhyo varānanāḥ
anūkā ca tathā jāmī miśrakeśī alaṃbusā
marīciḥ śucikā caiva vidyutparṇā tilottamā
adrikā lakṣmaṇā caiva rambhā tadvanmanoramā
asitā ca subāhuś ca supriyā subhagā tathā
urvaśī citralekhā ca sugrīvā ca sulocanā
puṇḍarīkā sugandhā ca surathā ca pramāthinī
nandā sārasvatī caiva tathānyās tatra saṃghaśaḥ
menakā sahajanyā ca parṇikā puñjikasthalā
etāś cāpsaraso 'nyāś ca pranṛtyanti sahasraśaḥ
dhātāryamā ca mitraś ca varuṇo 'ṃśo bhagas tathā
indro vivasvān pūṣā ca tvaṣṭā ca savitā tathā
kathito viṣṇur ity evaṃ kāśyapeyo gaṇas tathā
ity ete dvādaśādityā jvalantaḥ sūryavarcasaḥ
cakrus tasya sureśasya namaskāraṃ mahātmanaḥ
mṛgavyādhaś ca sarpaś ca nirṛtiś ca mahāyaśāḥ
ajaikapād ahirbudhnyaḥ pinākī cāparājitaḥ
dahano 'atheśvaraś caiva kapālī ca viśāṃ pate
sthāṇur bhagaś ca bhagavān rudras tatrāvatasthire
aśvinau vasavaś cāṣṭau marutaś ca mahābalāḥ
viśvedevāś ca sādhyāś ca tasya prāñjalayaḥ sthitāḥ
śeṣānujā mahābhāgā vāsukipramukhās tathā
kacchapaś cāpahantā ca takṣakaś ca mahābalaḥ
adhṛṣyās tejasā yuktā mahākrodhā mahābalāḥ
ete nāgā mahātmānas tasmai prāñjalayaḥ sthitāḥ
tārkṣyaś cāriṣṭanemiś ca garuḍaś ca mahābalaḥ
aruṇaś cāruṇiś caiva vainateyā hy upasthitāḥ
pitāmahaś ca bhagavān svayam āgamya lokakṛt
prāha devaguruḥ śrīmān saha sarvair mahātmabhiḥ
yasmāt prasūyate lokaḥ prabhaviṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥ
tasmāl lokeśvaraḥ śrīmān viṣṇur eva bhavatv ayam
evam uktvā tu bhagavān sārdhaṃ devarṣibhiḥ prabhuḥ
namas kṛtvā sureśāya jagāma tridivaṃ punaḥ
sa tu jātaḥ sureśānaḥ kaśyapasyātmajaḥ prabhuḥ
navadurdinameghābho raktākṣo vāmanākṛtiḥ
śrīvatsenorasi śrīmāṃl lomajātena rājatā
utphullalocanāḥ sarvāḥ paśyanty apsarasas tadā
divi sūryasahasrasya bhaved yugapatthitā
yadi bhāḥ sadṛśī sā syād bhāsas tasya mahātmanaḥ
surarṣipratimaḥ śrīmān bhūr bhuvo bhūtabhāvanaḥ
śucilomā mahāskandhaḥ sarvatejomayaḥ prabhuḥ
yo gatiḥ puṇyakīrtīnām agatiḥ pāpakarmiṇām
yogasiddhaṃ mahātmānaṃ yaṃ vidur yogam uttamam
yasyāṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryaṃ yam āhur devasattamam
yaṃ prāpya śāśvataṃ viprā niyatā mokṣakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
janmato maraṇāc caiva mucyante bhavabhīravaḥ
yad etat tapa ity āhuḥ sarvāśrayanivāsinaḥ
sevante yaṃ yatāhārā duścaraṃ vratam āsthitāḥ
yo 'nanta iti nāgeṣu sevyate sarvabhogibhiḥ
sahasramūrdhā raktākṣaḥ śeṣādibhir anuttamaiḥ
yo yajña iti viprendrair ijyate svargalipsubhiḥ
nānāsthānagataḥ śrīmān ekaḥ kavir anuttamaḥ
yaṃ vedā gānti vettāraṃ yajñabhāgapradāyinam
vṛṣārciś candrasūryākṣaṃ devam ākāśavigraham
sa prāha tridaśān sarvān vācā vai parayā vibhuḥ
jānann api mahātejā gato yogena bālatām
kiṃ karomi suraśreṣṭhāḥ kaṃ varaṃ ca dadāmi vaḥ
yat kāṅkṣitaṃ vaḥ sarveṣāṃ tad vai brūta mudā yutāḥ
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā vāmanasya mahātmanaḥ
sarve te hṛṣṭamanaso devāḥ kaśyapanandanāḥ
ūcuḥ prāñjalayo viṣṇuṃ surāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ
brahmaṇo varadānena hṛtaṃ no nikhilaṃ jagat
tapasā mahatā caiva vikrameṇa damena ca
balinā daityamukhyena sarvajñena mahātmanā
avadhyaḥ kila sarveśāṃ so 'smākaṃ devasattama
bhavān prabhavate tasya nānyaḥ kaścana suvrata
tat prapadyāmahe sarvaṃ bhavantaṃ śaraṇārthinaḥ
śaraṇyaṃ varadaṃ devaṃ sarvadevabhayāpaham
ṛṣīṇāṃ ca hitārthāya lokānāṃ ca sureśvara
priyārthaṃ ca tathādityāḥ kaśyapasya tathaiva ca
kavyaṃ pitṝṇām ucitaṃ surāṇāṃ havyam uttamam
pravartatāṃ mahābāho yathāpūrvaṃ surottama
ānṛṇyārthaṃ sureśasya vāsavasya mahātmanaḥ
pratyānaya mahendrasya trailokyam idam avyayam
kratunā vājimeghena yajate sa hi dānavaḥ
yat pratyānayane yuktaṃ lokānāṃ tad vicintaya
evam uktas tadā devair viṣṇur vāmanarūpadhṛk
praharṣayann uvācātha sarvān devān idaṃ vacaḥ
tasya yajñasakāśaṃ māṃ maharṣir vedapāragaḥ
bṛhaspatir bṛhattejā nayatām aṅgiraḥsutaḥ
tasyāhaṃ samanuprāpto yajñavāṭaṃ surottamāḥ
vicariṣye yathāyuktaṃ trailokyaharaṇāya vai
tato bṛhaspatiḥ śrīmān anayad vāmanaṃ prabhum
yajñavāṭaṃ mahātejā dānavendrasya dhīmataḥ
mauñjī yajñopavītī ca chatrī daṇḍī dhvajī tathā
vāmano dhūmraraktākṣo bhagavān bālarūpadhṛk
taṃ gatvā yajñavāṭaṃ tu brahmarṣigaṇasevitam
ātmānam eva bhagavān varṇayām āsa taṃ kratum
aho yajño 'sureśasya bahubhakṣaḥ susaṃskṛtaḥ
pitāmahasyeva purā yajataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
sureśvarasya śakrasya yamasya varuṇasya ca
viśeṣitās tvayā yajñā dānavendra mahābala
yajatā vājimeghena kratūnāṃ pravareṇa ha
sarvapāpavināśāya svargamārgapradarśinā
sarvakāmamayo hy eṣa saṃmato brahmavādinām
kratūnāṃ pravaraḥ śrīmān aśvamedha iti smṛtaḥ
suvarṇaśṛṅgo hi mahānubhāvo
lokeśvaro vāyumayo mahātmā
svargekṣaṇaḥ kāñcanagarbhagauraḥ
sa viśvayoniḥ paramo hi medhyaḥ
āsthāya vai vājinam āśvamedhikam
iṣṭvā narā duṣkṛtam uttaranti
yam āhur vai vedavido dvijendrā
vaiśvānaraṃ vājinam āśvamedhikam
yathāśramāṇāṃ pravaro gṛhāśramo
yathā nṛṇāṃ pravarā brāhmaṇāś ca
yathāsurāṇāṃ pravaro bhavān iha
tathā kratūnāṃ pravaro 'śvamedhaḥ
etac chrutvā tu daityendro vāmanena samīritam
mudā paramayā yuktaḥ prāha daityapatir baliḥ
kasyāsi brāhmaṇaśreṣṭha kim icchasi dadāmi te
varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yatheṣṭaṃ kāmam āpnuhi
vāmana uvāca
na rājyaṃ na ca yānāni na ratnāni na ca striyaḥ
kāmaye yadi tuṣṭo 'si dharme ca yadi te matiḥ
gurvarthaṃ me grayacchasva padāni trīṇi dānava
tvam agniśaraṇārthāya eṣa me paramo varaḥ
balir uvāca
tribhiḥ kiṃ tava viprendra padaiḥ pravadatāṃ vara
śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ padānāṃ mārgatāṃ bhavān
śukra uvāca
mā dadasva mahābāho na taṃ vetsi mahāsura
eṣa māyāpraticchanno bhagavān pravaro hariḥ
vāmanaṃ rūpam āsthāya śakrapriyahitepsayā
tvāṃ vañcayitum āyāto baṭurūpadharo vibhuḥ
evam uktaḥ sa śukreṇa ciraṃ saṃcintya vai baliḥ
praharṣeṇa samāyuktaḥ kiṃ ataḥ pātram iṣyate
gṛhya haste tv asaṃbhrānto bhṛṅgāraṃ kanakāmayam
balir uvāca
viprendra prāṅmukhas tiṣṭha sthito 'si kamalekṣaṇa
pratīccha dehi kiṃ bhūmiṃ kiṃmātrā bhoḥ padatrayam
dattaṃ vaḥ pātaya jalaṃ naiva mithyā bhaved guruḥ
śukra uvāca
bho na deyaṃ kuto daitya vijñāto 'yaṃ yathā dhruvam
ko 'yaṃ viṣṇur aho prītir vañcitas tvaṃ na vañcitaḥ
balir uvāca
kathaṃ sa nātho 'yaṃ viṣṇur yajñe svayam upasthitaḥ
dāsyāmi devadevāya yad yad icchaty ayaṃ prabhuḥ
ko vānyaḥ pātrabhūto 'smād viṣṇoḥ parataraṃ bhavet
evam uktvā baliḥ śīghraṃ pātayām āsa vai jalam
vāmana uvāca
padāni trīṇi daityendra paryāptāni mamānagha
yan mayā pūrvam uktaṃ hi tat tathā na tad anyathā

prahrāda uvāca

vāmana uvāca
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
tathāstv iti baliḥ procya sparśayām āsa dānavaḥ
padāni trīṇi devāya viṣṇave 'mitatejase
toye tu patite haste vāmano 'bhūd avāmanaḥ
sarvadevamayaṃ rūpaṃ darśayām āsa vai prabhuḥ
bhūḥ pādau dyauḥ śiraś cāsya candrādityau ca cakṣuṣī
pādāṅgulyaḥ piśācāś ca hastāṅgulyaś ca guhyakāḥ
viśvedevāś ca jānusthā jaṅghe sādhyāḥ surottamāḥ
yakṣā nakheṣu saṃbhūtā lekhāś cāpsarasas tathā
dṛṣṭir dhiṣṇyāni vipulāḥ keśāḥ sūryāṃśavas tathā
tārakā lomakūpāni lomāni ca maharṣayaḥ
bāhavo vidiśaś cāsya diśaḥ śrotraṃ tathaiva ca
aśvinau śravaṇau cāsya nāsā vāyur mahābalaḥ
prasādaś candramāś caiva mano dharmas tathaiva ca
satyam asyābhavad vāṇī jihvā devī sarasvatī
grīvāditir mahādevī tāluḥ sūryaś ca dīptamān
dvāraṃ svargasya nābhir vai mitras tvaṣṭā ca vai bhruvau
mukhaṃ vaiśvānaraś cāsya vṛṣaṇau tu prajāpatiḥ
hṛdayaṃ bhagavān brahmā puṃstvaṃ vai kaśyapo muniḥ
pṛṣṭhe 'sya vasavo devā marutaḥ sarvasaṃdhiṣu
sarvacchandāṃsi daśanā jyotīṃṣi vimalāḥ prabhāḥ
uro rudro mahādevo dhairyaṃ cāsya mahārṇavaḥ
udaraṃ cāsya gandharvā bhujagāś ca mahābalāḥ
lakṣmīr medhā dhṛtiḥ kāntiḥ sarvavidyāś ca vai kaṭiḥ
lalāṭam asya paramaṃ svasthānaṃ paramātmanaḥ
sarvajyotīṃṣi yānīha tapaḥ śakras tu devarāṭ
tasya devādhidevasya tejaś cāsīn mahātmanaḥ
stanau kakṣau ca vedāś ca oṣṭhau cāsya makhāḥ sthitāḥ
iṣṭayaḥ paśubandhāś ca dvijānāṃ ceṣṭitāni ca
tasya devamayaṃ rūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣṇor mahāsurāḥ
abhisarpanti saṃkruddhāḥ pataṃgā iva pāvakam
śṛṇu nāmāni sarveṣāṃ rūpāṇy abhijanāni ca
vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
āyudhāni ca mukhyāni dānavānāṃ mahātmanām
vipracittiḥ śibiḥ śaṅkur ayaḥśaṅkus tathaiva ca
ayaḥśirā aśvaśirā hayagrīvaś ca vīryavān
vegavān ketumān ugraḥ sogravyagro mahāsuraḥ
puṣkaraḥ puṣkalaś caiva sāśvo 'śvapatir eva ca
prahrādo 'śvaśirāḥ kumbhaḥ saṃhrādo gaganapriyaḥ
anuhrādo hariharau varāhaḥ saṃharo 'rujaḥ
vṛṣaparvā virūpākṣo aticandraḥ sulocanaḥ
niṣprabhaḥ suprabhaḥ śrīmāṃs tathaiva ca nirūdaraḥ
ekacakro mahācakro dvicakraḥ kālasaṃnibhaḥ
śarabhaḥ śalabhaś caiva kuṇapaḥ kulapaḥ krathaḥ
bṛhatkīrtir mahāgarbhaḥ śaṅkukarṇo mahādhvaniḥ
dīrghajihvo 'rkavadano mṛdubāhur mṛdupriyaḥ
vāyur gaviṣṭho namuciḥ śambaro vikṣaro mahān
candrahantā krodhahantā krodhavardhana eva ca
kālakaḥ kālakākṣaś ca vṛtraḥ krodho vimokṣaṇaḥ
gaviṣṭhaś ca haviṣṭhaś ca pralambo narakaḥ pṛthuḥ
candratāpanavātāpī ketumān baladarpitaḥ
asilomā pulomā ca bāṣkalaḥ pramado madaḥ
śṛgālavadanaś caiva karālaḥ keśir eva ca
ekākṣaś ca varāhaś ca tuhuṇḍaḥ sṛmalaḥ sṛpaḥ
ete cānye ca bahavaḥ kramamāṇaṃ trivikramam
upatasthur mahātmānaṃ viṣṇuṃ daityagaṇās tadā
pāśodyatakarāḥ ke 'pi vyāditāsyāḥ kharasvanāḥ
śataghnīcakrahastāś ca vajrahastās tathāpare
khaḍgapaṭṭiśahastāś ca paraśvadhadharāḥ pare
prāsamudgarahastāś ca tathā parighapāṇayaḥ
mahāśanivyagrakarā śūlahastā mahābalāḥ
mahāvṛkṣodyatakarās tathaiva ca dhanurdharāḥ
gadābhuśuṇḍihastāś ca vajrahastās tathāpare
asikampanahastāś ca dānavā yuddhadurmadāḥ
nānāpraharaṇā ghorā nānāveṣā mahābalāḥ
kūrmakukkuṭavaktrāś ca hastivaktrās tathāpare
kharoṣṭravadanāś caiva varāhavadanās tathā
bhīmā makaravaktrāś ca śiśumāramukhās tathā
mārjāraśukavaktrāś ca dīrghavaktrāś ca dānavaḥ
guruḍānanāḥ khaḍgamukhā mayūravadanās tathā
aśvavaktrā babhruvaktrā ghorā mṛgamukhās tathā
uṣṭraśalyakavaktrāś ca krauñcavaktrāś dānavāḥ
nakulaśyenavaktrāś ca pārāvatamukhāstathā
cakravākamukhāś caiva godhāvaktrās tathāpare
tathā mṛgānanāḥ śūrā gojāvimahiṣānanāḥ
kṛkalāsamukhāś caiva vyāghravaktrās tathāpare
ṛkṣaśārdūlavaktrāś ca siṃhavaktrās tathāpare
gajendracarmavasanās tathā kṛṣṇājināmbarāḥ
cīrasaṃvṛtagātrāś ca tathā phalakavāsasaḥ
uṣṇīṣiṇo mukuṭinas tathā kuṇḍalino 'surāḥ
kirīṭino lambaśikhāḥ kambugrīvāḥ suvarcasaḥ
nānāveṣadharā daityā nānāmālyānulepanāḥ
svāny āyudhāni dīptāni pragṛhyāsurasattamāḥ
kramamāṇaṃ hṛṣīkeśam upatiṣṭhanti dānavāḥ
pramathya sarvān daiteyān pādahastatalaiḥ prabhuḥ
rūpaṃ kṛtvā mahākāyaṃ jahārāśu sa medinīm
tasya vikramato bhūmiṃ candrādityau stanāntare
nabhaḥ prakramamāṇasya sakthideśe vyavasthitau
paraṃ vikramamāṇasya jānudeśe vyavasthitau
viṣṇor amitavīryasya vadanty evaṃ dvijātayaḥ
jitvā lokatrayaṃ kṛtsnaṃ hatvā cāsurapuṃgavān
dadau śakrāya vasudhāṃ harir lokanamaskṛtaḥ
sutalaṃ nāma pātālam aghastād vasudhātale
baler dattaṃ bhagavatā viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
tad avāpyāsuraśreṣṭhaś cakāra matim uttamām
rasātalatale vāsam akarod asurādhipaḥ
tatrasthaś ca mahātejā dhyānaṃ paramam āsthitaḥ
uvāca vacanaṃ dhīmān viṣṇuṃ lokanamaskṛtam
kiṃ mayā deva kartavyaṃ brūhi sarvam aśeṣataḥ
viṣṇur uvāca
dadāmi te mahābhāga parituṣṭo 'smi te 'sura
varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yatheṣṭaṃ kāmam āpnuhi
mā ca śakrasya vacanaṃ pratihāsīḥ kathaṃcana
aham ājñāpayāmi tvāṃ śreyaś caivam avāpsyasi
atha daityādhipaṃ prāha viṣṇur devādhipānujaḥ
vācā paramayā devo vareṇyaḥ prabhur īśvaraḥ
yat tvayā salilaṃ dattaṃ gṛhītaṃ pāṇinā mayā
tasmāt te daitya devebhyo nāsti jātu bhayaṃ kvacit
sutalaṃ nāma pātālaṃ tatra tvaṃ sānugo vasa
sarvadaitygaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ matprasādān mahāsura
na ca te devadevasya śakrasyāmitatejasaḥ
śāsanaṃ pratihantavyaṃ smaratā śāsanaṃ mama
devatāś cāpi te sarvāḥ pūjyā eva mahāsura
prāpsyase ca mahābhāga divyān kāmān yathepsitān
iha cāmutra cākṣayyān vividhāṃś ca paricchadān
daityādhipatyaṃ ca sadā matprasādād avāpsyasi
bhogāṃś ca vividhān samyag yajñāṃś ca sahadakṣiṇān
yadā caitāṃ mayā proktāṃ maryādāṃ cālayiṣyasi
bandhiṣyanti tadā hi tvāṃ nāgapāśā mahābalāḥ
namaskāryāś ca te nityaṃ mahendrādyā divaukasaḥ
mama jyeṣṭhaḥ suraśreṣṭhaḥ śāsanaṃ pratigṛhyatām
balir uvāca
devadeva mahābhāga śaṅkhacakragadādhara
surāsuraguruśreṣṭha sarvalokamaheśvara
tatrāsato me pātāle bhāgaṃ brūhi surottama
mamānnam aśanaṃ deva prāśanārtham ariṃdama
tad vadasva suraśreṣṭha tṛptir yena mamākṣayā
bhagavān uvāca
aśrotriyaṃ śrāddam adhītam avratam
adakṣiṇaṃ yajñam anṛtvijā hutam
aśraddhayā dattam asaṃskṛtaṃ havir
ete pradattās tava daitya bhāgāḥ
puṇyaṃ maddveṣiṇāṃ yac ca madbhaktadveṣiṇāṃ tathā
krayavikrayasaktānāṃ puṇyaṃ yac cāgnihotriṇām
aśraddhayā ca yad dānaṃ dadatām yajatāṃ yathā
tat sarvaṃ tava daityendra matprasādād bhaviṣyati
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
etac chrutvā tu vacanaṃ balir viṣṇor mahātmanaḥ
evam astv iti taṃ proktvā pātālam asuro gataḥ
praviveśa mahābhāgo devājñāṃ pratipālayan
bhagavān api rājyānāṃ pravibhāgaṃ cakāra ha
dadau pūrvāṃ diśaṃ caindrīṃ śakrāyāmitatejase
yāmyāṃ yamāya devāya pitṛrājñe mahātmane
paścimām tu diśaṃ prādād varuṇāya mahātmane
uttarāṃ ca kuberāya yakṣādhipataye diśam
aghastān nāgarājāya somāyordhvāṃ diśaṃ dadau
evaṃ vibhajya trailokyaṃ viṣṇur balavatāṃ varaḥ
jagāma tridivaṃ devaḥ pūjyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
vāmanaḥ sarvabhūteṣu pratiṣṭāpyaiva vāsavam
tasmin prayāte durdharṣe vāmane 'mitatejasi
sarve mumudire devāḥ puraskṛtya śatakratum
gate tu tridivaṃ kṛṣṇe badhvā vairocaniṃ balim
nāgaiḥ saptaśirobhiś ca kambalāśvatarādibhiḥ
nāgabandhanaduḥkhārtaṃ baliṃ vairocaniṃ tataḥ
papracchayāsau devarṣir nāradaḥ pratyapadyata
sa taṃ kṛcchragataṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛpayābhipariplutaḥ
uvāca dānavaśreṣṭhaṃ mokṣopāyaṃ dadāmi te
stavaṃ devādhidevasya vāsudevasya dhīmataḥ
anādinidhanasyāsya akṣayasyāvyayasya ca
tam adhīṣvātha daityendra viśuddhenāntarātmanā
tadgatas tanmanā bhūtvā drutaṃ mokṣam avāpsyasi
tato virocanasutaḥ prāñjaliḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ
mokṣaviṃśakam avyagro nāradāt samadhītavān
tam adhītya stavaṃ divyaṃ nāradena samīritam
pṛthivī coddhṛtā yena taṃ jajāpa mahāsuraḥ
auṃ namo 'stv anantapataye akṣayāya mahātmane
jaleśayāya devāya padmanābhāya viṣṇave
saptasūryavapuḥ kṛtvā trīṃl lokān krāntavān asi
bhagavan kālakālas tvaṃ tena satyena mokṣaya
naṣṭacandrārkagagane kṣīṇayajñatapaḥkriye
punaś cintayase lokāṃs tena satyena mokṣaya
brahmarudrendravāyvagnisaridbhujagaparvatāḥ
tvatsthā dṛṣṭā dvijendreṇa tena satyena mokṣaya
mārkaṇḍena purākalpe praviśya jaṭharaṃ tava
carācaragataṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tena satyena mokṣaya
eko vidyāsahāyas tvaṃ yogī yogam upāgataḥ
punas trailokyam utsṛjya tena satyena mokṣaya
jagmaśayyām upāsīno yoganidrām upāgataḥ
lokāṃś cintayase bhūyas tena satyena mokṣaya
vārāhaṃ rūpam āsthāya vedayajñapuraskṛtam
dharā jaloddhṛtā yena tena satyena mokṣaya
uddhṛtya daṃṣṭrayā yajñāṃs tripiṇḍān kṛtavān asi
tvaṃ pitṝṇām api hare tena satyena mokṣaya
pradudruvuḥ surāḥ sarve hiraṇyākṣabhayārditāḥ
paritrātās tvayā deva tena satyena mokṣaya
dīrghavaktreṇa rūpeṇa hiraṇyākṣasya saṃyuge
śiro jahāra cakreṇa tena satyena mokṣaya
bhagnamūrdhāsthimastiṣko hiraṇyakaśipuḥ purā
huṃkāreṇa hato daityas tena satyena mokṣaya
dānavābhyāṃ hṛtā vedā brahmaṇaḥ paśyataḥ purā
paritrātās tvayā deva tena satyena mokṣaya
kṛtvā hayaśirorūpam hatvā tu madhukaiṭabhau
brahmaṇe te 'rpitā vedās tena satyena mokṣaya
devadānavagandharvā yakṣasiddhamahoragāḥ
antaṃ tava na paśyanti tena satyena mokṣaya
apāntaratamā nāma jāto devasya vai sutaḥ
kṛtāś ca tena vedārthās tena satyena mokṣaya
vedayajñāgnihotrāṇi pitṛyajñahavīṃṣi ca
rahasyaṃ tava devasya tena satyena mokṣaya
ṛṣir dhīrghatamā nāma jātyandho guruśāpataḥ
tvatprasādāc ca cakṣuṣmāṃs tena satyena mokṣaya
grāhagrastaṃ gajendraṃ ca dīnaṃ mṛtyuvaśaṃ gatam
bhaktaṃ mokṣitavāṃs tvaṃ hi tena satyena mokṣaya
akṣayaś cāvyayaś ca tvaṃ brahmaṇyo bhaktavatsalaḥ
ucchritānāṃ niyantāsi tena satyena mokṣaya
śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ gadāṃ padmaṃ śārṅgaṃ garuḍam eva ca
prasādayāmi śirasā te bandhān mokṣayantu mām
śaṅkhacakragadātūṇaśārṅgaṃ ca garuḍādayaḥ
hariṃ prasādayām āsur baliṃ mokṣaya bandhanāt
tataḥ prasanno bhagavān ādideśa khageśvaram
garuḍaṃ nāgahantāraṃ baliṃ mokṣaya bandhanāt
tato vikṣipya garuḍaḥ pakṣāvatulavikramaḥ
jagāma vasudhāmūlaṃ yatrāste saṃyato baliḥ
āgamaṃ tasya vijñāya nāgā muktvā mahāsuram
yayuḥ purīṃ bhogavatīṃ vainateyabhayārditāḥ
muktaṃ kṛṣṇaprasādena cintayānam adhomukham
bhraṣṭaśriyam uvācedaṃ garutmān apapannagam
dānavendra mahābāho viṣṇus tvām abravīt prabhuḥ
mukto nivasa pātāle saputrajanabāndhavaḥ
itasvayā na gantavyaṃ gavyūtim api dānava
samayaṃ yadi bhindyās tvaṃ mūrdhā te śatadhā vrajet
pakṣīndravacanaṃ śrutvā dānavendro 'bravīd idam
sthito 'smi samaye tasya anantasya mahātmanaḥ
jīvyopāyaṃ tu bhagavān mama kiṃcit karotu saḥ
ihastho 'ham sukhāsīno yenāpyāye khageśvara
bales tu vacanaṃ śrutvā garutmān idam abravit
pūrvam eva kṛtas tena jīvyopāyo mahātmanā
pravartiṣyanti ye yajñā vidhihīnā hy anṛtvijaḥ
prāyaścittam ajānanto yajñabhāgas tatas tava
na teṣāṃ yajñabhāgaṃ vai pratigṛhṇanti devatāḥ
anenāpyāyitabalaḥ sukham atra nivatsyasi
saṃdeśam etaṃ bhagavān dattavān kaśyapātmajaḥ
dānavendra mahābāho viṣṇus trailokyabhāvanaḥ
imaṃ stavam anantasya sarvapāpapramocanam
yaḥ paṭheta naro bhaktyā tasya naśyati kilbiṣam
gohatyāyāḥ pramucyeta brahmaghno brahmahatyayā
aputro labhate putraṃ kanyā caivepsitaṃ patim
lagnagarbhāt pramucyeta garbhiṇī janayet sutam
ye ca mokṣaiṣiṇo loke yoginaḥ sāṃkhyakāpilāḥ
stavenānena gacchanti śvetadvīpam akalmaṣāḥ
sarvakāmaprado hy eṣa stavo 'nantasya kīrtyate
yaḥ paṭhet prātar utthāya śuciḥ prayatamānasaḥ
sarvakāmam avāpnoti mānavo nātra saṃśayaḥ
eṣa vai vāmano nāma prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ
vedavidbhir dvijair eva paṭhyate vaiṣṇavaṃ yaśaḥ
yas tv imaṃ vāmanaṃ divyaṃ prādurbhāvaṃ mahātmanaḥ
śṛṇuyān niyato bhaktyā sadā parvasu parvasu
parān vijayate rājā yathā viṣṇur mahābalaḥ
yaśo vipulam āpnoti vipulaṃ cāpnute vasu
priyo bhavati bhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ vāmano yathā
putrapautrāś ca vardhante ārogyaguṇasaṃpadā
prīyate paṭhataś cāsya devadevo janārdanaḥ
sarvakāmayutaś caiva kṛṣṇadvaipāyano 'bravīt
